47b1(phal chen): chu klung gi lha dga' bde kun nas 'byung ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad kyi 'byung pa sel cing gtong ba phun sum tshogs pa yongs su spyod pa zhes bya'o/ /chu klung gi lha yon tan gyi shugs yangs pa'i rgyal
47b2(phal chen): mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ thams cad tshims par byed pa'i bsod nams kyi zhing rab tu 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /chu klung gis lha 'jig rten thams cad kyi dpal gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad
47b3(phal chen): kyi nyon mongs pa rnam par byang bar byed cing / 'khon du 'dzin pa dam po dang / khro ba'i shugs dang bar byed pa zhes bya'o/ /chu klung gi lha tshogs chen po rgya mtsho dpal gyi 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba thams
47b4(phal chen): cad bde ba phun sum tshogs pa myong bar byed cing thar par rgya mtsho la 'dzud pa zhes bya'o/ /de nas chu klung gi lha chu bo kun dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ chu klung gi lha'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa
47b5(phal chen): thams cad la rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /chos rnams rgya mtsho mtha' yas spyod pa dag /thams cad rgyal bas sems can don du sbyangs/ /'jig rten
47b6(phal chen): bkang zhing nyon mongs gdungs pa'i rnams/ /sprin chen cher bzhin rab tu zhi bar mdzad/ /bskal pa brjod du med par rgyal bas sngon/ /smon lam 'od kyis sems can dbyings shes shing / /
47b7(phal chen): 'gro ba yongs smin dbang po chos kyang mkhyen/ /'khyil pa zhes bya chu klung lha dga' bo/ /'gro dang mnyam pa'i snying rje'i tshul bsgoms shing / /mgon po sems can nyon mongs dri ma sbyong / /
47b8(phal chen): yongs smin sems can rgyal ba mngon du lta/ /de la dri med mig gi lha yang mos/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbyangs snyan rgya chen ni/ /kun tu bsgrags pas 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal zhi/ /sangs rgyas
48a1(phal chen): dbyangs snyan thos nas dga' mgu yid/ /rnam thar 'di ni sgra dbyangs sgrog pas thos/ /bskal pa rgya mtshor 'gro la phan don du/ /sngon cad byang chub spyod pa spyad mthong na/ /de phyir de ni phyogs
48a2(phal chen): bkang 'jig rten mdzes/ /lam rgyud stobs pa rjes su dran zhing dga'/ /rgyal ba sngan cad spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe/ /sna tshogs sgo nas sems can smin par mdzad/ /de dag bsod nams rgya mtshos sdug
48a3(phal chen): bsngal 'jil/ /zhi byed chu klung lha ni des dga' bo/ /sbyin pa'i sgo mo tshad med mi zad mang / /'gro ba 'dod pa kun la yongs btang zhing / /rgyal bas 'gro ba'i 'jungs pa yongs su bstsal/ /
48a4(phal chen): kun nas dga' dpal rnam thar 'di mthong ngo / /thabs tshul rgya mtsho thams cad bsgoms pas na/ /yon tan mang po brgya phrag mang pos byung / /rgyal bas 'gro ba thams cad tshim mdzad de/ /rgya
48a5(phal chen): chen sgra dbyangs shugs ldan lha yang dga'/ /sgribs pa'i glong dang 'gro ba'i nyon mongs dri/ /'gro ba rnams la byams pa bskyed sbyangs pas/ /mkha' mnyam 'od kyis sangs rgyas rnam par
48a6(phal chen): mdzes/ /rnam par mdzes pa'i chu klung lha dga' bo/ /sangs rgyas rang byung yon tan rgya mtsho ste/ /bsod nams zhing ni 'dus byas sdug bsngal 'dor/ /byang chub lam la rim gyi yod smin mdzad/ /
48a7(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i tshogs dpal rnam thar 'di yin no/ /de la lo tog gi lha dang 'jam pa'i dpal gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ ro dang mdangs thams cad skyed cing / sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi gzugs kyi sku rab tu
48a8(phal chen): thob pa zhes bya'o/ /lo tog gi lha dus kyi me tog rnam par mdzes pa'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba thams cad nye bar 'tsho bas dga' ba chen po'-i shugs kyi tshim pa skyed pa zhes bya'o/ /lo tog gi lha bstsal
48b1(phal chen): dam pa'i stobs kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ chos thams cad kyi dbyings yongs su rgyas pas shin tu dag pa'i spyod yul zhes bya'o/ /lo tog gi lha mdangs kyi ngad mtha' yas pa rab tu 'gyed pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ snying rje
48b2(phal chen): mtha' yas pa'i sgo nas/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rab tu 'gyed cing rjes su dran pa zhes bya'o/ /lo tog gi lha kun gyi rtsa ba 'bras bu'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas thams cad mngon tu lta zhing /
48b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas rnams la yon tan yang dag par bskyed pa ston pa zhes bya'o/ /lo tog gi lha gtsug pud kha dog sna tshogs kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi mos pa'i me tog yongs su sbyangs pa zhes bya'o/ /
48b4(phal chen): lo tog gi lha yal ga dri ma med par grub pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can la phan pa'i byams pa dang / bsod nams rgya mtsho rgya chen po rnam par 'phel bar byed pa zhes bya'o/ /lo tog gi lha spos sna tshogs shin tu
48b5(phal chen): grub pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ chos thams cad la spyod pa kun tu gnon pas rtsom pa zhes bya'o/ /lo tog gi lha bzang zhing yid du 'ong bar snang ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi zhum pa dang / yid du mi
48b6(phal chen): 'ong ba rnam par zlog cing / chos kyi dbyings thams cad yongs su dag par byed pa zhes bya'o/ /lo tog gi lha kha dog rnam par dag cing / 'od dri ma med pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi dge
48b7(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba la rnam par lta zhing chos kyis 'khor gyi dbang po tshim par byed pa zhes bya'o/ /de nas lo tog gi lha dang 'jam dpal gyis sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ lo tog gi lha'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la rnam par
48b8(phal chen): bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /rang byung ye shes sgron ma skyod pa ni/ /'gro ba kun gyi skyabs dang mgon gyur te/ /ma lus 'gro ba'i bde ba yang dag skyed/ /bsod nams rgya mtsho
49a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bla na med/ /sangs rgyas mnyan na don yod yon tan sprin/ /'gro ba kun gyi sdug bsngal zhi bar mdzad/ /chos rgya chen po mi zad rab tu bskyed/ /dus kyi dkyil 'khor lha ni 'di la 'jug /
49a2(phal chen): bde gshegs stobs ni ma lus yongs su rgyas/ /'gro ba dag ni chos kyi legs pas mdzes/ /'gro ba kun 'dul kun tu rnam par snang / /stobs dang gzugs kyi mthu yis de mthong ngo / /sems kyi skad cig
49a3(phal chen): kun la 'gro mnyam pa'i/ /thugs rjes rgya mtsho snga cad rnam sbyangs pas/ /de phyir rdzu 'phrul rnams ni mtha' yas so/ /de ni mdangs mthong lha yis rab tu mthong / /thabs rnams kun gyi sgo rnams
49a4(phal chen): don yod par/ /sangs rgyas 'jig rten kun tu khyab gyur cing / /'gro ba kun gyi nyon mongs dag par mdzad/ /'di ni thams cad sgo mo'-i rnam thar to/ /'gro ba 'di na mos yangs gang yod pa/ /de dag thams cad
49a5(phal chen): rgyal ba'i mthus byung ste/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes rgya mtsho 'o/ /nag tshal rgyan gyis gtsug pud de la 'jug /'jig rten rnams la byams pa che bskyed de/ /sems can rnams la phan phyir rang byung
49a6(phal chen): skyes/ /lam rab dge ba zhi ba rab tu ston/ /zhi ba sna tshogs dpal gyi rnam thar to/ /phyogs su sems can yongs su smin byed pa'i/ /bde gshegs spyod pa ji ltar rnam dag pa/ /byang chub shing las de dag
49a7(phal chen): sgra yang 'byung / /spos zhim dpal gyi lha yis de thos so/ /rgyal ba'i jig rten yid du 'ong ba spong / /dga' ba ma lus rnams kyang rab tu skyed/ /'gro ba kun gyi dbang po rnam par sbyong / /dge bar snang ba'i
49a8(phal chen): lha yis de mthong ngo / /'gro ba kun na sangs rgyas shin tu 'phags/ /skye bo kun gyi bsam pa de mkhyen to/ /sna tshogs sgo nas 'gro ba yongs smin mdzad/ /rnam dag kha dog 'od kyi rnam thar to/ /de la sman
49b1(phal chen): gyi lha phun sum tshogs pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ bsam pa kun nas rnam par lta ba'i gnon pas 'gro ba rab tu gnon pa zhes bya'o/ /sman gyi lha tsan dan gyi nags tshal gyi shugs 'chang ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/
49b2(phal chen): blta ba yod pas sems can 'dren pa'i 'od ces bya'o/ /sman gyi lha 'od rdul med pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad nyon mongs pa rab tu zhi bas rdul dang bral ba'i sbyor ba zhes bya'o/ /sman gyi lha
49b3(phal chen): ming kun tu grags pa'i glang po'i rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ ming bsgrags pas dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya mtsho yang dag par 'phel ba zhes bya'o/ /sman gyi lha spu'i glong kun nas 'od byung ba'i rnam par thar pa
49b4(phal chen): ni/ nad thams cad la snying rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi shugs kyi rgyal mtshan zhes bya'o/ /sman gyi mun pa rnam par sel cing rnam par sbyong ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba mdongs pa lta bur thams cad kyi
49b5(phal chen): ye shes kyi mig rnam par dag par byed pa zhes bya'o/ /sman gyi lha sgra dbyangs kun tu 'byung ba'-i rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rab tu bsgrags pas don gyi dbyings 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /sman gyi
49b6(phal chen): lha nyi ma'i 'od 'gro ba'i mchog gi rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba thams cad la dge ba'i gshes su ston cing dge ba'i rtsa bas yang dag par bskul ba zhes bya'o/ /sman gyi lha phyogs
49b7(phal chen): bcur rmongs pa med pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ mos pa'i tshul gyis rnam par dag pa'i snying rje'i snying po zhes bya'o/ /sman gyi lha mdangs bzang po kun tu 'gyed pa'i mig gi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems
49b8(phal chen): can thams cad kyi nad rab tu zhi bar byed cing / sangs rgyas rjes su dran par sbyor ba zhes bya'o/ /de nas sman gyi lha phun sum tshogs pas sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ sman gyi lha'i 'khor gyi dkyil
50a1(phal chen): 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smraso/ /sangs rgyas ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab ltos/ /'gro ba kun gyi bsam pa rab tu mkhyen/ /thabs
50a2(phal chen): kyi rnam pa sna tshogs sgo dag nas/ /sdug bsngal kun las sems can rab tu 'grol/ /sangs rgyas chos nyid de ltar bsam mi khyab/ /de yi mthu ni thams cad don kyang yod/ /skye dgu rnams kyi sdug bsngal
50a3(phal chen): zhi bar mdzad/ /tsan dan shugs dang ldan pa'i rnam thar to/ /sngon cad rgyal ba'i chos nyid dag la ltos/ /bskal pa rgya mtsho mtha' med spyod pa na/ /srid pa kun la chags pa gang yang med/ /de la rdul med 'od
50a4(phal chen): kyi lha 'jug go/ /rgyal ba bskal pa stong phrag brgya dag tu/ /mthong zhing mtshan nyid de bzhin shin tu dkon/ /tshul rnams kun tu rang byung don yod de/ /de la rgyal mtshan mchog ni de ltar 'jug /rgyal ba'i
50a5(phal chen): spu yi sgo rnams kun nas kyang / /nad las rab tu grol ba'i 'od bkye bas/ /'jig rten nyon mongs ma lus zhi bar mdzad/ /spu mdangs rgyun gyi rnam thar 'di yin no/ /sdug bsngal las dang nyon mongs
50a6(phal chen): sna tshogs pas/ /'gro ba mdong shing rab tu rmongs gyur rnams/ /sangs rgyas ye shes 'od kyi rnam par spyod/ /de ni mun dang bral ba'i lhas mthong ngo / /rgyal ba'i gsungs gcig las ni mtha' yas
50a7(phal chen): pa'i/ /chos kyi sgo mo thams cad kun kyang 'byung / /de ni sems can ma lus kun kyang shes/ /'di ni sgra dang ldan pa'i rnam thar to/ /rgyal ba'i ye shes bsam gyi mi khyab ltos/ /srid par sems
50a8(phal chen): can yongs su smin byas pa/ /de la 'gro kun mi mgon mngon du snang / /nyi 'od zhi ba'i lha yis de mthong ngo / /sangs rgyas thugs rje'i tshul ni rgya mtsho' ste/ /'gro ba kun la phan don de skyes so/ /
50b1(phal chen): 'gro ba kun la lam rnams shin tu ston/ /de ni phyogs su snang ba'i lhas shes so/ /sangs rgyas 'gro dbang rnams kyi 'od yangs pa/ /phyogs rnams thams cad ma lus kun tu gang / /sangs rgyas rjes
50b2(phal chen): su dran pa'i gzi brjid bskyed/ /mdangs kyi 'od du ldan pa'i rnam thar to// //sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po bzhi pa/
50b3(phal chen): de la nag tshal gyi lha yal ga sna tshogs kyi sprin gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ ye shes rgya mtsho yangs shing mtha' yas pa'i snying po zhes bya'o/ /nags tshal gyi lha 'od kyi phung po sna tshogs kyi mig yid
50b4(phal chen): du 'ong ba'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ dge ba rgya chen po kun nas spungs pa'i shugs shes bya'o/ /nags tshal gyi lha myu gu yid du 'ong ba'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ mos pa sna tshogs kyi myu gu
50b5(phal chen): rnam par 'phel ba dang / yongs su dag par byed pa zhes bya'o/ /nags tshal gyi lha lo ma dri ma med pa'i phreng ba'i dpal gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi rgyan yongs
50b6(phal chen): su sbyong zhing / rnam par bsgom pa zhes bya'o/ /nags tshal gyi lha yan lag rab tu 'chang ba'i gzi brjid kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ shes rab dri ma med pa'i sgo nas chos kyi dbyings la dmigs
50b7(phal chen): shing / kun nas rnam par dmigs pas rgyas par 'gengs pa zhes bya'o/ /nags tshal gyi lha dge ba'i 'od sna tshogs kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi spyod pa rgya mtsho la yang dag par
50b8(phal chen): 'jug pa'i chos kyi sprin mngon par sgrub pa zhes bya'o/ /nags tshal gyi lha sgra skad yid du 'ong ba'i dbyangs kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad kyi yid du mi 'ong ba'i sgra la bzod pa rab tu
51a1(phal chen): thob pas chos kyi snang ba dri ma med pa zhes bya'o/ /nags tshal gyi lha kun nas spos mang po ldang ba'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ spyod pa rgya chen po 'di dkyil 'khor spyod pas yongs su dag par byed cing
51a2(phal chen): phyogs kun tu rnam par snang ba zhes bya'o/ /nags tshal gyi lha kun nas dpal gyi 'od rab tu 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba la phan pa'i don chos thams cad kyi yon tan gyis rgyas par
51a3(phal chen): yang dag par sbyong ba zhes bya'o/ /nags tshal gyi lha me tog dang 'bras bu dang ro'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad la dga' bar lta zhing rjes su dran pa'i yon tan gyi rgyan gyi snying po zhes
51a4(phal chen): bya'o/ /de nas nags tshal gyi lha yal ga sna tshogs kyi sprin gyi sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ nags tshal gyi lha'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su
51a5(phal chen): bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /bsod nams stobs dang ye shes stobs rnams dang / /sngon tshe byang chub spyod pas sangs rgyas byung / /stobs rnams kun gyi rang byung pha rol phyin/ /'gro ba
51a6(phal chen): kun na 'phags shing rnam par mdzes/ /'gro ba thams cad snyed kyi thugs rje'i sgo/ /de bzhin gshegs pas sngon tshe rab tu sbyangs/ /rang byung de bas 'gro ba'i don mdzad do/ /sna
51a7(phal chen): tshogs spungs 'od rnam thar 'di la 'jug / sems can kun gyis bde gshegs mthong ma thag /mos pa rgya mtsho rnam par dag par 'gyur/ /rgyal ba kun gyi lam yang yang dag
51a8(phal chen): ston/ /myu gu yid 'ong 'od kyi rnam thar yin/ /rgyal ba kun gyis ba spu'i yon tan 'khor/ /bskal pa rgya mtsho zad par mi nus te/ /'gro ba kun gyis sangs rgyas bsam mi
51b1(phal chen): khyab/ /rnam thar 'di ni phreng ba'i dpal gyis mthong / /sngan cad rgyal bas sangs rgyas gang gis rnams/ /zhing mang rdul snyed mchod pa de dag dran/ /kun tu shes rab dkyil 'khor rnam par
51b2(phal chen): sbyangs/ /yal ga 'od kyis brjid kyis 'di mthong ngo / /'gro ba kun gyi spyod pa rgya mtsho dag /skad cig gcig gis sangs rgyas thugs su chud/ /rgyal ba'i ye shes chags med
51b3(phal chen): shin tu yangs/ /sna tshogs 'gyur sprungs 'od kyi 'di mthong ngo / /bde gshegs gsungs ni zhi ba rab zhir gsung / /dga' ba yangs pa chen po rnam par skyed/ /sems can mos
51b4(phal chen): pa ji bzhin de dag shes/ /'di n-i sgra rnams sgrogs pa'i dbyangs kyi thos/ /phyogs bcu'i zhing gi dbyings rnams rgyas byas shing / /sangs rgyas byin brlabs rgya chen rab tu 'byung / /
51b5(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sngon gyi spyod pa dag kyang ston/ /kun tu dri zhim 'od dpal 'di la 'jug /ma rung sems can yon tan med pa'i rnams/ /myos shing 'khor ba kun tu 'khor ba dag /de dag
51b6(phal chen): la ni thams cad mkhyen lam ston/ /'phags pa'i 'od kyis 'khor gyis 'di mthong ngo / /sems can ma rungs sbyor ba spyod pa rnams/ /bskal pa bye bas sangs rgyas mthong bar
51b7(phal chen): 'gyur/ /gzhan ni bde gshegs skad cig gcig gis lta/ /ri'i 'od kyi lha yis 'di mthong ngo / /de la ri'i lha rin po che'i rtse mo'i me tog shin tu rgyas par gnas pa'i rnam par thar
51b8(phal chen): pa ni/ bsam gtan zhi zhing yangs la dben pa'i snang ba la rab tu 'jug pa zhes bya'o/ /ri'i lha nags tshal sna tshogs me tog shin tu rgyas pa'i gtsug phud kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba
52a1(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su smin par byed pa'i byams pa sgom pa'i rgyan ces bya'o/ /ri'i lha kun nas shin tu 'phags pas rnam par snang ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can
52a2(phal chen): thams cad kyi bsam pa rnam par lta ba'i dbang po la 'jug pas mngon par snang ba zhes bya'o/ /ri'i lha rdul thams cad dang mi gnas pas dri ma med pa'i gtsug phud kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ bskal pa rgya mtsho
52a3(phal chen): mtha' yas pas mi skyo ba'i brtson 'grus kyis rab tu sbyor ba zhes bya'o/ /ri'i lha snang bas phyogs su gsol ba'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan mtha' yas pa'i snang ba rnam par
52a4(phal chen): bstan pa ston pa zhes bya'o/ /ri'i lha stobs la thub pa med pa'i snang ba'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir gti mug yongs su sil ba'i 'od ces bya'o/ /
52a5(phal chen): ri'i lha kun nas gzi brjid dpal gyi dkyil 'khor gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ chags pa thams cad dang mnyam pa'i rgyan gyi sdugs bsngal yang dag par 'joms pa zhes bya'o/ /ri'i lha snang ba'i
52a6(phal chen): rdul chu bo'i dkyil 'khor gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bstan pa'i yon tan snang ba yang dag par ston pa zhes bya'o/ /ri'i lha kun tu mngon par lta ba'i mig gi
52a7(phal chen): rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad kyi rmi lam gyi mthar yang dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par 'phel bar byed pa zhes bya'o/ /ri'i lha kun nas sra ba'i rdo rje'i mtshams kyi mig gi rnam
52a8(phal chen): par thar pa ni/ don rgya mtsho rgya chen po mtha' yas pa dang / 'grogs pa zhes bya'o/ /de nas ri'i lha rin po che'i rtse mo me tog shin tu rgyas par gnas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi
52b1(phal chen): mthus/ ri'i lha'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /rgyal ba'i rnam 'phrul mi zad tshad med ltos/ /sngon tshe
52b2(phal chen): spyod rab mtha' yas rgyal bas spyod/ /rnam thar zhing gi rdul snyed bsgom mdzad pas/ /'gro ba ma lus dga' ba'i shugs kyang skyed/ /sangs rgyas spu nas dri ma med dpal bkye/ /yan lag
52b3(phal chen): mtshan brgyan 'gro ba kun bkang zhing / /byams tshul mtha' yas 'jig rten kun la ston/ /nags tshal rgyas pa'i gtsug gi rnam thar to/ /sangs rgyas sku ni mtha' yas 'gro bar mngon/ /'jig rten
52b4(phal chen): kun tu phyogs bcu bkang zhing 'phags/ /dbang po dang ba'i sems can rangs shing dga'/ /rnam thar 'di la 'phags pa'i rgyal mtshan 'jug /rang byung mkha' mnyam 'jig rten kun ma chags/ /
52b5(phal chen): bskal pa kun spyod brtson 'grus stobs mi skyo/ /sna tshogs mkhas 'gro sbyor ba ma lus 'dul/ /dga' ba dri med gtsug phud rnam thar to/ /'jig rten kun ni mdongs gyur mun stug zhugs/ /
52b6(phal chen): thugs rjes der bskyed sangs rgyas 'od bkye zhing / /'gro khams yun rings nyal ba sad par mdzad/ /rigs nas dga' 'od lha'i rnam thar to/ /srid pa'i rgya mtshor spyad pa sngon spyod tshe/ /
52b7(phal chen): zhing rdul mnyam pa'i sems can gtso mchod pas/ /de dag dgyes bzhin sems can byang chub bkod/ /zhi ba'i sa 'di stobs 'chang lha 'jug go/ /las kyi sprin sgrib g.yogs shing
52b8(phal chen): bsgribs pa rnams/ /srid par sems can sdug bsngal 'khor gzigs nas/ /de dag mun pa ye shes 'od kyis bstsal/ /gzi brjid dpal 'od rnam thar 'di sems so/ /
53a1(phal chen): rgyal ba'i spu las sangs rgyas yon tan kun/ /phyogs dbyings sems can bsam pa bzhin du grags/ /rdzu 'phrul rnam pa bskal pa kun tu gnas/ /'od ma rdul gyi chu bo'i lha 'jug
53a2(phal chen): go/ /sems can kun spyod dge ba rgya mtsho kun/ /de la phyogs bkang sangs rgyas mngon par snang / /sna tshogs thabs ky-is 'jig rten chos kyang ston/ /tshul mngon mig gi lha yis de thos so/ /
53a3(phal chen): chos sgo rgya mtsho mi zad tshad med pa/ /sangs rgyas gsung gcig sems can kun la gsung / /bskal pa kun brjod 'jig rten mang la ston/ /rdo rje tshul mig 'di yi gnas la 'jug /de la sa'i lha dpal
53a4(phal chen): gyi me tog kun nas shin tu rgyas par dri ma med pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ skad cig skad cig cing sems can thams cad la byams pa dang / snying rje'i dkyil 'khor gyis rnam par lta ba zhes bya'o/ /sa'i lha bsod
53a5(phal chen): nams brten pa shin tu bsags pa'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi stobs dang shugs kyi rgyan ces bya'o/ /sa'i lha sems can rin po ches rgyas pa'i rnam par thar
53a6(phal chen): pa ni/ ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs bsgoms pa rnam par 'byed pa dri ma med pa zhes bya'o/ /sa'i lha dus su dge ba'i mig rab tu ston pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad dga' zhing bde ba dang
53a7(phal chen): rtse ba'i sbyor ba zhes bya'o/ /sa'i lha gser gyi mig gi dpal gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ lus thams cad yongs su dag par byed pa'i tshul stan pa zhes bya'o/ /sa'i lha spu las spos kyi 'od rnam
53a8(phal chen): par 'gyed pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yon tan rgya mtsho thams cad rnam par sgom pa brjod pa zhes bya'o/ /sa'i lha sgra dbyangs yid du 'ong ba bsgrogs pa'i rnam par thar
53b1(phal chen): pa ni/ 'gro ba thams cad smra ba'i sgra rgya mtsho byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya'o/ /sa'i lha me tog gi klong sna tshogs kyi gtsug pud kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing phun sum tshogs pa'i rang bzhin
53b2(phal chen): dri ma med pa zhes bya'o/ /sa'i lha kun nas rdo rje'i rdul gyi rgyud kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi 'khor lo byin gyi rlabs kun nas rgyu zhing 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /sa'i lha khyim
53b3(phal chen): dri ma med pa'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi tshul la yang dag par 'jug pa'i chos kyi rgyan bsgom pa 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /de nas sa'i lha dpal gyi me tog kun nas
53b4(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa dri ma med pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus sa'i lha'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sngan cad skad cig skad
53b5(phal chen): cig bde gshegs kyis/ /brjod du med pa'i snying rje'i sgo rnams dang / /byams pa'i sgo yang mi zad sgoms pas na/ /de tshe sangs rgyas sku ni mi shigs sra/ /dus gsum gtogs pa'i sems can
53b6(phal chen): bsod nams dang / /snying rje byang chub sems dpa'i bsod nams dag /rgyal ba'i spu gcig de snyed bsod nams 'od/ /bsod nams de mthong rab tu dga' bar 'gyur/ /'byung ba med cing byon pa gang yang
53b7(phal chen): med/ /ting 'dzin zhi ba rgya mtsho rab tu zhugs/ /sems can rgyan gyi sa 'di rab tu ston/ /'di ni sna tshogs shing gi ze ba'i sa yin no/ /sngon cad thub pas spyod pa spyad pa dang / /'gro ba'i sgrib pa rnam par zlog pa ni/ /rin chen
53b8(phal chen): bkram pa'i 'od kyi sa yin te/ /rnam thar de la dga' bar lha lta'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa ni mtha' yas te/ /'jig rten kun tu skad cig cig la ston/ /dus tshod yang dag ston pa'i sa yi lha/ /dga'
54a1(phal chen): bar sangs rgyas yul la rnam par lta/ /sangs rgyas gsung ni mtha' yas bsam mi khyab/ /sems can kun bsgrags nyon mongs zhi bar mdzad/ /gser 'od mig gi dpal ni rab dga' ba/ /
54a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas mnga' ba ste/ /sangs rgyas sprul pas rnam par kun gzugs su/ /phyogs kun chos kyi dbyings su rgyas par mdzad/ /spu las dri zhim 'od kyi sa yi lha/ /sangs rgyas sems can
54a3(phal chen): 'dul ba de la lta/ /phyogs rnams yid 'ong dbyangs kyis gang byas shing / /'gro ba 'di ni phyi mtha'i bskal par brjod/ /yid du 'ong ba'i sgra dbyangs sa'i lha/ /rab tu dga' bar sangs rgyas dbyangs la nyan/ /rgyal
54a4(phal chen): ba'i spu las sems can mnyam pa yi/ /spos kyi 'od bkye 'jig rten kun bkang zhing / /sems can ma lus yongs su smin mdzad cing / /me tog gtsug phud 'phyang bas yang dag mthong / /de bzhin gshegs
54a5(phal chen): sku rdo rje lta bu ste/ /mtshams su mi phyed sra ba'i ri bo 'dra/ /'gro ba kun gyis sangs rgyas bskyed mi nus/ /rdo rje rdul kyi lha ni des dga' 'o/ /de la grong khyer gyi lha rin chen rtse mo'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can
54a6(phal chen): la phan pa yang dag par sbyar ba 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /grong khyer gyi lha rgyan rnam pa sna tshogs 'byung ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba'i dbang po yongs su smin par byed pa'i 'dul ba 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /grong
54a7(phal chen): khyer gyi lha rin chen dri med shin tu dge ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad bsod nams dang dga' ba myong bar byed pa zhes bya'o/ /grong khyer gyi lha slos pa'i mya ngan thams cad spong bas rnam par snang ba'i
54a8(phal chen): rnam par thar pa ni/ skyob pa dang mi 'jigs pa dang / snying rje chen po zhes bya'o/ /grong khyer gyi lha sgron ma shin tu rgyas pa'i mig gi rnam par thar pa ni/ shes rab kyi kun tu rnam par 'byed pa zhes bya'o/ /grong
54b1(phal chen): khyer gyi lha 'od 'phro ba'i dpal mngon par 'bar ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ thabs kyi sgo kun nas ston pa'i mthu zhes bya'o/ /grong khyer gyis lha bsod nams kyi shugs snang ba'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/
54b2(phal chen): 'gro ba kun gyis bsod nams 'byung ba'i snang ba zhes bya'o/ /grong khyer gyi lha lus dri ma med pas mnyam pa'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can rmongs pa thams cad la rmi lam rnam par ston pa'i
54b3(phal chen): 'od ces bya'o/ /grong khyer gyi lha spos kyi rgyal mtshan gtsug phud kyi rgyan gyis rnam par thar pa ni/ nyon mongs pa dang mi dge ba'i dri ma rnam par sel cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi dri yang dag par bskyed pa
54b4(phal chen): zhes bya'o/ /grong khyer gyi lha rin chen dpal gyi 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgrib pa'i ri rnam par 'jom pa'i 'od ces bya'o/ /de nas grong khyer gyi lha rin po che'i rtse mo'i 'od kyis
54b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ grong khyer gyi lha'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /mgon po'i chos nyid
54b6(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ /snang ba rnyes shing phyogs su rnam par mdzes/ /sems can mtha' yas yongs su smin mdzad pa'i/ /sangs rgyas 'gro ba kun la mngon du snang / /sems can
54b7(phal chen): thams cad dbang po sna tshogs te/ /de dag ma lus rgyal bas 'gro bar mkhyen/ /rnam thar 'di ni rab tu thob pa'i phyir/ /sna tshogs 'od 'byung lha yang rab tu dga'/ /rgyal bas bskal pa mtha'
54b8(phal chen): yas yang dag spyad/ /sngon chad rgyal bas chos kyang yang dag bzung / /dga' ba'i yid kyis rtag tu de dag blangs/ /rnam thar 'di ni dga' ba'i 'od kyis mthong / /'gro ba 'dir ni thugs rje byams
55a1(phal chen): bskyed cing / /de bzhin gshegs pas sngan cad sems can rnams/ /kun gyi mya ngan mtha' yas rnam par zlog /nyon mongs yongs su sbyong ba 'di la dga'/ /rgyal bas shes
55a2(phal chen): rab rgya che mtha' yas te/ /tshad med nam mkha' 'dra zhing mtshungs pa yin/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i shes rab rnam spyod pas/ /mar me'i me tog 'od kyi lha dga' 'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pas
55a3(phal chen): 'gro mnyam sku gzugs rnams/ /'gro ba kun gyi bsam pa rnams la bstan/ /de 'dra'i tshul la rab tu bsgoms pa yis/ /mngon 'od 'phro ba'i lha de rab tu dga'/ /bsod nams rgya mtsho rgya
55a4(phal chen): chen mtha' yas pa/ /sngon chad de bzhin gshegs pas yongs su sbyangs/ /de 'dra'i rnam par thar la rnam lta bas/ /bsod nams dpal gyi 'od de rab tu dga'/ /srid par rab tu rmongs pa'i sems
55a5(phal chen): can rnams/ /'khor gyur rab rib mdongs pa gzigs pas na/ /de dag phan phyir sangs rgyas mngon du byung / /dri med 'od kyis rnam thar 'di thob po/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdzu 'phrul stobs la ltos/ /
55a6(phal chen): 'gro la sprin 'dra mtha' dang dbus yang med/ /de dag bstan cing 'gro ba rnam par 'dul/ /spos kyi rgyal mtshan 'od kyis 'di mthong ngo / /sems can rmongs pa mun pas mdongs gyur cing / /rnam
55a7(phal chen): pa sna tshogs sgribs pas bsgribs gyur pa/ /sangs rgyas 'od kyis rnam par kun shes 'gyur/ /rtse mo'i 'od kyi lha ni 'di la 'jug /de la snying po byang chub kyi lha dge ba dri ma med pa'i rgyun gyis brgyan pa'i
55a8(phal chen): rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas mang po mchod pa yang dag par 'byung zhing / sngon gyi smon lam gyi rgyan ston pa zhes bya'o/ /snying po byang chub kyi lha ri rab spo'i rin po che'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/
55b1(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad dang mngon sum du byang chub kyi spyod pa yang dag par bsgrub cing 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /snying po byang chub kyi lha dbyangs kyi 'brug sgra sgrogs pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can
55b2(phal chen): thams cad kyi bsam pa la sangs rgyas ston cing rmi lam gyi mthar/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi 'brug sgra sgrogs pa zhes bya'o/ /snying po byang chub ky-i lha me tog gi char sna tshogs 'bab pa'i mig gi rnam par thar
55b3(phal chen): pa ni/ dga' ba thams cad yongs su gtong zhing rin po che'i char 'beb pa'i rgyan ces bya'o/ /snying po byang chub kyi lha 'od 'phro mang po shin tu dri ma med pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ 'dul ba'i sems can yongasu
55b4(phal chen): smin par byed cing snying po byang chub kyi phun sum tshogs pa sna tshogs ston pa zhes bya'o/ /snying po byang chub kyi lha me tog gi phreng ba 'od kyi gtsug phud kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad kyi dbang po
55b5(phal chen): bzhin du chos kyi tshul zab mo dran pa ston pa 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /snying po byang chub kyi lha rin po che'i rgyan gyi char rab tu 'bebs pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ dga' ba yang dag par myong ba mtha' yas pa la
55b6(phal chen): yang dag par 'jug pa zhes bya'o/ /snying po byang chub kyi lha mthu dam pa spos kyi mig gi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang legs pa rab tu brjod pa'i byin gyis rlabs zhes bya'o/ /
55b7(phal chen): snying po byang chub kyi lha rdo rje sna tshogs kyi sprin gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ snying po byang chub rnam pa mtha' yas pa yang dag par ston pa'i rgyan ces bya'o/ /snying po byang chub kyi lha pad+mo'i shing snang ba'i 'od kyi
55b8(phal chen): rnam par thar pa ni/ byang chub kyi shing yongs su zhi bas phyogs rgyas par byed pa zhes bya'o/ /snying po byang chub kyi lha dge ba'i lta ba sna tshogs rnam par ston pa'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs
56a1(phal chen): pa'i stobs sna tshogs yang dag par rgyu ba zhes bya'o/ /de nas snying po byang chub kyi lha dge ba dri ma med pa'i rgyan gyi brgyan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ snying po byang chub kyi lha'i 'khor gyi
56a2(phal chen): dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /bskal pa mang po mtha' dang dbus med par/ /de bzhin gshegs pas ji ltar sngon spyad dran/ /sangs rgyas thams
56a3(phal chen): cad mchod cing bsgrubs pas na/ /de phyir de yi bsod nams nam mkha'i tshad/ /zhing rnams mtha' yas tshad med 'dra med par/ /mi zad gtong ba'i sgo nas sngon btang bas/ /ri bo spo'i 'od kyi lha de ni/ /bde gshegs dran zhing
56a4(phal chen): rab tu dga' bar 'gyur/ /bde gshegs sprul pa rnam pa mtha' yas pa/ /de dag zhing rnams kun tu rab tu rgyu/ /'gro bar sangs rgyas rmi lam bzhin ston cing / /sprin gyi sgra dbyangs lha de rab tu dga'/ /mtha' yas
56a5(phal chen): skal par dka' ba rab spyad do/ /dang ba'i spyan gyis 'gro la phan pa'i phyir/ /rgya mtsho'i spyan yang yongs su sngon btang ste/ /de la me tog mig gi lha dga' bo/ /yon tan rin chen 'od 'phro mtha' yas sprin/ /'gro ba kun
56a6(phal chen): tu snying po byang chub nas/ /rab tu bkye ba'i sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul gyis/ /'od 'phro 'gyed pa'i lus kyi lha yang dga'/ /sems can rnams kyi spyod pa rgya mtsho ste/ /de las rgyal ba chos kyi char yang 'bebs/ /ji ltar mos
56a7(phal chen): par nem nur rnam par sel/ /de yis gtsug phud 'phyang ba dga' ba thob/ /rgyan gyi char 'bebs mig bzang lha de ni/ /sems kyi skad cig gcig gis tshad med pa'i/ /chos don dbyings kyi bye brag mtha' yas pa/ /
56a8(phal chen): rgya mtsho tha dad yang dag shes pas 'jug /zhing rnams brjod du med pa thams cad du/ /'gro ba kun la sangs rgyas legs brjod pas/ /de phyir yon tan sangs rgyas zhing kun grags/ /de ni rjesu spos mig lha yang dran/ /
56b1(phal chen): mtha' yas shing gi rnam pa sna tshogs gzugs/ /byang chub shing la kun kyang ma lus bstan/ /rdo rje sna tshogs sprin gyi lha de ni/ /byang chub shing la dga' bar rnam par lta/ /sangs rgyas ye shes snying po byang chub la/ /phyogs
56b2(phal chen): rnams kun tu mtha' dang mu med de/ /pad+mo snang zhing gsal ba'i lha de ni/ /rnam thar rnam yangs 'di la rab dga' bo/ /sangs rgyas stobs rnams yongs dag bsam mi khyab/ /snying po byang chub 'dir ni kun kyang grag /yang dag bsgrubs
56b3(phal chen): pas byung ba de dag ni/ /thams cad sna tshogs snang ba'i 'od nyan to/ /de la rkang gis 'gro rin chen dpal gyi phyag rgya'i rnam par thar pa ni/ dga' ba yangs pa rin po che'i char gyis kun tu khyab pa zhes bya'o/ /rkang gis 'gro pad+mo snang ba'i 'od
56b4(phal chen): zer gyi 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi sku 'od zer gyi kha dog pad+mo'i dra ba thams cad du ston pas dga' bar byed pa zhes bya'o/ /rkang gi 'gro me tog gtsug phud kyi dpal dri ma med pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sems kyi skad cig thams
56b5(phal chen): cad la de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi dbyibs dang rgyan 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /rkang gis 'gro shin tu mdzes par gnon pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ gom pa 'dor ba thams cad mtha' yas pa 'dul ba'i rgyan ces bya'o/ /rkang gi 'gro
56b6(phal chen): rin chen dpal gyi rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ skad cig cig gi pad+mo'i dra ba sna tshogs sprul pa byed cing rin po che'i char pa dang dbyangs dang snang ba kun tu 'gyed pa zhes bya'o/ /rkang gis 'gro dga' ba'i dbyangs snyan pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/
56b7(phal chen): dga' ba shugs dang nyams bde ba'i rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /rkang gi 'gro shing tsan dan gyi 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du spos kyi ngad sprin du ldang ba zhes bya'o/ /rkang gis 'gro pad+mo yid du 'ong
56b8(phal chen): ba'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ pad+mo'i gseb thams cad nas yid du 'ong ba'i chos kyi dbyings 'byung bas snang ba skyed pa zhes bya'o/ /rkang gis 'gro rdul gyi shugs kyi 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni lus kyi 'od zer rnam pa sna tshogs thams
57a1(phal chen): cad kyi dra bas snang ba byed pa zhes bya'o/ /rkang gis 'gro me tog mang po'i dkyil 'khor gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad la dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya mtshos yang dag par skul ba 'byung ba
57a2(phal chen): zhes bya'o/ /de nas rkang gis 'gro rin chen dpal gyi phyag rgya sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ rkang gis 'gro ba'i lha'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su
57a3(phal chen): bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /dga' ba rgya mtsho'i tshul gyis shugs bskyed cing / /bskal pa mtha' yas sngon chad spyod pa mdzad/ /zhing rnams kun tu rdul shin tu phra mnyam pa'i/ /sangs rgyas rnams
57a4(phal chen): kyang dgyes pa'i thugs kyi mchod/ /skad gcig sems la pad mo brjod yangs pa/ /dri zhim sna tshogs mngon par sprul mdzad nas/ /zhing rnams kun tu rgyal ba gshegs mdzad pa/ /snang ba'i 'od zer ltar
57a5(phal chen): des rab tu mthong / /'dren pa rnams kyi chos nyid bsam mi khyab/ /'khor rnams kun tu 'byam klas mtha' yas pa'i/ /rnam par 'phrul pa mi zad rab tu ston/ /me tog gtsug phud lta des de mthong ngo / /
57a6(phal chen): phyogs bcu'i zhing gi dbyings rnams ma lus pa/ /thams cad kun tu gshegs shing bzhud pa yi/ /sems can mtha' yas yongs su smin par mdzad/ /shin tu mdzes pas dga' bar de mthong ngo / /
57a7(phal chen): sems can snyed kyi sprul pa kun 'phros pas/ /re re'i sku yi chos kyi dbyings kyang 'gengs/ /rin chen dri med 'od kyang rab tu gtong / /rkang 'gro dpal gyi mtshan gyi 'di mthong ngo / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i
57a8(phal chen): spyod yul mtha' yas te/ /'khor du rgyal ba chos kyi char yang 'babs/ /bde gshegs de'i 'khor na dgar gnas shing / /dga' sgra dbyangs kyi rnam thar de mthong ngo / /sangs rgyas dbyangs ni mkha' dang mnyam
57b1(phal chen): pa ste/ /dbyangs kyi yan lag yon tan kun dang ldan/ /'jig rten kun bkang sems can rnam par 'dul/ /tsan dan shing gi 'od ni de la nyan/ /spu rtse kun nas rgyal ba rnam 'phrul dang / /dus gsum gshegs pa'i
57b2(phal chen): rgyal ba'i mtshan rnams kyi/ /sgra bsgrags thos shing dga' ba skyer 'gyur te/ /de ni rdo rje 'od kyi lhas mthong ngo / /de bzhin gshegs sku bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ /gom pa gom par yon tan rgya mtsho ston/ /de dag sems can
57b3(phal chen): ji ltar mos pas mthong / /rdul gyi 'od kyi lhas ni de mthong ngo / /'jig rten mgon po rnam 'phrul rnam mang gis/ /phyogs bcur sems can yang dag skul ba mdzad/ /me tog 'khor mang rkang pas 'gro ba'i lha/ /
57b4(phal chen): mthong zhing dga' ba yangs pa rab tu 'thob/ /de la lus kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha khrel dang dge bas rgyas pa'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sngon gyi smon lam rjes su dran pas rnam par
57b5(phal chen): dpyod pa zhes bya'o/ /lus kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha 'od zer phyogs su snang ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams mu med par sangs rgyas kyi 'od rnam par ston pa'i rgyan ces bya'o/ /lus kyi ris su gtogs
57b6(phal chen): pa'i lha sgras 'dul ba rgya mtsho'i dpal gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi gsung 'dul ba'i sems can thams cad la brjod cing yang dag par skul bas rgal 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /lus kyi ris su gtogasu
57b7(phal chen): pa'i lha rgyan bzang po'i me tog gtsug phud kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku nam mkha'i mtshan nyid kyi byin gyis rlabs kun nas rab tu gnas pa 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /lus kyi ris su gtogs
57b8(phal chen): pa'i lha spyod yul mtha' yas dpal gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul 'gro ba rnams la yang dag par ston pa'i mthu zhes bya'o/ /lus kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha snang ba'i phreng ba 'dzin pa'i
58a1(phal chen): dpal gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad gsal ba dang 'dres pa'i mdangs kyis dga' ba zhes bya'o/ /lus kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha spos dri ma med pa'i sprin las char 'babs pa'i 'od kyi rnam
58a2(phal chen): par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i dri ma mngon par sel ba'i sbyor ba zhes bya'o/ /lus kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha srung 'dzin yongs su sdug pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad
58a3(phal chen): kyi bdud kyi las dang rmongs pa rnam par zlog pa zhes bya'o/ /lus kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha sgo kun nas yongs su gnon pa la mngon du gyur pa'i mig gi rnam par thar pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi dbang po thams cad kyi gnas
58a4(phal chen): su rgyal ba rnam par dmigs par mngon du ston pa'i rgyan ces bya'o/ /lus kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha khrel dang dpal mi g.yo ba'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i shugs thams cad yang
58a5(phal chen): dag par 'dzin cing / yang dag par sbyong ba zhes bya'o/ /de nas lus kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha khrel dang dge bas rgyas pa'i 'od kyis sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ lus kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor
58a6(phal chen): yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /ri rab rdul phran shin tu phra snyed kyi/ /bskal pa de dag pha snga'i bskal pa ni/ /rdul ces bya bar 'od mdzes 'od zer rgyal/ /
58a7(phal chen): mchod da smon lam btab pa bdag gis dran/ /sangs rgyas sku las 'od 'phro rab bkye ba/ /de'i 'od zer chos kyi dbyings su rgyu/ /rgyal ba'i 'od zer dra ba sems can 'dul/ /'od 'phro 'od zer lha yis de mthong ngo / /
58a8(phal chen): dbyangs kyi yan lag yon tan kun rgyas pa'i/ /sangs rgyas gsung ni zhing rnams kun tu sgrogs/ /'gro ba ma lus thams cad yang dag bskul/ /dbyangs kyis 'dul ba de la dga' bas nyan/ /rgyal ba'i
58b1(phal chen): sku ni rab tu zhi ba ltos/ /sku gzugs du ma'ang mtshan nyid mi mnga' ste/ /'gro ba kun na'ang bzhugs par rab tu snang / /me tog gtsug gis ji bzhin nyid du mthong / /'dren pa'i chos nyid bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ /
58b2(phal chen): sems can de dag dad pa ci bzhin du/ /la la bzhugs dang bzhengs dang gshegs par mthong / /de yang spyod lam 'byung ba'i lha mthong ngo / /rgyal ba'i tshems kyis mtshams rnams thams cad nas/ /dri zhim 'od
58b3(phal chen): 'phro sgron ma'i sprin bkye bas/ /'gro ba kun gyi nyon mongs zhi bar 'gyur/ /dri med spos kyi sprin gyis de mthong ngo / /sangs rgyas mgon po 'gro ba'i skyabs su byung / /nyon mongs shin tu sdug bsngal gzir
58b4(phal chen): ba rnams/ /mgu bar mdzad cing nyon mongs thams cad bsal/ /snang ba'i phreng ba 'chang bas 'di mthong ngo / /'dren pa bskal pa brgyar yang shin tu dkon/ /rang byung 'jig rten don mdzad skyes pa ni/ /
58b5(phal chen): 'jig rten kun gyi dbul ba rnam par sel/ /khrel yod dpal gyi 'od snang de skad smra/ /sems can nyon mongs sgrib pas nyon mongs shing / /bdud kyi las kyis bkrugs te 'phyin pa'i rnams/ /de dag rgyal
58b6(phal chen): ba rnam thar lam ston to/ /srung zhing skyong ba'i dpal gyis de mthong ngo / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa ltos/ /sangs rgyas sprin gyis chos kyi dbyings mnan cing / /'jig rten dbang po gnas su
58b7(phal chen): sems can 'dul/ /kun sgo'i mig gi dpal gyi spyod yul lo/ /de la lag na rdo rje mthu chen kha dog bzang po'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ yon tan mtha' yas pa dang / gzugs kyi sku rnam par dpyod pa
58b8(phal chen): yang dag par ston pa zhes bya'o/ /lag na rdo rje nyi ma'i shugs kyi rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ba spu las nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gyi sprin sna tshogs kyi rgyan 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /
59a1(phal chen): lag na rdo rje ri rab me tog 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ rnam par 'phrul pa rgya chen po bstan pas/ yon tan mtha' yas pa'i lus su 'phrul pa zhes bya'o/ /lag na rdo rje rnam dag sprin gyi dbyangs kyi
59a2(phal chen): rnam par thar pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbyangs mtha' yas tshad med pa'i rjes su song ba zhes bya'o/ /lag na rdo rje dbang po shin tu mang ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi dbang po thams cad kyi rnam
59a3(phal chen): par 'phrul pa ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis yang dag par skul ba zhes bya'o/ /lag na rdo rje yid du 'ong ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings rab tu phye ba thams cad ma lus pa
59a4(phal chen): la yang dag par spyod pa zhes bya'o/ /lag na rdo rje shing gi sgra dbyangs kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ shing gi lha thams cad 'dren pa'i rgyan yid du 'ong bas brgyan pa zhes bya'o/ /lag na rdo rje seng ge'i 'od kyi rgyal po'i rnam
59a5(phal chen): par thar pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams kyi dkyil 'khor yangs pa'i tshogs kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i yod ces bya'o/ /lag na rdo rje 'od 'phro stug po'i dpal gyi mig gi rnam par thar pa ni/ sems
59a6(phal chen): can ma rungs pa'i rgyud la lus 'jigs 'jigs ltar rab tu ston cing kun tu rnam par lta ba zhes bya'o/ /lag na rdo rje rin chen gtsug phud pad mo'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i rgyan
59a7(phal chen): thams cad kyis brgyan pa'i gtsug phud gi nor bu rin po che thams cad kyi char mngon par 'bebs pa zhes bya'o/ /de nas lag na rdo rje mthu chen kha dog bzang po'i 'od kyi sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ lag na rdo rje'i
59a8(phal chen): 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /chos rgyal chos kyis mdzes pa yi/ /chos nyid de la rnam par ltos/ /yon tan mtha' yas
59b1(phal chen): sku gzugs kyis/ /'jig rten kun tu rnam par mdzes/ /sangs rgyas ba spu thams cad nas/ /'od zer dra ba bsam myi khyab/ /nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor 'dra ba ste/ /phyogs bcu kun tu rnam par mdzes/ /sangs
59b2(phal chen): rgyas rnam 'phrul de dag gis/ /chos kyi dbyings su khyab byas shing / /'gro ba kun la mngon sum du/ /mi zad sku ni shin tu ston/ /sangs rgyas gsung gi dkyil 'khor ni/ /zhing rnams kun tu rab tu sgrog /
59b3(phal chen): gsungs gi sems can thams cad kyis/ /bsam pa thams cad rab tu 'gengs/ /'jig rten dbang po kun gnas na/ /thub pa rab tu bzhugs par snang / /de dag thams cad 'khor rnams la/ /'dren pa dag
59b4(phal chen): gi chos ston mdzad/ /rgya mtsho chos kyi sgo bskul bas/ /gzhan dang gzhan gyi tshul dag gis/ /thams cad chos kyi bye brag don/ /rgyal ba zad med rab tu ston/ /rgya chen mtha' med tshul dag la/ /rgya mtsho
59b5(phal chen): 'khor rnam rab tu 'jug / sangs rgyas 'od zer rab 'dres pas/ /kun gyis 'dren pa mthong bar 'gyur/ /zhing rnams bye ma'i rdul snyed du/ /rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun mchod pas/ /bsod nams rgya chen
59b6(phal chen): nam mkha' bzhin/ /kun gyis 'dren pa rab tu mthong / /sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul ma 'dres pa/ /thams cad zhing du ston pa mdzad/ /'gro la sangs rgyas mngon sum du/ /byang chub snying por rnam par mdzes/ /
59b7(phal chen): 'od zer sna tshogs dkyil 'khor gyi/ /'od 'phro sprin ni kun tu snang / /chos dbyings kun tu khyab byas shing / /sangs rgyas spyod yul rab tu ston/ /de la byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i rnam par thar
59b8(phal chen): pa ni/ tshul rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho la 'jug ste/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yongs su dag par bya ba dang / 'gro ba gdul ba la mthar
60a1(phal chen): thugs par mngon par sgrub pa zhes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi zhabs kyi drung du phyin pas/ yon tan gyi tshogs thams cad kyi yul zhes bya ba'i rnam par
60a2(phal chen): thar pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi sa nas sar smon lam rgya mtshos rab tu gnas pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa dang / sgo thams cad nas chos kyi dbyings su bdag gi lus kyi sprin rdul snyed
60a3(phal chen): mtha' yas pas rgyas par 'gengs pa zhes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa dang / zhing thams cad du rang gi ming bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i 'khor lo sgrog pa'i byin gyis rlabs shes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul
60a4(phal chen): shin tu phra ba'i thams cad kyi sbubs su byang chub sems dpa'i yul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' dang dbus med pa yang dag par ston pa zhes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa dang / dus gsum gyi bskal pa skad
60a5(phal chen): cig gcig tu ston pas 'byung ba dang / 'jig pa rab tu 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dbang po rgya mtsho'i yul phan tshun du 'jug pa yang dag par ston pa zhes bya ba'i
60a6(phal chen): rnam par thar pa dang / gang 'di chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa rang gi lus kyi sprul pas rgyas par rnam par 'phrul pa'i byin gyis rlabs shes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa dang / gang 'di byang chub sems
60a7(phal chen): dpa'i chos thams cad kyi tshul phan tshun du ston pa rgya chen pos thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshul la 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa dag go/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po rnam par thar
60a8(phal chen): pa'i tshul rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa dag gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho la 'jug cing sangs rgyas kyi mthus 'khor rgya mtsho yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs
60b1(phal chen): su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /zhing rnams rgyal bas dri med rnam par sbyangs/ /mkha' yangs rdul bzhin yon tan tshad kyang myed/ /sngon gyi rgyal ba'i sras po dri med kyis/ /de la bsam yas chos sprin char
60b2(phal chen): yang phab/ /ji ltar rgyal ba gdan la bzhugs snang ba/ /de bzhin rdul sbubs ma lus kun nang skye/ /'on kyang bde gshegs gshegs dang 'pho ba med/ /zhing rnams kun tu yul yang rab tu ston/ /sa yi tshul la
60b3(phal chen): 'jug pa tshad med de/ /spyod pa thub pas byang chub sems dpa' bstan/ /bsam gyis mi khyab tshul ni kun gsungs pas/ /rgyal sras rnams ni chos kyi dbyings la 'jug /chos kyi dbyings tshul rnam pa rgya cher
60b4(phal chen): ste/ /mtha' yas phyogs su mtha' dang dbus med sgo/ /rdul phran sbubs su rgyal ba 'phrul ba spros/ /'gro ba'i bsam pa kun kyang rab tu mkhyen/ /phyogs rnams thams cad zhing rnams kun tu yang / /'jig
60b5(phal chen): rten gtso mtshan 'gro dang mnyam par byung / /thams cad tshul sgor sangs rgyas don yod de/ /'dul bas sems can thams cad rnam par spyod/ /rdul sbubs kun tu mtha' dang dbus med pa'i/ /rnam 'phrul
60b6(phal chen): yangs pa rang byung shin tu ston/ /sngon chad thub pa'i byang chub spyod pa rnams/ /ci bzhin kun kyang snying po byang chub brjod/ /yangs dus bskal pa ji snyed yod pa'i rnams/ /skad cig skad cig sangs
60b7(phal chen): rgyas ma lus ston/ /der ni sems can 'byung zhing 'jig pa'ang bstan/ /'jig rten gtso bo ye shes mtha' yas ltos/ /'byam klas mi zad mtha' yas lo grangs pas/ /rgyal sras thams cad
60b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas de lta ste/ /thams cad sgor yang sangs rgyas mtha' dbus med/ /rgyal sras kun gyis shes par sla ba min/ /sangs rgyas mkha' 'dra rnam par mi rtog ste/ /chos nyid mi gnas chos kyi sprin dag gis/ /
61a1(phal chen): sprul pas spyod tshe kun tu rgyas mdzad cing / /shing mchog kun drung byang chub 'tshang rgya bstan/ /sangs rgyas gsung de rab tu brjod pas na/ /chos gnas thams cad ma lus brjod pa yin/ /'gro ba thams
61a2(phal chen): cad re re'i sgo dag nas/ /sangs rgyas chos rnams kun la rab tu 'jug /de la byang chub sems dpa' dge ba dri ma myed pa'i gzi brjid kyi 'od yid du 'ong ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du mngon
61a3(phal chen): par byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du 'gro ba'i rgyan byed pa zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' yon tan 'od mchog kun tu sgron ma'i rnam par thar pa ni/ sems skad cig gis mngon par
61a4(phal chen): rdzogs par byang chub pa'i sgo zad mi shes pa ston cing / chos ston gyi dbyings bsam gyis mi khyab pas yongs su smin pa dang rnam par 'dul bar byed pa'i 'od ces bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' kun tu 'bar ba
61a5(phal chen): seng ge'i rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi tshogs dang zhing yang dag par 'byung ba la rnam par lta ba zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' dpal gyi 'od zer
61a6(phal chen): kun tu 'od 'phro'i rnam par thar pa ni/ rdzu 'phrul gyi yul gyi rnam par spyod pa don yod pa zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' yon tan rgya mtsho kun tu sgra dbyangs rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi
61a7(phal chen): zhing gi rgyan thams cad 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du yang dag par ston pa zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul ye shes kun tu snang ba'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ de bzhin
61a8(phal chen): gshegs pa'i rjes su kun nas song zhing chos kyi dbyings la rnam par dpyod pa'i sprin chen po'i snying po zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' gtsug na rin chen kun tu rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/
61b1(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad kyi spyod pa la rab tu zhugs shing byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mtha' yas pa shin tu 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' rgyal ba'i gsung kun tu 'jam dbyangs kyi rnam par thar pa ni/
61b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad bsnyen bkur zhing mchod par nye bar 'gro ba'i snying po zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' bsod nams mi zad dri med kun tu gzi brjid kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ rdzu 'phrul dang rnam par 'phrul pa
61b3(phal chen): thams cad kyi byin gyis rlabs rgya chen po 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' mtshan gyi 'od zer kun tu snang ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku med pa las sangs rgyas kyi yul thams cad
61b4(phal chen): 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dge ba dri ma med pa'i gzi brjid kyi 'od yid du 'ong bas sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa rgya mtsho'i phyogs thams
61b5(phal chen): cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /ji snyed gang dag phyogs rnams kun gyi zhing / /rgyal bas de kun skad cig thugs kyi sbyangs/ /'gro ba kun tu zhi ba med pa'i gsung / /
61b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen bskor/ /skad cig thugs kyi chos dbyings kun bkang ste/ /mtha' yas spyod yul dbyings rnams rgyal ba ston/ /'gro ba kun lam snying po byang chub tu/ /byang chub 'tshang rgya rnam
61b7(phal chen): par 'phrul pa mdzad/ /bskal pa brgya phrag stong rnams tshad med du/ /de bzhin gshegs pas sngan chad spyod spyad de/ /nam mkha' 'dra bar byas nas rab bkye zhing / /sangs rgyas zhing 'di sngon tshe rab tu sbyangs/ /
61b8(phal chen): mtha' dang dbus med bskal par la la yi/ /skyo ba med par rgyal ba'i yul bsams kyang / /sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul stobs la dbus med pa/ /phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa kun tu 'gengs/ /rgyal ba'i rdzu 'phrul
62a1(phal chen): yul la rnam par ltos/ /phyogs bcu'i zhing rgyan de dag rnam dag pa/ /rgyal bas 'dir ni kun kyang rab tu bstan/ /skad cig skad cig sna tshogs gzugs kyang snang / /bskal pa brgya stong tshad med pa dag tu/ /
62a2(phal chen): rgyal ba'i ba spu gcig mtha' shes par dka'/ /tshul rnams kun sgor sangs rgyas chags pa med/ /'gro ba 'di na rgya chen bsam yas mdzes/ /sngon tshe'i bskal par rgyal bas 'gro kun tu/ /sangs rgyas rgya
62a3(phal chen): mtsho rgya chen bsnyen bkur bas/ /de bas 'jig rten gtso la chos dbyings rnams/ /kun nas mchod pa mang po rgya chen 'byung / /phyogs rnams bkang ste sangs rgyas 'byung ba dag /rdul gyi sbubs su tshad med zhing
62a4(phal chen): yang ston/ /de dag yul du mi zad mtha' yas pa'i/ /bskal pa rgya mtshor byin gyis rlob pa mdzad/ /sngon tshe'i bskal par rgyal bas 'gro don spyad/ /thugs rje'i rgya mtsho tshad med rab skyed cing / /'gro ba
62a5(phal chen): rgya mtsho kun nas 'khor ba yi/ /'khor rnams rgya mtsho mtha' yas kun kyang sbyangs/ /sangs rgyas mtshan med sku med rdul dang bral/ /de bzhin nyid gnas chos dbyings snying po ste/ /'gro ba kun na mtha' yas
62a6(phal chen): gzugs su snang / /'gro ba kun gyi sdug bsngal kun zhi mdzad/ /de la byang chub sems dpa' 'od zer rgya mtsho 'od ces dpal gyi zla ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ pha rol tu phyin pa dang sa'i shugs kyis sems can gyi
62a7(phal chen): khams kyi tshul dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa yang dag par 'byung ba zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' sprin dpa' po'i rgya mtsho dri med 'od kyi snying po'i rnam par thar pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa'
62a8(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems skad cig la chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul gyis khyim sna tshogs la rnam par lta ba zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' yon tan rin chen 'byung ba ye shes dpal gyi gtsug phud kyi rnam
62b1(phal chen): par thar pa ni/ skal pa bsam gyis mi khyab par 'gro ba rnams la mngon sum du yon tan dri ma med pas yongs su dag pa sgrub pa zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' rgya chen 'od 'bar blo gros dbang phyug gi rnam par
62b2(phal chen): thar pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi snying po byang chub tu thog ma 'gro ba'i ye shes kyi phyogs yang dag par 'byung ba'i rgyun ces bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' pad mo rnam par gnon pa 'od zer gtsug phud kyi
62b3(phal chen): rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad tha myi dad par 'gro ba thams cad kyi dbang po dang / mos pa rgya mtsho'i 'od ces bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' kun tu ye shes sprin gyi nyi ma'i rgyal mtshan snang ba'i
62b4(phal chen): rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas ye shes bsgrub par bskal pa mtha' yas pa dag tu byin gyis rlob cing rnam par spyod pa zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' mthu stobs brtson 'grus rdo rje yangs pa'i snying po'i
62b5(phal chen): rnam par thar pa ni/ chos thams cad kyi phyag rgya mtha' dang dbus med pa la yang dag par 'jug pa zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' spos kyi 'od 'phro shin tu 'bar ba'i 'od kyi rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/
62b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas da ltar byung ba thams cad kyi thog ma'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa shes pa'i dkyil 'khor yang dag par bsgrub pa zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnam par snang mdzad yon tan yangs pa'i rgyal mtshan
62b7(phal chen): gyi rnam par thar pa ni/ rnam par snang mdzad kyi smon lam rgya mtsho thams cad kyi dbyings la rab tu gnas pa zhes bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' bsod nams yangs pa shin tu 'phags pa'i 'od mchog yon tan
62b8(phal chen): 'byung ba'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi yul zab mo chos kyi dbyings thams cad la kun nas rab tu gnas pa rnam par spyod pa zhes bya'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'od zer rgya mtsho 'od chen
63a1(phal chen): dpal gyi zla bas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' rnam par phye ba rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /pha rol phyin pa rgya mtsho
63a2(phal chen): bsam yas dang / /sa yi dkyil 'khor rgya chen kun kyang yongs su rgyas/ /tshad med sems can rnam par 'dul ba'i tshe/ /sangs rgyas zhing yangs rnams kyang rnam par sbyangs/ /phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas zhing kun
63a3(phal chen): rgyas byas te/ /sangs rgyas sems can khams sbyin 'dul mdzad pa/ /skad cig thugs kyis chos kyi 'khor lo dag /mtha' yas 'gro mnyam bsam pa tshim par ston/ /bskal pa rgya che mi zad mu med par/ /
63a4(phal chen): rgyal ba 'gro la mngon sum kun nas bzhugs/ /mgon pos sngan cad ji ltar sbyangs tshul du/ /rgyal bas spyod yul rnam dag rab tu bstan/ /chos rgyal de dag ji ltar rnam 'phrul pa/ /phyogs rnams rgya mtsho ma lus
63a5(phal chen): kun na snang / /snying po byang chub kun na'ang rgyal ba dag /'khor gyis bskor cing chos rnams gsung ba snang / /'gro ba'i bsam pa thams cad tshim mdzad cing / /'jig rten dag na sangs rgyas tshul kun mdzes/ /
63a6(phal chen): dbang po ji bzhin chos kyi char yang 'bebs/ /sangs rgyas chos sku yangs pa rnam par mdzes/ /de bzhin nyid ltar mtshan nyid lus med de/ /rgyal ba dri med 'od gsal chos kyi sku/ /ye shes zhi ba'i sku ni tshad med de/ /
63a7(phal chen): phyogs dbyings kun bkang chos kyi char yang 'bebs/ /chos rje thams cad stobs kyis rnam par dag /bde gshegs ye shes mkha' 'dra mtha' yas te/ /rgya chen 'gro ba mtha' dbus myed bkang zhing / /
63a8(phal chen): rgyal ba stobs la 'jug pa rab tu ston/ /sangs rgyas 'od kyis chos dbyings kun bkang zhing / /sangs rgyas spyod pa thams cad rdzogs par bstan/ /rgyal bas sngon tshe ji ltar rnam sbyangs pas/ /de bzhin ye shes
63b1(phal chen): sa rnams rgyal bas bstan/ /phyogs rnams kun tu rang byung rnam par mdzes/ /smon lam rnam par 'phrul pa ma lus ston/ /ji ltar sngon tshe rgyal bas yongs sbyangs pa/ /rgyal ba'i 'od zer dra ba kun nas sgrog /
63b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas yul ni phyogs su zad pa med/ /dbus dang mtha' med gzhal med mtha' yas dbyings/ /chos dbyings kun tu chags med brnyes pa ni/ /sangs rgyas zhing rnams kun na shin tu mdzes/ /de'i tshe bcom
63b3(phal chen): ldan 'das kyi seng ge'i khri dang / pad mo'i ze ba'i dri thams cad dang / nor bu'i rgyal po thams cad kyis ngos dang / 'khor lo'i lte ba thams cad dang / me tog gi ze ba'i dri thams cad dang / stegs bu'i ngos thams
63b4(phal chen): cad dang / rta babs kyi sgo thams cad dang / nor bu'i gzugs kyi ngos thams cad dang / rin po che 'od 'phro ba'i sgo thams cad dang / 'od zer sgron ma'i sgo thams cad dang / seng ge'i khri'i rgyan gyi sgo thams cad nas/
63b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi byang chub sems dpa' mang po 'thon par 'gyur te/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho'i blo gros rnam par rol pa'i ye shes mngon par shes pa'i rgyal po zhes bya ba
63b6(phal chen): dang / byang chub sems dpa' sgra dbyangs kun tu sgrog pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' nor bu rin po che sna tshogs kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gtsug phud dang / byang chub sems dpa' ye shes chen po nyi ma yis rab tu
63b7(phal chen): gnon pa'i blo gros dang / byang chub sems dpa' yon tan rin po che bsam gyis mi khyab pa ye shes rgya mtsho'i dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' dmig rgya pa pad mo'i sna tshogs kyi gtsug phud dang / byang chub
63b8(phal chen): sems dpa' nam mkha'i tshul pad mo sna tshogs kyi gtsug phud dang / byang chub sems dpa' gser gyi 'od 'phro gzi brjid dkyil 'khor gyi 'od dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu sgra chos kyi dbyings kyi dbyings dang /
64a1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sprin yid du 'ong ba dri med pa'i zla ba dang / de dag la stsogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mchod pa'i sprin rnam pa sna tshogs rab tu 'gyed
64a2(phal chen): cing / 'di ltar nor bu rin po che'i me tog gi sprin thams cad ni rab tu 'byin/ spos kyi sprin thams cad ni shin tu 'gyed/ rin po che'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin thams cad ni mngon par 'byin/ yul mtha'
64a3(phal chen): yas pa'i spos kun tu 'phro ba'i bdug pa'i sprin ni/ rnam par 'gyed cing nor bu nyi ma'i snying po 'khor lo'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin ni rab tu gtong / sil snyan gyi sgra dbyangs yid du 'ong ba'i sprin ni rab tu sgrog /
64a4(phal chen): rin po che 'od 'phro ba kha dog mtha' yas pa'i sgron ma'i sprin gyis ni rab tu snang bar byed/ nor bu sna tshogs kyi shing gi yal ga las me tog gi kha dog ni rnam par spyod/ rin po che'i 'od dri ma med pa zad mi shes
64a5(phal chen): pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po'i char ni rab tu 'bebs/ rgyan mdzes pa thams cad yang dag par ston pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po'i sprin gyi char ni rab tu 'bebs shing / de lta bu dag la stsogs pa byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing
64a6(phal chen): yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi mchod pa'i sprin gyi char rab tu 'bebs pa byed cing lhags par gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te/ 'khor gyi
64a7(phal chen): dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho yod pa thams cad du mchod pa'i sprin rgyun mi 'chad pa'i char mngon par phab nas gang nas 'ongs pa'i phyogs su brten te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon du bltas nas seng ge'i khri rin po
64a8(phal chen): che sna tshogs du ma'i pad mo'i snying po can dag mngon par sprul te/ skyil mo krung bcas te 'khod par gyur to/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang spyod yul rgya mtsho cha chen po yongs su dag pa rnams so/ /
64b1(phal chen): sgo kun nas chos kyi snang ba rab tu thob pa rnams so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul chags pa med pa'i rjes su 'brang ba rnams so/ /tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa thams cad chos rgya mtsho la zhugs pa
64b2(phal chen): rnams so/ /rnam par thar pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i snang ba rab tu thob pa rnams so/ /sgo kun nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbyings rab tu thob pa rnams so/ /gzungs kyi sgo rgya mtsho thams cad kyis
64b3(phal chen): chos rgya mtsho rab tu 'dzin pa rnams so/ /dus gsum mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi sa la rab tu gnas pa rnams so/ /dga' ba'i shugs rgya chen po rab tu thob pa rnams so/ /bsod nams dkyil 'khor mu med pa
64b4(phal chen): yongs su dag pa'i rnams te/ chos kyi dbyings dang nam mkha' la rnam par rgyu zhing sangs rgyas thams cad mchod pa mngon par bsgrub pa la rab tu brtson pa sha stag go/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho'i blo gros
64b5(phal chen): rnam par rol pa'i ye shes mngon par shes pa'i rgyal pos sangs rgyas kyi mthus 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sangs rgyas
64b6(phal chen): rnam par sangs rgyas mnyam nyid mkhyen/ /chags med rnyed pas nam mkha' lta bu ste/ /phyogs rnams zhing kun rab tu snang byas nas/ /'byam klas 'khor na bzhugs pa rnam par mdzes/ /bde gshegs rang
64b7(phal chen): byung mtha' dang dbus med de/ /thams cad phyogs kyi chos dbyings kun rgyas par/ /dbang phyug chen po kun gyis mchod bskor cing / /shing gi rgyal po kun gyi drung na bzhugs/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdzu 'phrul
64b8(phal chen): stobs dag gis/ /skad cig sems la zad med yon tan gzugs/ /rnam thar gzhan dang gzhan dag thob pas mthong / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul ni mtha' yas so/ /bskal pa rgya mtshor sngon chad spyod
65a1(phal chen): pa'i tshe/ /de bzhin gshegs pas srid pa rgya mtshor 'dir/ /sna tshogs thabs kyis sems can smin byas pa/ /de dag rgyal ba de yi chos 'dzin to/ /yongs dag dri med 'khor rnams 'khod pa dag /
65a2(phal chen): thams cad sangs rgyas lta zhing rnam par gnas/ /pad mo'i snying po pad mo gdan bzhugs pa/ /tshogs kyi nang na rgyal ba mngon par mdzes/ /sangs rgyas gang na bzhugs pa'i seng ge'i khri/ /rin chen nor
65a3(phal chen): bu'i rgyal po'i 'od 'phro zhing / /spos 'phro sprin rnams mtha' yas rab tu 'byung / /snying po du ma'i me tog phreng spyangs pa'o/ /rin chen 'od 'phro'i sprin ni rtag tu 'gyed/ /'od zer sgron ma rgya chen rab tu 'bar/ /
65a4(phal chen): rta babs rnam pa sna tshogs rnams kyi brgyan/ /thub pa de bzhugs mngon par rab tu mdzes/ /sgra dbyangs yid du 'ong ba rab tu 'gyed/ /rin chen tshon du sna tshogs pad+mo 'phyang / /nor bu'i rgyal pos bskor
65a5(phal chen): rnams kang nas brgyan/ /sangs rgyas de bzhugs rnam par rab tu mdzes/ /zla gam rin chen mang pos yongs su bzung / /rdo rje 'od 'phro snang ba'i snying pos brgyan/ /gtsug na nor bu'i byang chub sems
65a6(phal chen): dpas bzung / /sangs rgyas de bzhugs rnam par shin tu mdzes/ /phyogs bcur sprul pa'i dra ba rab bkye zhing / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i smon lam sgra yang sgrog /gzugs brnyan bzhin du zhing rnams
65a7(phal chen): kun na snang / /thub pa de 'dra'i seng ge'i gdan la bzhugs/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' sgra dbyangs kun tu sgrogs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du yod pa thams cad la rnam
65a8(phal chen): par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /'di ni bde gshegs sangs rgyas byin rlabs te/ /byang chub spyod pa sngon chad spyad pa dang / /sangs rgyas mchod pa'i mchod pa du ma dag /
65b1(phal chen): rgyal ba'i gdan las de dag thams cad snang / /spos 'od snang ba nor bu'i rgyal po can/ /me tog snying po seng ge'i gdan gyi 'khor/ /rgyan rnams thams cad gzugs brnyan gyur pa dang / /'khor
65b2(phal chen): rnams de dag thams cad kun bkang ste/ /skad cig skad cig rgyan gyi kha dog kun/ /rnam pa du mar sangs rgyas gdan las snang / /sems can ji ltar mos pa de dag kyang / /'khod cing sangs rgyas tshad med
65b3(phal chen): gdan la lta/ /rin chen lda ldi pad mo mang btags pa/ /phyi zhing byang chub sems dpa' mang po rnams/ /sgra dbyangs yid du 'ong ba rab 'byin cing / /sangs rgyas gdan la bzhugs la stod pa byed/ /sangs
65b4(phal chen): rgyas bsod nams tshad med nam mkha' bzhin/ /'di dag rgyan kun de las rab tu byung / /sa rnams re re'i rgyan rnams gang yod pa/ /'gro ba kun gyis de dag bsam mi nus/ /mi phyed mtshams kyi rdo rje sna
65b5(phal chen): tshogs pa/ /'khor yangs rnam dag shin tu mnyam pa ste/ /nor bu'i dra ba sna tshogs kun tu bkram/ /byang chub shing gi sa yi 'khor kun to/ /sa phyogs gang na rgyal ba'i gdan yod pa/ /kha dog mtha'
65b6(phal chen): yas rgya chen sna tshogs ste/ /me tog mngon gtor rin chen rnam par bkram/ /gser mtshon mdzes pas de ni rab tu brgyan/ /sa yis lha mo de dag rab dga' zhing / /skad cig sems kyis mi zad sa yang ston/ /
65b7(phal chen): kun kyang rgyal ba'i zhal du mngon lta zhing / /kha dog thams cad rgyan gyi sprin gtong ngo / /rin chen sgron ma mang po gsal bar 'bar/ /spos mang dri zhim mang po rtag tu 'byung / /dus dang tshod kyi rnam pa mang ston cing / /
65b8(phal chen): lha rnams kun kyang sangs rgyas mchod pa byed/ /phyogs rnams bcu na zhing rnams ji snyed pa/ /de dag sa rgyan phun sum tshogs yod pa/ /de dag kun kyang sa dkyil 'di na snang / /sangs rgyas byin rlabs mnyam pa
66a1(phal chen): med pas phyung / /de nas byang chub sems dpa' nor bu rin po che sna tshogs kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gtsug phud kyis sangs rgyas kyi mthus 'od kyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas
66a2(phal chen): nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sngan cad spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe de dag /zhing kun phun sum tshogs pa mthong ba rnams/ /snying po byang chub 'khor gyi sa 'di la/ /myi zad sa dang de dag rab
66a3(phal chen): tu snang / /rnam par yangs pa gang na snang ba yi/ /sa la rin chen mdzes kun rnam par bkram/ /rin chen mang pos dkyil 'khor kun tu gtor/ /sangs rgyas 'od kyi sprin kyang rab tu snang / /sa rnams kun brgyan
66a4(phal chen): shing gi dam pa'i drung / /kun nas nor bu'i rgyal pos rgyan byas las/ /bsod nams 'od kyi dbyangs kyi 'brug sgra 'byung / /sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul tshul yang rab tu brjod/ /rin chen mang po sgron ma'i char
66a5(phal chen): phab cing / /rin chen mdzes par bkod pa rnam par mdzes/ /sgra dbyangs kun gyi 'brug sgra shin tu sgrog /sa yi lha rnams sa yang yang dag ston/ /rin chen 'od 'phro sgron ma rnam par snang / /'od zer sprin ni
66a6(phal chen): sa las rab tu 'byung / /nor bu dra ba sil ma kun nas bkram/ /rin chen sna tshogs rigs kyi yan lag brgyan/ /sa rnams kun nas mdzes pa 'di dag ltos/ /rin chen mang po tshon bzang brgyan tu bkye/ /'gro
66a7(phal chen): ba dag la chos kyi rgya mtsho sgrog / de dag chos nyid rnam par dag pa mthong / /ma lus phyogs na sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ /byang chub shing gi phun sum tshogs pa dag /sa yi dkyil 'khor 'di na kun snang ste/ /
66a8(phal chen): de dag chos nyid rnam par dag pa brjod/ /sangs rgyas gdan las chos rnams rgya mtsho yi/ /chos sgo bde bar gshegs pas gang gsungs pa/ /sems can kun gyi bsam pa ji bzhin du/ /sa 'khor rnams kyang
66b1(phal chen): kun nas rab tu 'byung / /dri zhim 'od rnams rtag tu 'byung bas na/ /de dag ji bzhin snod kyi 'gro ba 'gengs/ /srog chags rnams kyi nyon mongs zhi bar byed/ /sa 'khor de nas de 'dra rab tu sgrog /sangs
66b2(phal chen): rgyas rdzu 'phrul phun sum gang dag dang / /dri med sa ni gang gis mdzes gyur pa'i/ /phun sum tshogs pa'i rgyan rnams re re zhing / /bskal pa bye ba dag tu 'ang brjod myi nus/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa'
66b3(phal chen): ye shes chen po'i nyi mas rab tu gnon pa'i blo gros kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// //
66b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po lnga pa/ 'jig rten kun gyi bsam pa tshim mdzad cing / /sangs rgyas chos kyi gzhal med khang na mdzes/ /'byam
66b5(phal chen): klas phyogs rnams kun tu mngon sum du/ /sangs rgyas 'gro gtso gzhal med khang na snang / /rin chen kun gyi snying po rab tu brgyan/ /rgyan rnams kun gyis de bzhin mdzes shing 'bar/ /sangs rgyas pho brang 'od ni
66b6(phal chen): bsam myi khyab/ /de na bzhugs shing sangs rgyas rab tu mdzes/ /ka ba'i rgyan ni nor bu sna tshogs ste/ /phyogs rnams kun sgor rta babs sprin kyang bris/ /stegs bu'i phreng ba kun nas brgyan tu bkod/ /
66b7(phal chen): gser gyi dril bu'i sprin kyang rnam par rgyu/ /me tog bla re rnam par sna tshogs ltos/ /rin chen shing sdong dar gyi bla re bres/ /nor bu thams cad sgo nas phreng ba 'brul/ /de nas ye shes rgya mtshor rab tu mdzes/ /
66b8(phal chen): spos dri rgyal mtshan rin chen dra ba ste/ /'od zer sgron ma'i sprin gyis kun tu g.yogs/ /rgyan rnams sna tshogs kun nas shin tu bres/ /de na sangs rgyas rab tu 'phags pa bzhugs/ /phyogs rnams kun sgo
67a1(phal chen): sprul pa'i sprin gyi rnams/ /dbyangs kyis 'jig rten khyab par grag byed cing / /'byam klas phyogs kyi sems can rnam 'dul ba/ /sangs rgyas pho brang 'di na de dag grag /me tog shing dang rin
67a2(phal chen): chen spos bsngal ba/ /'phags pa phyogs rnams kun tu mngon par mdzes/ /de las dus gsum zhing rnams thams cad kyang / /gzugs brnyan gyur par de dag rab tu snang / /phyogs rnams kun tu rin chen mang
67a3(phal chen): bkye ba/ /de dag sna tshogs mdzes par rnam par 'bar/ /phyogs rnams kun tu skar kun mdzes par brgyan/ /rta babs mda' yab sna tshogs mang pos brgyan/ /dri med 'od zer kun nas snang ba yi/ /sangs rgyas
67a4(phal chen): pho brang rnam pa bsam yas te/ /gzhal med khang mang thams cad de la snang / /de dag kun na'ang rgyal ba bzhugs shing mdzes/ /phyogs rnams kun na 'khor rnams ji snyed pa/ /rgyal ba'i pho brang 'dir ni kun zhugs
67a5(phal chen): kyang / /mtha' med dbus myed mu'ang de bzhin du/ /rang byung sangs rgyas pho brang de na bzhugs/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' yon tan rin po che bsam gyis mi khyab pa ye shes rgya mtsho dpal gyis/ sangs rgyas
67a6(phal chen): kyi mthus/ 'khor 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho yod pa de dag thams cad la rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sangs rgyas zhing rdul shin tu phra snyed kyi/ /bsod nams rgya mtsho
67a7(phal chen): rnam par rab sbyangs te/ /sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul smon lam yang dag byung / /snying po byang chub dri med rnam par mdzes/ /spos zhim thams cad rtsa ba yang dag rgyu/ /yid bzhin nor mchog rgyal pos kun nas brgyan/ /rdo rje
67a8(phal chen): phye ma'i nor bu'i rgyal po bres/ /shing sdong rtsa ba rin chen kun las byas/ /rdo rje phye ma'i nor bu 'khor lo 'byung / /lhun rnams thams cad rin chen brgyan gyis brgyan/ /yal ga stug po sprin ltar kun nas 'khyil/ /
67b1(phal chen): snying po byang chub de na rgyal ba mdzes/ /yal ga dog pa kun nas mngon pa ste/ /'khor rnams snum 'jam phyogs rnams kun tu 'phags/ /me tog 'bras bu rin rnams kun kyang 'gyed/ /snying po byang chub rgya chen
67b2(phal chen): bsam myi khyab/ /'od rnams bkye ba phyogs su rnam par mdzes/ /dri ma med pa'i 'od 'bar zad mi shes/ /yal ga'i sgo nas sprin kun char yang 'bebs/ /snying po byang chub smon lam yangs pa byung / /me tog

67b5(phal chen): cad dag / byang chub shing la de dag kun nas snang / /de drung sangs rgyas dri med rnam par mdzes/ /yal ga kun nas rin chen mi zad nor/ /byang chub sems dpa' dag kyang rtag 'byung zhing / /bsod nams rgya chen
67b6(phal chen): dkyil 'khor char phab ste/ /phyogs bcur rgyal ba mchod phyir de dag 'dong / /de bzhin gshegs pa sngan cad cir gyur dang / /byang chub spyod las byung ba 'di dag ltos/ /yal ga kun nas rin chen nor mi zad/ /sangs rgyas
67b7(phal chen): yul kun bsam gyis myi khyab po/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' myig brgya pa pad mo sna tshogs kyi gtsug phud kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus 'khor rgya mtsho yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad
67b8(phal chen): pa 'di dag smras so/ /dus gsum gshegs pa'i rgyal ba'i rnam 'phrul ba/ /de dag rin chen sgo nas kun kyang grags/ /de ni mtha' dang dbus yang myed pa ste/ /snying po byang chub 'di la kun snang ngo / /me tog mang po'i phreng
68a1(phal chen): ba sbyangs bkye zhing / /'od zer sprin gyis phyogs rnams kun bkang ste/ /byang chub shing la gnas pa'i lha yi rnams/ /sangs rgyas blta zhing rtag tu mchod pa byed/ /spos kyi rgyal mtshan nor bu sna tshogs
68a2(phal chen): 'bar/ /spos kyi 'od 'phro bdug spos rtag tu 'byung / /'khor gyi rgya mtsho kun la khyab par zhim/ /shing gi rgyal po de phyir phyogs su mdzes/ /pad mo 'brul ba stug cing gser mdog 'dra/ /rgyal ba'i sprin
68a3(phal chen): sgra rtag par rab tu 'gyed/ /phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams ma lus khyab byas shing / /sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs gdung ba sel/ /rgyal ba'i 'khor ni tshad med rgya che ste/ /phyogs rnams kun nas snying po byang chub la/ /

68a5(phal chen): sngan cad du/ /rgyal ba'i spyod pa ji ltar byung ba ston/ /byang chub lha rnams zhing gi rdul snyed do/ /de dag thams cad snying po byang chub gnas/ /thub pa'i byang chub shing la skad cig cing / /rnam thar gzhan dang gzhan
68a6(phal chen): mang de dag ston/ /rang byung spyad pa thams cad spyod pa'i tshe/ /sngon chad de bzhin gshegs pa gang mchod pa/ /de dag mtshan bcas sngon gyi sbyor bcas pa/ /thams cad rin chen sgo nas rab tu 'byung / /phyogs bcu'i
68a7(phal chen): sems can ji snyed snod gyur pa/ /de dag thams cad 'di las sgra 'byung ste/ /de dag cis 'dul rnam dag ci 'dra ba'ang / /snying po byang chub 'di las kun brjod do/ /byang chub shing rnams mtha' yas phyogs kun na/ /bsam
68a8(phal chen): gyis myi khyab rgyan gyi sprin can dag / mtha' yas sna tshogs rgyan pa thams cad kyang / /sngon chad de bzhin gshegs pas yongs sbyangs pa'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' gser gyi 'od 'phro gzi brjid dkyil

80a3(phal chen): ba'i lte ba'i gdugs kyi sprin bcus nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / spos dang gdugs kyi sprin bcus nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / tsan dan gyi phye
80a4(phal chen): ma mang pos kun tu rgyas par 'gengs pa'i gdugs kyi sprin bcus nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul rgya chen po rnam par bstan pas kun tu brgyan gyis khyab
80a5(phal chen): par byed pa'i gdugs kyi sprin bcus nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / de dag la stsogs pa gdugs kyi sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi nam mkha'
80a6(phal chen): kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs par byed cing / bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der phyin te/ bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas lho dang nub kyi phyogs 'tshams su brten te/ seng ge'i khri
80a7(phal chen): in dra nI la yid du 'ong bar 'bar ba'i 'od zer gyi snying po can dag mngon par sprul nas skyil mo dkrung bcas te 'khod do/ /de nas yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'di dang 'dab chags su nub dang byang
80a8(phal chen): gi phyogs mtshams na 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'di rin po che'i 'od zer 'bar ba'i skar mda' 'od kyi snying po zhes bya ba yod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams bar ma'i rgyun de dag las 'jig rten
80b1(phal chen): gyi khams spos kyi rgyan yid du 'ong ba'i snying po na/ de bzhin gshegs pa yon tan rgya mtsho tshad med pa'i 'od bzhugs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho nas/ byang chub sems dpa' 'od zer dang gzi

80b4(phal chen): nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / me tog gi sprin gyis rnam par snang bar byas pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin gyi nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / 'od zer gyi sgo nas sangs
80b5(phal chen): rgyas sprul pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin bcus nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlab pa dang / phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gzugs brnyan gyi khongs su chud pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor

80b8(phal chen): sems can mtha' yas pa'i gzugs yongs su ston pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin bcus nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi smon lam 'byung
81a1(phal chen): ba'i sgra yid du 'ong ba rab tu gtong ba'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin bcus nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du sems can 'dul

81b8(phal chen): pa 'di dang 'dab chags su steng gi phyogs na 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho nor bu rin po che sna tshogs kyi 'od rgya mtsho'i rgyan ces bya ba yod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams bar ma'i rgyud de dag las
82a1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams mtshan yid du 'ong ba rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba na/ de bzhin gshegs pa yon tan dang grags pa thogs pa med pa'i rnam par thar pa rab tu snang ba'i rgyal po bzhugs
82a2(phal chen): pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho nas/ byang chub sems dpa' stobs dang brtson 'grus chags pa med pa'i blo gros shes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul

83a1(phal chen): gyur to/ /rin po che re re'i sgo nas kyang byang chub sems dpa' seng ge'i khri pad mo'i snying po can la 'khod pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu byung bar
