85b2(phal chen): dpa' kun tu bzang po'i 'khor dag tu dga' bar phrad par byas nas/ bcom ldan 'das la g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar pad+mo chen po chu bo rin po che thams cad
85b3(phal chen): las bsgrubs pa/ nang rim nor bu'i rgyal po'i mdzod sna tshogs las byas pa lo ma rin po che thams cad kyi rigs kyi char 'beb pa/ ze ba'i phreng ba'i rgyan spos rin po che thams cad las byas pa/ snying
85b4(phal chen): po'i 'dzam bu chu klung gser gyi tshon gyis rab tu mdzes par bris pa/ 'od kyi 'khor rnam par dag cing 'od zer gyi dra bas rnam par snang bar byas pa'i sprin dang ldan pa/ rgyan thams cad rab tu 'byung ba sems
85b5(phal chen): kyi skad cig la sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' yas ston pa'i sgra rab tu 'byung ba/ nor bu'i rgyal po mtha' yas pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku'i gzugs brnyan gyi sprin gyis thams cad du gang bar byed
85b6(phal chen): pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / smon lam thams cad rab tu ston pa'i dbyangs 'byin par gyur te byung ngo / /pad mo mtha' yas chen po byung ba'i rjes su byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad la
85b7(phal chen): pham pa med pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu bcom ldan 'das kyi mdzod spu de nyid nas byung ste/ bcom ldan 'das
85b8(phal chen): la lan du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal te/ pad+mo chen po de'i snying po la 'jug go/ /byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul
86a1(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed po de dag la 'khod do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad la pham pa med pa'i dbyings chos kyi dbyings rgya che zhing tshad med pas rab tu dga' ba'i shugs shin tu
86a2(phal chen): skyes pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyod yul gyi rjes su song ba'i ye shes can/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi sku rgya mtsho bsam gyis myi khyab pa la rab tu zhugs pa'i mthu dang ldan pa zhing 'byam
86a3(phal chen): klas pa thams cad kyi de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi zhabs kyi drung du phyin pa dang / ba spu thams cad las sprul pa'i sprin zad mi shes pas kun tu khebs par byed pa/ sems kyi skad cig thams cad
86a4(phal chen): la dmigs pa/ thams cad chos kyi dbyings thams cad la dus gsum khyab par byed pa'i spyod yul gyis rnam par spyod pa/ phyogs thams cad kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs 'chang ba/
86a5(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin thams cad la rab tu 'jog cing phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thugs par ting nge 'dzin dang / rnam par thar pa la rnam par spyod pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa
86a6(phal chen): thams cad dang chos kyi dbyings kyi lus dang ldan pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' dang dbus med pa la rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag
86a7(phal chen): smras so/ /sangs rgyas kun ni chos kyi dbyings kyis gsal/ /'gro ba kun la rgyal ba mngon sum ste/ /ji ltar mos pa'i sems can rgyas bkang nas/ /snying po byang chub de la rgyal ba bzhugs/ /
86a8(phal chen): zhing rnams kun gyi rdul phran mchog snyed kyi/ /rgyal ba spu rtse kun la rab bzhugs te/ /byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyis kun nas bskor/ /kun kyang bzang po'i spyod pa mchog ston to/ /
86b1(phal chen): spu gcig rtse la zhing mang rgya mtsho ste/ /byang chub snying po pad mo'i gdan la bzhugs/ /chos dbyings rgya chen thams cad kun bkang ste/ /spu rnams kun la rnam par 'phrul ba ston/ /zhing rnams
86b2(phal chen): re re dag na rab bzhugs shing / /zhing rnams 'byam klas kun tu rgyas mdzad pas/ /phyogs bcu'i byang chub sems dpa'i sprin gyi rnams/ /kun kyang snying po byang chub drung du 'dong / /zhing rnams
86b3(phal chen): kun gyi rdul phran mchog snyed kyi/ /byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan rgya mtsho'i 'od/ /sangs rgyas kyi ni 'khor du nye bar 'dong / /chos dbyings 'byam klas rtag tu rgyas par 'gengs/ /zhing
86b4(phal chen): rnams thams cad gzugs brnyan rab tu ston/ /chos dbyings rdul rnams ye shes spyod yul can/ /kun kyang bzang po'i spyod la rab tu gnas/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi 'khor du yang dag byung / /byang
86b5(phal chen): chub sems dpa' ye shes mchog yul can/ /sangs rgyas chos sprin nyan cing rab tu mkhas/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi 'khor rnams kun na gnas/ /zhing rnams kun tu bskal pa rgya mtshor spyod/ /
86b6(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i chos la rnam par snang bar spyod/ /de dag rgyal ba'i sa rnams rgya mtshor bzhugs/ /sangs rgyas chos rnams gzhan dang gzhan byung ba/ /de dag smon lam rgya mtshor rab tu 'jug /
86b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas yon tan legs pa rgya mtsho dang / /kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa de dag shes/ /sangs rgyas chos kyi dbyings rnams kun bkang zhing / /de dag rnam 'phrul rgya chen kun la zhugs/ /zhing
86b8(phal chen): rnams kun gyi rdul phran mang snyed kyi/ /lus kyi sprin ni rtag par rab tu ston/ /sems can kun bkang 'od kyis kun la skyob/ /bsam pa yid bzhin chos kyi char yang 'bebs/ /de nas byang chub sems
87a1(phal chen): dpa' chos kyi dpal pad mo rnam par lta ba'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /
87a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas ye shes shin tu zab/ /dus rnams kun tu de 'byung ste/ /chos dbyings thugs su chud pas na/ /'jig rten mgon zhes rab tu brjod/ /yang dag sangs rgyas chos kyi sku/ /'dres pa med
87a3(phal chen): cing gnas pa med/ /sems can thams cad yid bzhin du/ /gzugs kyi skur yang rab tu mthong / /chos rnams thams cad mngon sangs rgyas/ /chos rnams kun la rab tu zhugs/ /thams cad
87a4(phal chen): mkhyen pa thams cad gzigs/ /zhing rnams kun na rnam par mdzes/ /kha dog bsam gyis mi khyab par/ /sems can thams cad yid bzhin du/ /sems can mchog gi 'od rnams dang / /
87a5(phal chen): de bzhin sku yi sprin kyang mthong / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dag las/ /mi zad sangs rgyas sprul pa rnams/ /zhing rnams kun tu rab sgrog cing / /chos kyi rgya mtsho shin tu ston/ /spu rnams re re kun
87a6(phal chen): nas kyang / /phyogs bcur 'od zer dra ba dag /sangs rgyas gsung ni rab 'byin cing / /gdul dka' thams cad rnam par 'dul/ /sangs rgyas 'od zer sgra rnams nas/ /sgra dbyangs zab mo rtag tu 'byung / /
87a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas yon tan rgya mtsho ni/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod yul lo/ /sangs rgyas chos kyi 'khor lo dag /mtha' dang dbus med rab tu bskor/ /ye shes zab mo shes bya ba/ /rgya che phyogs su rab tu
87a8(phal chen): ston/ /'jig rten khams rnams thams cad du/ /rnam par 'phrul pa gzhan dang gzhan/ /chos kyi dbyings rnams kun bkang zhing / /yang dag sangs rgyas ston pa mdzad/ /sku rnams re re kun nas
87b1(phal chen): kyang / /zhing rnams kun gyi rdul mnyam par/ /sangs rgyas sems can mnyam phyung zhing / /rnam par 'phrul pa rab tu ston/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi rgya mtsho rnam par
87b2(phal chen): snang ba'i blo gros kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /chos kyi dbyings rnams kun khyab par/ /sangs rgyas sku
87b3(phal chen): ni rnam par mdzes/ /rgya chen gsung ni rang byung ba/ /zhing rnams rgya mtshor shin tu sgrog /'jig rten thams cad kun 'jug par/ /'jig rten mgon po shin tu mdzes/ /'gro ba kun gyi
87b4(phal chen): bsam mkhyen cing / /byin gyis brlabs ni rab tu ston/ /sangs rgyas 'jig rten kun la mngon/ /sems can thams cad bsam pa bzhin/ /thams cad gzigs pa sangs rgyas kyi/ /rnam par
87b5(phal chen): 'phrul pa thams cad mthong / /mtha' yas 'od mnga' sangs rgyas sprin/ /chos rnams rgya mtsho'i 'brug kyang sgrog /ye shes rnam rgyu'i tshul bzhin du/ /rgyal ba'i sras rnams de la 'jug /'jug
87b6(phal chen): pa rnams la 'byung ba med/ /'byung ba yod pa rnam par bstan/ /gang la sangs rgyas bzhugs pa yi/ /chos rnams 'byung ba nam mkha' bzhin/ /'pho dang gnas pa mi mnga' ste/ /'on kyang rgyal ba
87b7(phal chen): kun na snang / /sangs rgyas chos kyi dbyings las byung / /de phyir sangs rgyas rab tu brjod/ /yul na bzhugs med rang bzhin med/ /de la 'byung ba mi mnga' ste/ /sku dang mtshan kyang de bzhin med/ /rgyal
87b8(phal chen): ba'i gzugs brnyan 'dra ba'o/ /'gro ba kun tu chos kyi sprin/ /bsam pa kun la rab tu byung / /yang dag sangs rgyas rnams kun tu/ /sems can rgya mtsho 'dul ba mdzad/ /'jig rten
88a1(phal chen): khams rnams thams cad kyi/ /snying po byang chub kun na snang / /'khod pa'i rgya mtsho thams cad na/ /zhing rnams kun gyis rnam par mdzes/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi sku dag la/ /yon tan rgya
88a2(phal chen): mtsho zad mi shes/ /sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas te/ /de dag yon tan zad pa med/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' spos 'od 'phro ba'i rgyan zla ba'i 'od kyis sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyi phyogs
88a3(phal chen): bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /bsam gyis myi khyab sangs rgyas sar/ /byang chub sems dpa' gang bzhugs pa/ /de dang de dag sangs rgyas kyi/ /sangs
88a4(phal chen): rgyas rnam 'phrul thams cad mthong / /ye shes lus kyi zhugs pa rnams/ /zhing kun rdul gyi sbubasu yang / /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / /bdag nyid lus kyang der mthong ngo / /gzugs
88a5(phal chen): brnyan zhing rnams thams cad dang / /sangs rgyas kun gyi spyan sngar 'byung / /kun tu byin gyis rlabs rnams dang / /rnam par 'phrul pa rab tu ston/ /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang / /spyod pa gang gis rnam
88a6(phal chen): sbyangs pa/ /de dag zhing rnams thams cad du/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi rnam 'phrul mthong / /kun tu lung mnyam nyid gyur cing / /kun tu lus kyis rab gnas te/ /ye shes kun gyi rjes song na/ /sangs rgyas
88a7(phal chen): spyod yul bzhugs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas ye shes zhugs pa rnams/ /chos kyi dbyings la rnam par mdzes/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi spu dag tu/ /rgya mtsho'i zhing la rab tu 'jug /sangs rgyas kun gyi zhing
88a8(phal chen): dag tu/ /byin gyis brlabs rnams rab bstan pas/ /gzhan dang gzhan gyi lus ngag dang / /ming gis kun na rab tu gnas/ /byang chub snying por rnam 'phrul dang / /byang chub mngon par 'tshang rgya zhing / /
88b1(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dag /skad cig sems kyis ston pa byed/ /zhing rnams 'byam klas thams cad dang / /bskal pa bye ba bsam yas dag /byang chub sems dpa' mnyam
88b2(phal chen): bzhag rnams/ /skad cig sems kyi rnam par ston/ /sangs rgyas zhing rnams thams cad na/ /byang chub sems dpa'i sprul pa rnams/ /sangs rgyas sku la rnam spyod kyang / /mtha' ma rnyed par myi rung ngo /
88b3(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' seng ge 'od zer snang ba'i mthus 'byin pa'i blo gros kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag
88b4(phal chen): smras so/ /sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad kyi/ /chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor/ /chos dbyings tshul rnams thams cad kyang / /sangs rgyas sprin gyis mngon du yog /'jig rten khams rnams
88b5(phal chen): rgya mtsho dag / phyogs bcu kun na gang yod pa/ /thams cad kun tu 'khor lo 'khor/ /de ni smon lam rnam par 'phrul pa'o/ /'khor rnams rgya mtsho rgya che ba/ /gzhan dang gzhan gyi ming dag gis/ /
88b6(phal chen): zhing rnams gnas pa kun tu yang / /chos kyi 'khor lo kun tu 'khor/ /rnam par snang mdzad byin gyis rlabs/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun tu yang / /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dag /brjod cing zhing
88b7(phal chen): rnams kun tu 'byung / /zhing kun rdul la sku yi rnams/ /thams cad chos rab rab tu 'bebs/ /'dres pa med cing 'byung ba med/ /'jig rten dag na rnam par mdzes/ /bskal pa bye ba grangs med
88b8(phal chen): par/ /zhing kun rdul phran sbubs dag du/ /rnam par snang ba mdzad pa'i gsung / /sngon gyi spyod pa rab tu sgrog /zhing rnams thams cad rdul snyed kyi/ /'od zer dra ba phyogs bcu na/ /sangs rgyas 'od zer
89a1(phal chen): kun sgo nas/ /byang chub mchog phyir sems can 'dul/ /kun tu ma 'dres sku dag gis/ /chos dbyings yongs su rab gsal te/ /'gro rnams 'dul ba ji bzhin du/ /gzugs kyi sku yang
89a2(phal chen): rab tu mthong / /dus gsum zhing rnams thams cad kyi/ /mgon po ji snyed bzhugs pa rnams/ /de dag kun gyi mtshan kyang sgrog /sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul la ltos/ /da ltar byung dang 'das pa dang /
89a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas gang rnams ma byon pa/ /de dag kun gyi bsam yas pa/ /chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu grag /de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi yon tan gyi mdzod mi zad pa'i dpal gyi gzi brjid mar mas
89a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /gang gis byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /ye shes tshogs 'di kun non cing / /
89a5(phal chen): ye shes rtogs pa rnyed pa rnams/ /de dag 'di yi tshul la zhugs/ /chos kyi dbyings dang mnyam pa'i dbyangs/ /zhing rnams kun tu rab tu 'byung / /sangs rgyas kun gyi spyod yul te/ /byang chub sems
89a6(phal chen): dpa'i ched du brjod/ /skad cig re re'i sems kun la/ /chos kyi dbyings su rnam par rgyu/ /de bzhin nyid la gnas shing rten/ /chos rnams rgya mtsho kun la zhugs/ /rgyan gyi pha rol phyin pa rnams/ /
89a7(phal chen): bskal pa bye ba bsam yas su/ /sangs rgyas thams cad sku dag dang / /zhing rnams kun na gnas shing spyod/ /rdul rnams re re'i steng nas kyang / /chos rnams kun ni rab tu 'byung / /zhing rnams kun
89a8(phal chen): kyang khyab par byed/ /ye shes chags med spyod yul lo/ /sangs rgyas thams cad spyod yul du/ /las la med par kun bkang zhing / /rnam par 'phrul pa'i rnam spyod pas/ /sangs rgyas spyod yul
89b1(phal chen): rnams la zhugs/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi rjes snyegs dbyangs/ /chos kyi dbyings ni rab sgrog pa/ /chos dbyings rjes su shes pa rnams/ /dbyangs kyi rgya mtsho rnams la spyod/ /bskal pa rgya mtshor
89b2(phal chen): ma 'dres par/ /sgra dang dbyangs rnams shin tu sgrog /dus rnams thams cad shes pas gsal/ /dbyangs kyi de dag sa la zhugs/ /sgra yi shes la rmongs pa myed/ /sems can sgra yang spyod yul te/
89b3(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa kun gyi yang / /rnam par 'phrul pa'i dbyangs shes so/ /sa nas sar yang phyin gyur cing / /stobs kyi sa la rab gnas te/ /bskal pa bye bar sbyangs pas na/ /chos nyid 'di
89b4(phal chen): la rab tu 'jug / de nas byang chub sems dpa' ye shes kyi 'od zer shes rab kun nas sgron ma'i blo gros kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su
89b5(phal chen): bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /gang la sangs rgyas bzhugs pa yi/ /chos rnams de dag mtshan nyid myed/ /ye shes sa ni thob pa rnams/ /'jig rten gtso bo rab tu mthong / /shes rab snang ba'i kun 'od
89b6(phal chen): can/ /byang chub sems dpa' mnyam bzhag rnams/ /sangs rgyas thams cad kun gyi yang / /sku yi rnam par 'phrul la zhugs/ /chos kyi dbyings la rnam spyad cing / /lus kyi dngos la rab 'jug ste/ /
89b7(phal chen): zab mo'i chos rnams rtogs gyur nas/ /smon lam dag gis yang dag byung / /bsod nams rgya mtshos byung gyur cing / /ye shes sa la rnam par gnas/ /chos la rnam spyod khong du chud/ /spyod pa'i
89b8(phal chen): mchog la rab tu spyod/ /sangs rgyas zhing rnams thams cad kyi/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi drung dag tu/ /chos kyi dbyings la spyad pas na/ /rang bzhin lus ni rab tu mthong / /zhing rnams 'byam klas thams cad du/ /
90a1(phal chen): bskal pa bye ba bsam yas su/ /thams cad gzigs pa'i chos kyi rnams/ /rgya mtsho kun la rab tu spyod/ /bdag mthong bas ni lus dang rdul/ /gcig tu 'dres pa mngon par byas/ /ma skyes
90a2(phal chen): mtshan nyid med pa ste/ /zhing rnams kun tu'ang rnam par mdzes/ /'jig rten kun gyi bsam mthun par/ /sems can kun la mngon sum du/ /lus kyi sprin ni bstan byas shing / /byang chub don du
90a3(phal chen): sems can 'dul/ /sangs rgyas thams cad mthu yis ni/ /byang chub sems dpa' brjod pa ste/ /gang gis mgon po mthong ba yi/ /rgyal ba'i byin brlabs shin tu zab/ /mgon po ji snyed
90a4(phal chen): gang bzhugs pa'i/ /byin rlabs mtha' dang dbus med de/ /chos dbyings rab tu gang byas nas/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnam 'tshang rgya/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' me tog kun nas 'od 'phro
90a5(phal chen): gtsug phud rab tu 'phyang bas/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /zhing rnams kun tu sangs rgyas kyi/ /gsung gi
90a6(phal chen): dkyil 'khor sgra 'byin te/ /chos kyi dbyings rnams gang byas nas/ /yon tan sprin ni rab tu brjod/ /yang dag sangs rgyas chos kyi sku/ /rnam par nam mkha' 'dra ba ste/ /gzugs kyi sku yang rab ston
90a7(phal chen): cing / /chos nyid 'di la shin tu 'jug /dga' dang mos pa'i shugs rnams dang / /sangs rgyas stobs rnams thams cad la/ /rab tu gnas shing de dag ni/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes 'jug /shes
90a8(phal chen): rab chung ngus chos 'di dag / kun nas shes par mi nus te/ /ye shes mig ni rnam sbyangs shing / /'di yi tshul la 'jug par 'gyur/ /rab tu gnas dang byin rlabs dang / /chos kun rnam par spyad pa dang / /
90b1(phal chen): rab tu 'jug dang ldang ba yi/ /mnyam pa nyid la rab tu zhugs/ /chos rnams mtha' yas klong gi rnams/ /chos kun mtshan nyid rnams la ste/ /kun mkhyen nyid la rab zhugs shing / /chos
90b2(phal chen): kyi rgya mtsho kun la spyod/ /sangs rgyas zhing na kun 'khod cing / /thams cad kun na rnam par mdzes/ /'ongs pa med cing 'phos pa med/ /sangs rgyas chos nyid de 'dra 'o/ /gzugs brnyan
90b3(phal chen): 'dra ba'i sku rnams ni/ /sems can rgya mtsho'i nang na snang / /mos pa ci 'dra yod pa rnams/ /de bzhin mgon po kun gyis mthong / /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang / /spyod pa mang po sus
90b4(phal chen): sbyangs pa/ /de dag thams cad ba spu la'ang / /rnam 'phrul gzhan dang gzhan dag mthong / /lus kyi rnams ni re res kyang / /chos kyi dbyings rnams kun tu khyab/ /'khor lo kun na 'khor
90b5(phal chen): ba ste/ /chos kyi 'khor lo bsam mi khyab/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'od zer dang gzi brjid mi zad pa'i rgyal po'i blo gros kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam
90b6(phal chen): par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sangs rgyas sku ni thams cad nas/ /'od zer sprin mang phyogs rnams bcur/ /kha dog mtha' yas 'bar ba'i 'od/ /sems
90b7(phal chen): can rnam pa kun la 'phro/ /sangs rgyas zhing rnams thams cad kyi/ /snying po byang chub kun na bzhugs/ /bdud rnams thams cad rab btul te/ /'khor gyi nang na rnam par mdzes/ /thams cad
90b8(phal chen): rdul na'ang ma 'dres par/ /'od zer dkyil 'khor rgyas par 'gengs/ /phyogs rnams gzhan dang gzhan lam du/ /zhing gi rgyud rnams rab tu ston/ /zhing gi rnams ni rgya mtsho'i klong / /phyogs kyi
91a1(phal chen): rnams kyang kun tu gnon/ /zhing rnams thang chen mnyam zhing dag /in dra ni lar kun nas gnas/ /spyi'u tshugs dag dang snrel gzhi dang / /pad+mo'i dbyibs dang khyud khyud dang / /
91a2(phal chen): dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i khyad par du/ /gzugs rnams kun gyis rab tu gnas/ /chos kyi dbyings rnams gar phyin par/ /thub pa myed par gram bdal ba/ /de dag kun gyi 'khor rnams su/ /
91a3(phal chen): shin tu bstan pa'i chos 'byung ngo / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dbyings na/ /'khod pa'i zhing rnams bsam myi khyab/ /de dag kun tu chos nyid 'di/ /'jig rten mgon po rnams kyang ston/ /tha dad
91a4(phal chen): med pa'i chos kyi dbyings/ /chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu 'khor/ /tshig gi tshul gyi rnam pa yis/ /chos bstan pa ni kun tu 'byung / /sangs rgyas gsung gi dkyil 'khor ni/ /tshul rnams bsam
91a5(phal chen): cing rab tu brjod/ /dad pa rgya mtsho'i tshul dag gis/ /mi zad tshul rnams rab tu bstan/ /sangs rgyas zhing rnams kun na yang / /rgyal ba rnams ni myig yor 'dra/ /snying po byang chub rnams na snang / /

91a7(phal chen): par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /blta zhing blta zhing sangs rgyas rnams/ /sku gzugs bsam gyis myi khyab ste/ /dga' ba rgya mtsho kun kyang 'byung / /chos kyi shugs ni
91a8(phal chen): rab tu 'phel/ /mtshan rab kun nas sangs rgyas rnams/ /phyogs bcu kun tu rab tu 'byung / /rdul rnams kun tu 'jug pa yi/ /sangs rgyas sprin kyang de bzhin bstan/ /skad cig skad cig sems

91b2(phal chen): rnams/ /sangs rgyas kun gyis byin rlabs pa/ /'di yi yul la rnam par spyod/ /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam la/ /gang rnams shin tu gnas gyur pa/ /de dang de rnams zhing dag du/ /sangs
91b3(phal chen): rgyas rnam 'phrul kun la blta/ /ye shes zab mo rnam gnon cing / /chos kyi dbyings la gzhol ba ni/ /mos pa rgya mtsho shes pa ste/ /smon lam kun gyis byung ba'o/ /sangs rgyas kun
91b4(phal chen): gyi sku dang gsung / /chags pa med la rab tu zhugs/ /spyod pa gzhan dang gzhan dag gis/ /spyod yul kun kyang khong du chud/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi sku gnas shing / /ye shes spyod yul gyur pa
91b5(phal chen): rnams/ /chos kyi dbyings la rab brtson pa/ /rgyal ba rnams kyi sa gnon to/ /skad cig sems kyis zhing gi rnams/ /sangs rgyas zhing gi rdul mnyam pa/ /de dag chos nyid ji bzhin du/ /rdul cig
91b6(phal chen): steng du rnam par spyod/ /zhing rnams ji snyed thams cad ni/ /zhing gi rnam 'phrul gang yod pa/ /chos nyid 'di la zhugs pa rnams/ /zhing cig tu ni sdud pa byed/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' stobs
91b7(phal chen): dang brtson 'grus chags pa myed pa'i blo gros kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcud pa 'di dag smras so/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho
91b8(phal chen): thams cad du/ /de dag gsung ni zab mo byung / /dbyangs kyi yan lag kun rgyas pa/ /chos kyi sprin gyi char 'bebs so/ /brjod pa rgya mtsho thams cad kyi/ /sems can kun gyi skad dag tu/ /sangs
92a1(phal chen): rgyas zhing rnams kun tu yang / /chos rnams bstan pa rab tu 'byung / /zhing rnams kun tu ma lus par/ /sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul mthong zhing / /sangs rgyas gsung rnams thos pa

92a3(phal chen): byed/ /chos kyi sku ni tha dad min/ /nam mkha' bzhin te chags pa med/ /gzugs kyi skur ni rnam dmyigs pa/ /mig yor snang ba'i mtshan nyid do/ /myig yor yul la mi gnas ste/ /nam mkha'
92a4(phal chen): bzhin du dngos po myed/ /mnyam pa nyid 'di rtogs gyur nas/ /ye shes rgya mtsho mthong bar gyur/ /sangs rgyas sku ni ma skyes te/ /gzung ba med cing 'byung ba myed/ /nam mkha' mnyam pa nyid dang

92b5(phal chen): dbyings kyi gzugs brnyan rnam par brtags pa'i tshogs/ nam mkha'i dbyings na brdal ba med cing rgya che ba khyab par byed pa'i rang bzhin chos kyi dbyings rgya mtsho'i klong mnyam pa nyid kyi rjesu song zhing shin

92b7(phal chen): yog par byas pa'i rang bzhin gyi snying po can dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i ye shes snang ba/ rgya mtsho'i klong phyogs thams cad du sgo kun nas tshul rgya mtsho rnam par rig par bya bas mngon tu yang dag
92b8(phal chen): par ston pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi stobs dang rnam par thar pas byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi lus rgyas par 'gengs pa'i snying po can/ zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par chos kyi dbyingasu
93a1(phal chen): 'jug pas rgyas par 'gengs pa'i ye shes dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su grub par byed pa bskal pa thams cad du smon lam rgya mtshos rnam par snang bar byed

93a4(phal chen): gyi khams 'byam klas pa chos kyi dbyings kyi klas pa namakha'i dbyings kyi mthas btugs pa/ phyogs rgya mtsho thams cad kyi khongasu gtogs pa/ dus gsum thams cad na yod pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byung
93a5(phal chen): ba'i khams chos kyi dbyings rgya chen pos non pa'i risu gtogs pa shin tu phra zhing sgrib pa myed pa mang ba dang / phyogs rgya chen po rgya mtsho thams cad snang ba 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i ris su gtogs

93a7(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings kyi rdul ma lus pa kun tu gtogs pa/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du rgyas par gang ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba dang mnyam pa dag tu rdul phra mo re re la'ang /
93a8(phal chen): zhing 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la rab tu zhugs nas zhing re re zhing yang de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la rab tu zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa

93b4(phal chen): 'das de dag gis 'di skad ces kyang bka' bstsal to/ rigs kyi bu khyod de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i snying po 'di la
93b5(phal chen): mnyam par gzhog pa la legaso legaso/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras khyod la phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa 'di dag thams cad kyang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par
93b6(phal chen): snang mdzad 'di'i sngon gyi smon lam gyi byin gyis rlabs dang / khyod kyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi smon lam dang / spyod pa yongs su dag pa'i mthus 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor

93b8(phal chen): thams cad kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba dang / chags pa med par 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad yongs su gnan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul thams cad
94a1(phal chen): la chags pa myed par 'jug par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi 'khor thams cad sgo kun nas rab tu brjod pa dang / chos tshul gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la zhugs pas/ thams cad mkhyen
94a2(phal chen): pa nyid yongasu bzung ba dang / chos kyi snang ba thams cad kyi tshul rnam par lta ba dang / sems can gyi dbang po rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su shes par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi yan

94b4(phal chen): mdzes par brgyan pa/ 'od zer gyi dra ba'i me tog sna tshogs shin tu rgyas pa/ 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa'i sprin 'gyed pa/ rin po che 'od 'phro ba thams cad kyi sprin gyi rnam par gsal bar gyur pa/

94b6(phal chen): 'phrul pa dang / khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba yang dag par ston pa/ byang chub sems dpa' 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyi kun tu bzang po'i smon lam gyi dkyil 'khor rab tu snang ba rnam par

95a1(phal chen): dag tu byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyi bo la phyag rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams rab tu bzhag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis/ reg
95a2(phal chen): ma thag tu don de'i mod la ting nge 'dzin de las ldang ba'i sgo rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed/ dus gsum thams cad du sems kyi skad cig re re la/ ting nge 'dzin las ldang ba'i

95a4(phal chen): thams cad kyi sgo dang / sems can ma lus pa'i gnas thams cad dang / mnyam zhing sems can thams cad kyi sems rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i sgo dang / sems can thams cad kyi lus dang / ming gi 'khor lo las
95a5(phal chen): ldang ba'i sgo dang / phyogs dang mtshams thams cad du chos kyi dbyings rnam par 'byed pa'i sgo dang / rdul shin tu phra ba thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi sku'i sprin mtha' dang dbus myed par 'byam klas pa'i sgo dang /

95a7(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la rab tu zhugs par gyur to/ /gzungs rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la yang rab tu

95b5(phal chen): nas 'pho ba dang 'byung ba dang / byang chub tu rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa bstan pa rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la yang rab tu zhugs par gyur to/ /
95b6(phal chen): 'dir ji lta ba de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i thams cad na yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gyi 'khor rgya mtsho rnams dang / rdul shin tu phra ba thams cad kyi khongs na yod pa kun tu yang byang
95b7(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho rnams rab tu zhugs par gyur te/ sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i ting nge 'dzin gyi chos nyid rab tu thob pas/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig
95b8(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad ma lus par bag langs pa tsam du g.yos te/ rin po che thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan par gnas shing chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi sgra yang shin tu grag par 'gyur te/
96a1(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor rgya mtsho thams cad du yang / nor bu'i rgyal po chen po bcu'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab par gyur to/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste nor bu'i rgyal po mtshan dang
96a2(phal chen): ldan pa'i gser dpal gyi rgyal mtshan gyi dpal gyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /'di lta ste nor bu'i rgyal po 'od kyis rnam par gsal bar byed pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /'di lta ste nor bu'i
96a3(phal chen): rgyal po phyogs bcur rin po che'i 'khor lo rab tu 'grems pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /'di lta ste nor bu'i rgyal po byang chub sems dpa'i gzugs brnyan rin po che'i snying po'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab
96a4(phal chen): po/ /'di lta ste nor bu'i rgyal po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mtshan gyi khams rab tu sgrog pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /'di lta ste nor bu'i rgyal po zhing rnam par snang bar byed cing snying po byang chub
96a5(phal chen): tu dpal rab tu 'bar ba'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /'di lta ste nor bu'i rgyal po phyogs bcur snang ba'i sprul pa 'gyed pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /'di lta ste nor bu'i rgyal po byang chub sems
96a6(phal chen): dpa' thams cad kyi yon tan gyi 'khor lo dang mthu rab tu grags par byed pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /'di lta ste nor bu'i rgyal po nyi ma'i dpal gyi gzi brjid kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /'di lta
96a7(phal chen): ste nor bu'i rgyal po rol mo'i sgra yid du 'ong bas phyogs thams cad khyab par byed pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po'i sprin gyi char bcu po 'di dag mngon par bab par gyur to/ /de bzhin gshegs
96a8(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi ba spu'i sgo thams cad dang 'od zer gyi sgo thams cad nas kyang tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag byung bar gyur to/ /zhing rnams 'byam klas kun na kun tu bzang po de/ /dbang po yid du 'ong la rab tu
96b1(phal chen): 'jug pa mthong / /kun tu rnam 'phrul rnam par 'di 'dra ston pa byed/ /ting 'dzin yul la 'jug pa mtha' dang dbus myed do/ /lus rnams thams cad nas kyang kun tu bzang po de/ /sprul pa rab tu 'gyed cing chos
96b2(phal chen): dbyings rtag par 'gengs/ /ting 'dzin kun gyi tshul dang mying dang rnam 'phrul pa/ /thams cad dbyangs kyis chags pa myed par rgya che sgrog /ting 'dzin thams cad gzhan dang gzhan gyi rnam kun gyis/ /de bzhin
96b3(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad zhabs kyi drung dag tu/ /rgyal ba kun gyi spyod yul yangs pa gang byas te/ /zhing rnams kun tu rnam par 'phrul pa mang po ston/ /zhing kun rgyal ba kun gyi zhabs drung ji bzhin tu/ /de ltar zhing
96b4(phal chen): kun shin tu phra ba'i rdul phran la/ /ting 'dzin rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad ma lus ston/ /rnam par snang mdzad smon lam dbyings la rab tu zhugs/ /kun tu bzang po'i lus ni nam mkha'i mtshan nyid do/ /thams
96b5(phal chen): cad zhing la mi gnas de bzhin nyid la gnas/ /lus kyi sprin ni 'gro ba kun dang mnyam par kun bkye zhing / /sems can kun la bsam pa bzhin du de dag ston/ /sangs rgyas rnams kun zhing rnams gang yod pa/ /
96b6(phal chen): mtha' dang dbus myed kun la rab tu zhugs pa rnams/ /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam gnas pa dag la bstan/ /rnam par 'phrul pa 'di 'dra dam pa tshad kyang med/ /'khor rnams rgya mtsho rdul phran mtha' dang dbus
96b7(phal chen): myed pa/ /tshad myed thams cad lus kyi nang du kun tshud cing / /dbyings la zhing mang dra bar rnam 'tshang rgya ba ston/ /skad cig sems la bskal pa mang po de bzhin ston/ /zhing rnams thams cad 'byam klas pa na
96b8(phal chen): rnam grags shing / /rnam par 'phrul pa dam pa ston par rab tu snang / /phyogs rnams kun gyi zhing gi dbyings rnams ma lus spyod/ /kun tu bzang po de la rnam lta kun kyang mthong / /rgyal ba kun gyi yon tan
97a1(phal chen): ye shes stobs la zhugs/ /ting 'dzin sa ni tshul rnams kun gyis rab tu mnan/ /chos rnams 'byam klas gzhan dang gzhan la rab tu zhugs/ /rang gi byang chub spyod pas sngan cad spyad pa ston/ /
97a2(phal chen): de ltar zhing rnams kun tu bsam yas rnam 'phrul ba/ /phyogs rnam rgya che kun tu bkang ste rab tu bsten/ /ting 'dzin rnams la 'jug pa rab tu bstan pa'i phyir/ /rgyal ba'i 'od zer sprin las yon tan legs
97a3(phal chen): sgra 'byung / /de nas byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor yod pa thams cad sangs rgyas kyi mthus thal mo sbyar te/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la lta zhing dbyangs kyi nga ro gcig tu de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa
97a4(phal chen): 'di dag smras so/ /rgyal ba thams cad chos las skyes pa ste/ /smon lam kun gyis sangs rgyas rab tu byung / /de bzhin nyid mnyam nam mkha'i snying po ste/ /chos kyi sku yis rnam par rab tu mdzes/ /zhing rnams
97a5(phal chen): 'byam klas kun la bzhugs myed kyang / /kun tu bzang po'i 'khor rnams kun na snang / /phyogs bcu kun tu yon tan grags pas khyab/ /ye shes rgya mtsho rab tu snang bar mnga'/ /rgyal ba thams cad sku
97a6(phal chen): thob phyir spyod pa/ /phyogs bcu'i yon tan rgya mtsho yod pa'i rnams/ /rdul sbubs kun tu de dag chud byas shing / /zhing rnams kun tu rnam par rab tu mdzes/ /zhing rnams kun gyi rgyal ba'i zhabs drung na/ /
97a7(phal chen): rgyal sras ting nge 'dzin dang spyad pa dang / /chos rnams kun la spyod cing gnas pa'i rnams/ /rdul dang mnyam pa'i bskal par kun kyang snang / /chos kyi dbyings rnams lus kyi khyab byas shing / /zhing rnams 'byam klas
97a8(phal chen): kun la shin tu zhugs/ /sems can rgya mtsho'i don du de spyod cing / /rdul phran kun la chos kyi dbyings su zhugs/ /chos kyi dbyings la da ltar zhugs nas kyang / /rdul phran kun la mi zad tha mi dad/ /namakha'i dbyings ni
97b1(phal chen): lus kyi gang byas shing / /rgyal ba'i chos rnams yangs pa rab tu ston/ /yon tan rgya mtsho 'od kun gzhal du med/ /rnam yangs stobs chen 'od zer yon tan sprin/ /'gro ba rgya mtsho'i don du spyod byed cing / /rgyal
97b2(phal chen): ba'i spyod lam gzhan du med pa ston/ /gang gi don du bskal pa rgya mtsho dag /mtha' yas par ni bzang po'i spyod spyad pa/ /de dag chos kyi dbyings rnams gang byas nas/ /thams cad chos kyi sprin las rab tu brjod/ /zhing
97b3(phal chen): rnams ji ltar 'byung bar 'gyur ba dang / /stobs bcu rnams kyang ji ltar 'byung 'gyur dang / /sems can rgya mtsho ji ltar 'byung 'gyur ba/ /sems can rnams la sgra dbyangs gtong zhing ston/ /'khor rnams yangs pa
97b4(phal chen): 'di dag thams cad kyang / /kun tu bzang po khyod la mngon sum gnas/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi gnang bar 'gyur ba yin/ /chos kyi 'khor lo de ring khyod kyis bskor/ /kun tu bzang po'i ting nge 'dzin dang rnam par
97b5(phal chen): 'phrul pa rab tu byung ba zhes bya ba ste le'u gsum pa'o/ / // de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad la rnam par bltas/
97b6(phal chen): sems can gyi khams rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang dbang po rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ sangs rgyas thams
97b7(phal chen): cad kyi chos kyi rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ dus rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yang dag par 'byung ba'i smon lam rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa
97b8(phal chen): rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas nas/ byang chub sems dpa' 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
98a1(phal chen): 'du zhing 'jig pa yongs su dag pa 'byung ba'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can thams cad kyi las 'byung ba rgya mtsho mkhyen pa ni bsam gyi
98a2(phal chen): mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la rnam par gnas pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin
98a3(phal chen): gshegs pa rgya mtsho thams cad mtha' dang dbus myed par bstan pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtsho rnam par dgod pa'i
98a4(phal chen): ye shes ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bsam pa dang / dad pa dang dbang po rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
98a5(phal chen): thugs kyi skad cig gcig la dus thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid thugs su chud pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul
98a6(phal chen): pa rgya mtsho yang dag par bstan pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyi myi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba'i ye shes ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
98a7(phal chen): rnam par dgod pa rab tu bstan pa rgya mtsho ni bsam gyi myi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sku rab tu bstan pa yongs su dag pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab po/ /
98a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yon tan rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus myed pas rnam par snang ba ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos yongs su dag
98b1(phal chen): pa ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su dag pa mtha' yas pa ni bsam gyis myi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od zer rgya
98b2(phal chen): mtsho kha dog sna tshogs kyi sprin rab tu dbye ba mdzad pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dpal rin po che 'phro ba'i rgya mtsho rnam par rgyu ba ni bsam gyis mi
98b3(phal chen): khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang dbyangs rgya mtsho rab tu 'grub pa ni bsam gyis myi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi cho 'phrul rnam pa gsum
98b4(phal chen): yongs su bstan pas sems can rgya mtsho yongs su smin par mdzad pa dang / 'dul ba mdzad pa ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gdul ba rgya mtsho thams cad la brtson
98b5(phal chen): pa don yod pa ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sa la rab tu zhugs pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin
98b6(phal chen): gshegs pa'i yul la 'jug pa ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byin gyis rlabs kyi mthu ni bsam gyis mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs
98b7(phal chen): rgyas kyi ye shes kyi spyod yul rnam par rgyu ba ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi stobs la thub pa myed pa ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
98b8(phal chen): kyi mi snyings pa zil gyi non pa ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin tha mi dad par spyod pa ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
99a1(phal chen): rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdzu 'phrul dang rnam par 'phrul pa ni bsam gyi mi khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' ba chen po'i ye shes rnam par dag pa ni bsam gyis mi
99a2(phal chen): khyab po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mi 'phrogs pa ni bsam gyis myi khyab po/ de dag thams cad sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis
99a3(phal chen): rlabs pas/ sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rgya mtsho la gzung ba dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho la rab tu dgod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams
99a4(phal chen): rgya mtsho thams cad sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad kyis rnam par rgyan pa dang / bskal pa rgya mtsho thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung rjes su gsal ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams
99a5(phal chen): thams cad du chos kyi rang bzhin gyis dkyil 'khor rab tu brjod pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dad pa rgya mtsho tha dad pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu bstan pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi dbang po
99a6(phal chen): rgya mtsho la sangs rgyas kyi chos tshul kun tu snang ba yang dag par bskyed pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa rgya mtsho'i sgrib pa'i ri thams cad rnam par gzhom pa dang / sems can thams cad kyis
99a7(phal chen): sems dang spyod pa rgya mtsho la 'byung ba'i lam rnam par sbyang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i spyod lam rgya mtsho la rab tu dgod pa'i phyir yang dag par bstan par bya'o/ /
99a8(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos 'khor gyis dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho rnams de bas kyang shin tu dga' bar bya ba dang / chos la dga' ba'i shugs thams cad rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang /
99b1(phal chen): mos pa'i tshul yangs pa rgya mtsho yang dag par 'byung bar bya ba dang chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin dang snying po sgo kun dang ldan pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / kun tu bzang po'i smon lam rgya mtsho la rab tu dgod
99b2(phal chen): par bya ba dang / ye shes kyi myig dus gsum gyi rjes su song ba yongs su sbyang ba dang / 'jig rten thams cad kun nas snang bar byed pa'i snying po shes rab chen po'i rgya mtsho rnam par 'phel bar bya
99b3(phal chen): ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad yongs su bzung ba'i phyir/ gzung gi rtogs pa yang dag pa bskyed pa dang / snying po byang chub thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi yul thams cad rab tu brjod pa dang / de
99b4(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi tshul snang ba'i 'od chos kyi dbyings rgya chen po dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la dga' ba'i shugs rgya mtsho rnam par 'phel bar bya ba'i phyir/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di
99b5(phal chen): dag smras so/ / //sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po bdun pa/ yon tan rgya mtsho rnams kyi ye shes zab/ /mtha' dang dbus med
99b6(phal chen): des ni zhing rnams khyab/ /sems can bsam la sbyor ba ci bzhin snang / /rnam par snang mdzad chos kyi 'khor lo'o/ /bsam gyis mi khyab rgya mtsho'i zhing yod pa/ /bskal pa rgya mtshor rgyal
99b7(phal chen): bas rnams sbyangs pa/ /sems can rgya mtsho yongs su smin bya'i phyir/ /sems can nang na rgyal ba rnam par mdzes/ /sems can rgya mtsho 'byung ba bsam myi khyab/ /sangs rgyas yul la 'jug
99b8(phal chen): pa shin tu zab/ /srid pa'i gnas can dad pa chung ba yis/ /sangs rgyas byang chub shes par myi nus so/ /gzhan du gang rnams shin tu sems bstan cing / /dge ba'i bshes kyis yongs su bzung
100a1(phal chen): ba dang / /sangs rgyas kun gyi byin gyis rlabs pa dag /sangs rgyas ye shes 'di la rab tu 'jug /gang rnams sems dag g.yo med sgyu myed cing / /snying rje'i sems can khong nas byams
100a2(phal chen): dga' dang / /dad pa che zhing brlabs chen de dag ni/ /'di dag thos shing dga' ba thob par 'gyur/ /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam sa dag dang / /chos dbyings nam mkha'i dbyings su khyab pa la/ /
100a3(phal chen): gnas shing spyad pa rab tu sus spyod pa/ /de dag rgyal ba'i spyod yul de shes so/ /gang gis rgyal ba'i rnam 'phrul 'di mthong ba'i/ /byang chub sems dpa' thob bya legs par thob/ /gzhan gyis
100a4(phal chen): yul gyis shes par myi nus te/ /'di ni kun tu bzang pos rtogs pa'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyis byin rlabs shing / /'gro ba mtha' dang dbus med 'di dag na/ /kun tu chos kyi 'khor
100a5(phal chen): lo rab tu 'khor/ /rnam par snang mdzad yul dang mthu yin no/ /bdag gi lus su zhing rnams thams cad kyang / /rab tu zhugs shing de zhugs zhing rnams kun/ /de dag spu rtse kun tu blta
100a6(phal chen): bar gsol/ /rgyal ba'i spyod yul shin tu bshad par bya/ /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam spyod pa rnams/ /mtha' dang dbus myed mngon par bsgrub pa dang / /kun tu myig gi yul dang lus ldan pa/ /
100a7(phal chen): de dag mgon po'i spyod yul 'di nyid do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bcu po 'di dag ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang /
100a8(phal chen): da ltar byung ba rnams kyis gsungaso gsung ngo gsung bar 'gyur ro/ /bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su 'byung ba'i tshogs kyi rgyu rkyen shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste 'jig
100b1(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gnas pa shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i dbyibs dang rnam pa shin tu bstan pa dang 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i lhun shin tu bstan pa
100b2(phal chen): dang / 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho yongs su dag par bya ba'i tshul shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu sangs rgyas 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di
100b3(phal chen): lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa'i byin gyis rlabs shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste bskal pa mtha' yas pa'i rgyud rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi
100b4(phal chen): khams rgya mtsho tha mi dad pa shin tu bstan pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu po 'di dag la sogs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa/ 'jig rten gyi
100b5(phal chen): khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyi gsungaso/ /gsung ngo gsung bar 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal
100b6(phal chen): ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad ni rgyu dang rkyen la dmigs pa'i sgo 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed phrag bcus byung ngo / /byung ngo byung bar
100b7(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs dang / chos nyid rab tu thob pa dang / sems can rnams kyi las kyi tshogs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i
100b8(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yang dag par sgrub pa'i chos nyid dang / sems can rnams kyis kyang byang chub sems dpa' dag dang / bsod nams kyi rtsa ba bskal ba 'thun pa bsags pa dang / byang chub
101a1(phal chen): seMda' rnams kyi zhing yongs su dag pa'i smon lam gyi khyad par dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pas/ rnam par bsgrubs pa'i smon lam gyis mngon par bsgrubs pa dang / byang
101a2(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mos pa'i dbang rnam par dag pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'jig rten las 'das pa dang / rgyu 'thun pas mngon par 'tshang rgya zhing sangs rgyas
101a3(phal chen): kyi rnam par 'phrul pa khyu mchog gi mthu dbyung ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po rnams kyi smon lam gyis rnam par 'phrul pa'i sgo'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ltar rgyu dang rkyen la
101a4(phal chen): dmyigs pa'i sgo bcu po 'di dag la stsogs pa rgyu dang rkyen la dmyigs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad byung ngo / /'byung ngo
101a5(phal chen): 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa nyid gsal bar brjod pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs
101a6(phal chen): kyis/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sangs rgyas ye shes yul ni bsam yas kyis/ /byin rlabs rnam 'phrul de dag 'di lta bu/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho bstan pa mtha' dbus med/ /
101a7(phal chen): rnam par snang mdzad chos kyi yongs su sbyangs/ /byang chub sems ni kun gyis bsam pa bzhin/ /smon lam rgya mtsho bsam yas rnam sbyangs shing / /sems can las rnams rgya mtsho bsam yas pas/ /
101a8(phal chen): phyogs kun zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad 'byung / /byang chub sems dpa' kun gyi rnam 'phrul dang / /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la 'jug pa'i sgos/ /smon lam rgya mtsho thams cad mngon
101b1(phal chen): bsgrub shing / /namakha'i dbyings la 'byam klas zhing 'byung ngo / /spyod pa rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus myed rnams/ /spyod cing tshad med bde gshegs yul la 'jug /phyogs kyi zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun
101b2(phal chen): sbyong zhing / /bskal pa mtha' yas zhing rnams re rer spyod/ /sems can bsam dbyings bsam gyi mi khyab pa'i/ /las kyi zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad byung / /nyon mongs las kyis de dag nyon mongs
101b3(phal chen): bcas/ /mos dang bsam pas rnam pa sna tshogs gzugs/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho rnam dag rgyan can rnams/ /rin chen rgyus byung sna tshogs dri med pa/ /dad pa rgya mtsho rnam par spel ba'i phyir/ /rgyal
101b4(phal chen): sras rnams ni phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams spyod/ /chos dbyings rdul gyi khongs su rgyal sras rnams/ /kun tu bzang po spyod pa spyod pa dag /rtul gyi khongs su mtha' yas zhing ston te/ /rnam
101b5(phal chen): dag mkha' bzhin mtha' dang dbus yang myed/ /namakha'i dbyings 'dra'i rnam 'phrul 'di 'dra ste/ /snying po byang chub rgyal ba'i zhabs drung na/ /pad mo'i stan 'khod kha dogs mtha' yas kun/ /
101b6(phal chen): de dag zhing bcas lus kyi nang na 'khod/ /skad cig sems kyi dus gsum byung ba yi/ /zhing 'byung tshul dang 'jug pa kun kyang ston/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis dus gsum zhing stan pa/ /rnam par snang
101b7(phal chen): mdzad rgya mtsho'i zhing myi zad/ /tshul gyi khyad par mtha' yas sna tshogs pas/ /rdul rnams kun la mtha' yas rgyan gyi rnams/ /sangs rgyas skad cig gcig la byin gyis rlob/ /rgyan gyi
101b8(phal chen): rnam pa tshul kun rab tu mkhyen/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la gnas pa shin tu bstan pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho re re zhing 'jig rten gyi khams/ rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba
102a1(phal chen): snyed de 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rgyan thams cad kyi rgya mtsho kun la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni nam mkha'i dbyings kyi gnas la rab tu
102a2(phal chen): gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od dkyil
102a3(phal chen): 'khor rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs rgyas thams cad
102a4(phal chen): dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sgyu ma lta bu'i las kyi byung ba lha ma yin dang mthu'o che lta bu'i lag na rdo rje rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so/ /
102a5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams dbang po thams cad kyi lus kyi gzugs brnyen rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyis khams rgya mtsho la la ni byang
102a6(phal chen): chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi lus rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i smon lam gyi byung ba'i rgyan rnam pa thams cad
102a7(phal chen): dang ldan pa rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas te/ de dag la stsogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rab tu bstan pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho re re zhing / yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i
102a8(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rab tu gnas pa shin tu bstan pa'i don 'di nyid yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/
102b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi mthus de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /kun kyang zhing rnams rgya mtsho 'di dag rin chen rang bzhin dri myed pa/ /rnam dag sna tshogs nor bu kun 'bar 'od zer rgya mtsho'i 'od ldan
102b2(phal chen): ltos/ /'di dag rgyal ba'i byin rlabs rgyu yis dbyings legs 'khor bar snang / /de dag gis ni phyogs bcu' nam mkha'i dbyings rnams gzhi kun rab tu khyab/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho la la dri myed
102b3(phal chen): 'od can nam mkha'i dbyings la gnas/ /snang ba'i snying po 'od can nor bu'i rgya mtsho dag la legs par gnas/ /'gro ba de dbus rgyal ba 'khor la chos kyi 'khor lo bzang po bskor/ /'di ni sangs rgyas
102b4(phal chen): yul yin sems can rgya chen shin tu mgu ba byed pa'o/ /la la me tog sgron ma kun tu rgyas pa'i mu tig nor bus brgyan/ /'od zer dra ba'i kun nas sprin 'bab spros 'phro sprin gyi 'od can te/ /
102b5(phal chen): zhing mang mtha' dang dbus med rgya chen pad mo'i rgya mtsho dag la gnas/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyi rab brgyan zhing rnams 'byam klas kun kyang rab tu mdzes/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho dkyil 'khor dbyings
102b6(phal chen): rnams la la sangs rgyas byin la gnas/ /yangs shing rin chen mang ldan rgya chen de dag byang chub sems dpa' gang / /lag na rdo rje rgya mtsho mang tshogs lha dbang lus la de bzhin gnas/ /de nas bcom
102b7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi 'khor lo rtag tu 'khor/ /nor bu'i shing dang spos kyi 'od 'phro'i sprin rnams mnyam pa'i dbyings la gnas/ /chu yi phung po dag dang rdo rje'i rgya mtsho brtan la'ang de bzhin
102b8(phal chen): gnas/ /la la gos dang brag dang rgyal mtshan me tog rgya chen dag la gnas/ /kun na'ang rnam 'phrul 'di dag rgya chen rnam par snang mdzad ston pa mdzad/ /zhing rnams ring dang thung dang gling gi gzugs
103a1(phal chen): dang rnam pa sna tshogs ste/ /sna tshogs rgya chen snying po dri ma bral ba yongs dag dri med snang / /rnam pa sna tshogs de dag smon lam rgya mtsho'i dbyings la rab tu gnas/ /sangs rgyas sprin gyis
103a2(phal chen): kun nas yog par rtag tu nam mkha'i dbyings la gnas/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho 'byam klas la la spyi'u tshugs yod dang med la gnas/ /byang chub sems dpa'i cod pan rin chen 'khor los bzung
103a3(phal chen): bas dag par gnas/ /de na sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul rgya chen thams cad kun nas rab tu snang / /rin chen sangs rgyas gsung rnams kun tu gtong ldan las kyis de dag sprul/ /chos kyi dbyings mnyam
103a4(phal chen): zhing rnams 'byam klas mig yor sgyu ma dang yang 'dra/ /mig 'phrul rnam phye rnam dag dri med sems kyis shin tu bskyed pa ste/ /nam mkha'i dbyings rnams sna tshogs rgyan gyi snying po gnas 'gyur 'di la
103a5(phal chen): snang / /las kyi yul ni bsam gyis mi khyab 'di dag bde bar gshegs pas bstan/ /skad cig sems kyis zhing rnams 'byam klas 'gro ba'i kun dang mnyam pa'i rnams/ /zhing rdul kun la kun tu
103a6(phal chen): bzang po rtog par rab tu bsgrub byed cing / /de na bskal pa rgya mtshor 'gro ba smin par bya phyir spyad pa spyod/ /chos dbyings rgyas par bkang ste de dag kun tu rnam 'phrul rgya chen ston/ /rdul rnams kun na chos
103a7(phal chen): dbyings yangs pa'i zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun kyang gnas/ /sangs rgyas sprin gyis byin gyis rlabs pas kun kyang yog cing yongs su rgyas/ /ji ltar rdul phran gcig la rnam 'phrul de bzhin 'gro ba kun
103a8(phal chen): na'o/ /rnam par snang ba'i sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul rgya chen rab tu ston pa mdzad/ /zhing rnams 'byam klas thams cad mig yor lta bu sgyu ma smyig sgyu 'dra/ /snang ba med cing 'byung med phyogs bcu
103b1(phal chen): dag na 'gro dang 'ong ba med/ /mkha' la gnas pa de dag rtag par 'byung zhing 'jig par de bzhin 'gyur/ /shin tu yangs pa de dag smon lam rnam sbyangs las kyis yongs su bzung / /kye rgyal
103b2(phal chen): ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rnams kyi dbyibs ni rnam pa sna tshogs ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni kun nas zlum pa'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
103b3(phal chen): 'byam klas pa la la ni kun nas gru bzhi'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni nam mkha'i rnam pa du mar rnam par phye ba'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la
103b4(phal chen): la ni kun nas 'khyil ba'i dbyibs su 'dug go/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni 'od 'phro ba'i ri'i dbyibs su 'dug go/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni shing
103b5(phal chen): sna tshogs kyi lhun gyi dbyibs su 'dug go/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni me tog sna tshogs kyi dbyibs su 'dug go/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni
103b6(phal chen): khyims sna tshogs kyi dbyibs su 'dug go/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni sems can sna tshogs kyi lus kyi dbyibs su 'dug go/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam
103b7(phal chen): klas pa la la ni mtshan sna tshogs kyi dbyibs su 'dug ste/ de dag la stsogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams kyi dbyibs shin tu bstan pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do/ /de nas
103b8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'di nyid yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su
104a1(phal chen): bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /rnam pa sna tshogs rgya mtsho'i zhing la ltos/ /rnam phye sna tshogs mtha' yas dbyibs su gnas/ /dbyibs kyis rnam par phye ba sna tshogs te/ /phyogs
104a2(phal chen): rnams kun nas zhing rnams rgya mtsho snang / /la la zlum po la la zur gsum ste/ /de dag la la phyogs dang gru bzhir gnas/ /nor bu pad+mo 'khor lo'i yan lags brgyad/ /kun kyang las rnams
104a3(phal chen): rgya mtsho rnam par bris/ /rdul med 'od kyi dbyibs dang tshul bzhin ci/ /gser las grub pa rnam phye sna tshogs ste/ /sgo mang mtha' yas pa ni rgyu zhing 'jug /las rnams rgya mtsho bsam pa dag
104a4(phal chen): pas gnas/ /zhing rnam rgya mtsho sna tshogs snying po can/ /nam mkha' 'di la ji ltar sprin gnas bzhin/ /de dag rin chen mang zhing rnam par phye/ /de dag kun ni sangs rgyas rnam par mdzes/ /
104a5(phal chen): zhing rnams 'di kun sems kyi rnam par brtags/ /sna tshogs rgyan dang snang bas kun nas gnas/ /rnam par 'phrul pa gzhan dang gzhan dag gis/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho sangs rgyas ston pa mdzad/ /
104a6(phal chen): bde dang sdug bsngal myong bar gyur pa ni/ /rnam par dag dang nyon mongs tshul bzhin te/ /chos nyid 'di ni rtag tu yod pa yin/ /de ltar las rnams rgya mtsho bsam mi khyab/ /skra gcig rtse la bsam
104a7(phal chen): gyi mi khyab cing / /thams cad rdul med sna tshogs dbyibs su gnas/ /kun nas sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad bzhugs/ /'khor rnams rgya mtshor chos rnams rab tu ston/ /rdul gcig
104a8(phal chen): rtse la phra dang yangs pa'i rnams/ /thams cad rdul snyed kha dog kun dang ldan/ /kha dog dbyibs rnams kun kyang rnam par brtags/ /de dag kun na rgyal ba'i 'khor lo bskor/ /rdul rnams
104b1(phal chen): kun la rab tu zhing bstan pa/ /de dag smon lam rnam par sprul pa yin/ /nam mkha'i dbyings su las kyis sprul pa ni/ /sna tshogs sems dang bsam pas rnam par brtags/ /sems
104b2(phal chen): can kun mnyam rdul rnams thams cad la/ /sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa sprul pa dag /rnam par snang mdzad chos nyid de yin te/ /rdul 'phran kun la zhing rnams shin tu gnas/ /kye rgyal
104b3(phal chen): ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i lhun dag ni gzhan dang gzhan du shes par byas ste/ de ltar 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che'i rgyun thams cad kyi lhun can no/ /
104b4(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la rin po che gcig las rnam pa sna tshogs su bkod pa'i rgyan gyis lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po ches thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi lhun
104b5(phal chen): can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni 'od kha dog sna tshogs kyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rgyan thams cad kyi mdog gi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams
104b6(phal chen): rgya mtsho la la ni rdo rje'i gzhi mi shigs pa'i lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul dang byin gyis rlabs kyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la
104b7(phal chen): ni rin po che'i mtshan nyid kyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa'i lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni nyi ma'i nor bu'i dkyil
104b8(phal chen): 'khor gyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni shin tu phra ba 'dzin pa'i lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni snang ba'i lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams
105a1(phal chen): rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog 'od 'phro ba'i rnam pa'i lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni dri dang kha dog sna tshogs kyi spos kyi lhun can no/ /'jig
105a2(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi me tog cod pan gyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi 'od kyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams
105a3(phal chen): rgya mtsho la la ni rgyan thams cad shin tu brtan pa'i lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sems kyi rnam par rtog pa skad cig gis dmyigs pa thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i
105a4(phal chen): lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni byang chub sems dpa'i lus kyi rin po che'i dbyibs kyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi
105a5(phal chen): me tog gi me tog ze ba'i lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung dbyangs rnam par dmigs pa'i lhun can no/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun
105a6(phal chen): tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i lhun shin tu bstan pa rgya mtsho 'di nyid la rab tu gzung bar bya ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs gyi phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/
105a7(phal chen): de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /zhing gi rgya mtsho rnams la ni/ /rin chen rang bzhin kun nas gnas/ /rdo rje bzhin du mi shigs sra/ /rin chen pad mo rnams la gnas/ /la la 'od
105a8(phal chen): zer rang bzhin te/ /dag cing gzung med 'od zer 'byung / /rgyan rnams kun gyi 'od zer gyis/ /sna tshogs mkha' bzhin dri ma med/ /la la 'od kyi rang bzhin te/ /dag cing 'od gsal gsal
105b1(phal chen): la gnas/ /'od kyi sprin can sna tshogs 'od/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gnas/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho la la ni/ /mig yor lta bur gnas pa ste/ /brjod du med cing gzung du med/ /
105b2(phal chen): smon lam dbang gi rab tu byung / /la la nor bu mu tig rgyu/ /snying po thams cad rnam par 'bar/ /mu tig 'khor lo zhig dag la/ /byang chub sems dpa' yongs su gang / /rin chen 'od 'phro byung
105b3(phal chen): ba'i zhing / /'od 'phro'i sprin gyis mngon 'bebs shing / /rin chen thams cad sna tshogs ldan/ /thams cad las kyi sprul pa yin/ /la la mtshan las byung ba ste/ /bzhi kun mtshan gyis
105b4(phal chen): kun tu bris/ /cod pan rnam pa sna tshogs bkod/ /sangs rgyas kun gyis mngon par sprul/ /rgya mtsho sems las byung ba yi/ /zhing rnams mos pa nyid la gnas/ /yul na mi gnas rgyu ma
105b5(phal chen): bzhin/ /yongs su rtogs pas yang dag brnyed/ /sangs rgyas sku'i 'od zer gyis/ /nor bu sna tshogs kun tu gnas/ /sangs rgyas sprin rnams rnam par snang / /sangs rgyas kun gyis rab sprul
105b6(phal chen): nas/ /la la kun tu bzang po yis/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho shin tu sprul/ /nam mkha'i rgyan rnams thams cad dang / /smon lam rnams kyi rnam par bris/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig
105b7(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rgyan shin tu bstan pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya ste/ 'di ltar dmyigs pa'i rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad kyi sprin rab tu
105b8(phal chen): 'phros pa'i brgyan dang / 'di lta ste byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi yon tan gyi 'khor lo rjes su brjod cing rab tu byung ba'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rtogs pa'i
106a1(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi rnam par smin pa rgya mtsho las rab tu byung ba'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam rgya mtsho'i klong yongs su ston pa'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste
106a2(phal chen): dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan sna tshogs rnam par dmigs pa'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste sems kyi skad gcig la bskal pa mtha' yas par rnam par 'phrul pa'i yul yongs su ston
106a3(phal chen): pa'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste rgyan gyi dmigs pa thams cad las sangs rgyas kyi sku rab tu byung ba'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste rin po che dang spos thams cad kyi sprin rab tu 'byung ba'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste snying po byang chub kyi rgyan
106a4(phal chen): dang / 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rnam par ston pa'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang / spyod pa yongs su ston pa'i rgyan dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de dag las
106a5(phal chen): stsogs pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rgyan shin tu bstan pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams
106a6(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i rgyan shin tu bstan pa 'di nyid yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho
106a7(phal chen): rgya chen mtha' yas te/ /rnam dag las kyis rnam pa sna tshogs gnas/ /phyogs bzhi zhing rnams rgya mtsho rnams kun kyang / /sna tshogs rgyan can yangs par kun nas gnas/ /kha dog sna tshogs yangs pa'i
106a8(phal chen): zhing gi rnams/ /rgya mtsho rtag par phyogs rnams kun tu 'byung / /rgyan dang rin chen 'od 'phro sna tshogs sprin/ /sgra 'byin zhing gi dbyibs rnams khebs par byed/ /byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan rgya mtsho
106b1(phal chen): rnams/ /de dag kun kyang rgya mtsho'i zhing na grags/ /sna tshogs brgyan dang smon lam sprin gyi rnams/ /de dag zhing mang rgya mtshor sgra yang 'byin/ /'gro ba'i las rnams rgya mtsho yangs pa dag /rgyan gyi
106b2(phal chen): sprin rnams kun nas sgrar 'byin te/ /sems can de dag rnam smyin ci 'dra ba/ /sangs rgyas byin gyis kun nas sgra yang sgrog /dus gsum byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa yis/ /rnam 'phrul zhing rnams rgya
106b3(phal chen): mtsho kun na snang / /dmigs pa re re la yang sangs rgyas kun/ /de 'dra'i zhing mang rgya mtsho'i rgyan la ltos/ /'das pa'i bskal pa de bzhin ma 'ongs dang / /phyogs bcu'i da ltar 'byung ba'i ji snyed pa'i/ /
106b4(phal chen): bskal pa de dag rgyan mang yangs pa yang / /zhing rnams rgya mtsho re re dag na snang / /dmigs pa kun la sangs rgyas sprin gyi rnams/ /'gro dang mnyam pas 'jig rten kun tu 'gengs/ /rnam par 'phrul zhing
106b5(phal chen): sems can rnam par 'dul/ /'di ni zhing rnams rgya mtsho'i rnam thar to/ /spos 'od sprin dang de bzhin me tog klung / /rgyan rnams sna tshogs thams cad kun nas kyang / /rtag par kun tu khyab par rab tu 'byung / /
106b6(phal chen): 'di ni zhing rnams rgya mtsho'i rnam thar te/ /phyogs bcu kun gyi snying po byang chub rnams/ /sna tshogs rgyan can kun kyang ma lus par/ /thams cad rgya mtsho'i zhing 'di dbyibs dag na/ /nam mkha'i
106b7(phal chen): sprin bzhin rnam par ston pa snang / /rgyal sras kun tu bzang po thams cad kyi/ /zhing rnams mtha' yas 'byam klas rgyan gyi rnams/ /'gro ba'i grangs snyed bskal pa rgya mtsho rnams sbyangs pa/ /zhing rnams
106b8(phal chen): rgya mtsho kun na rab tu snang / /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho yongasu dag par bya ba'i tshul rgya mtsho ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya ste/ 'di
107a1(phal chen): ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad la brtan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bas bskal pa mnyam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos dbyings kyi bsod nams
107a2(phal chen): rgya chen po'i sprin rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mos pa'i dkyil 'khor rgya chen po rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa' thams
107a3(phal chen): cad rab tu brtan pa'i yul la rnam par spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / yongs su sbyangs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'
107a4(phal chen): rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i sa thams cad kyi dbyings la rab tu 'god cing gzungs ba'i rnam par spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa dang / 'byung ba rgya mtsho la rnam par
107a5(phal chen): spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi smon lam rgya mtsho thams cad mngon par bsgrubs pa rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan rgya mtsho thams cad mngon par bsgrub pa
107a6(phal chen): rnam par dag pa la rab tu 'jug pa dang / 'di lta ste byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stobs kyi tshul yang dag par bsgrubs pa rnam par dag pa dang / de dag la stsogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho yongasu
107a7(phal chen): dag par bya ba'i tshul rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho yongs su
107a8(phal chen): dag par bya ba'i tshul rgya mtsho 'di nyid rnam par brtan pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyi phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho
107b1(phal chen): thams cad sna tshogs rgyan/ /smon lam tshul rnams rgya mtsho kun gyis byung / /kha dog mtha' yas las kyi rgya mtsho dag /zhing rnams rgya mtsho rtag tu 'od mang 'gyed/ /sngan cad dge ba'i bshes
107b2(phal chen): gnyen bsnyen bkur cing / /bskal pa mnyam pa'i las dge yongs sbyangs te/ /snying rje byams pas dgongs yangs kun bkang zhing / /zhing rnams rgya mtsho yangs pa 'di kun sbyangs/ /chos sgo kun tu
107b3(phal chen): ting 'dzin sa kun gyi / /sangs rgyas yon tan rgya mtsho yongs sbyangs te/ /bsam gtan tshul dang rnam thar sa sbyang zhing / /zhing rnams rgya mtsho sna tshogs yangs pa byung / /mos pa'i dkyil 'khor mtha'
107b4(phal chen): yas stobs bskyed cing / /rgyal ba'i mnyam nyid ma nor rtogs byas nas/ /bzod pa rgya mtsho'i tshul rnams yongs sbyangs shing / /rnam dag kha dog mtha' yas zhing rnams byung / /bsod nams sprin ni
107b5(phal chen): nam mkha' mnyam bskyed cing / /'gro ba kun phan bde don spyod spyad de/ /bsod nams rgya mtsho sems can kun bstan pas/ /'jig rten khams rnams rgya mtsho kun kyang 'byung / /zhing rnams rgya mtsho'i rdul
107b6(phal chen): snyed tshad med pa'i/ /pha rol phyin pa ma lus kun sbyangs te/ /smon lam mthar phyin mi zad goms byas pas/ /dri med rgya mtsho'i zhing rnams yang pa 'byung / /'byung ba'i spyod pa gang yod tshad med dang /
107b7(phal chen): chos rnams thams cad yangs pa yongs sbyangs te/ /sna tshogs thabs sgos sems can sbyangs pas na/ /'di 'dra yid 'ong rgya mtsho'i zhing rnams 'byung / /rgyan rnams kun gyi tshul dang sa sbyangs shing / /
107b8(phal chen): rgyal ba'i yon tan rgya mtsho kun zhugs nas/ /'gro ba kun gyi sdug bsngal mtsho bskams pas/ /zhing gi mtsho yangs 'di kun dga' bar 'gyur/ /stobs rnams rgya mtsho gzhal med yongs sbyangs shing / /
108a1(phal chen): 'gro ba 'di 'dra tshad med rnams sbyangs te/ /sangs rgyas rgya mtsho yongs kun bsnyen bkur bas/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho rnam mang rnam par dag /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams
108a2(phal chen): rgya mtsho re rer sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i tshul rgya mtsho ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya ste/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni sku chung ngur kun tu ston to/ /'di lta ste sangs rgyas
108a3(phal chen): 'byung ba la la ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad gzugs kyi skus gang bar ston to/ /sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni sku tshe'i tshad mi ring ngo / /sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni sku tshe'i tshad ring ngo / /sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni
108a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig yongs su dag par byin gyis rlob bo/ /sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su dag par byin gyis rlob po/ /sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni tshul
108a5(phal chen): gcig gis bstan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo byin gyis rlob po/ /sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni tshul bsam gyis mi khyab par bstan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo byin gyis rlob po/ /sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni sems
108a6(phal chen): can gyi khams nyung ngu rnam par gdul ba'i byin gyis rlob po/ /sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni sems can rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa rnam par gdul ba byin gyis rlob ste/ de dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams
108a7(phal chen): rgya mtsho re rer sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i tshul rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i tshul rgya mtsho'i
108a8(phal chen): phyogs 'di nyid yongasu bstan pa'i byin gyis rlabs kyi phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smraso/ /rgyal ba 'byung thabs rnam pa sna tshogs kyi/ /sgo nas zhing rnams rgya mtshor rab tu
108b1(phal chen): 'byung / /de dag sems can bsam pa ji bzhin mkhyen/ /sangs rgyas thabs kyi sgo mang rgya mtsho'o/ /sangs rgyas chos skur bsam gyis myi khyab ste/ /mi yor ma yin mtshan nyid med pa'i gzugs/ /gzugs
108b2(phal chen): kyi khyad par 'gro ba 'di dag du/ /sems can bsam pa'i phyogs bzhin ston la ltos/ /sku tshe thung bar la la rnam par ston/ /la la bskal pa bsam yas byin gyis rlob/ /chos kyi sku ni phyogs rnams
108b3(phal chen): kun gyi sgo/ /rab tu mdzes par 'gro ba 'di ni bzhugs/ /la la zhing rnams rgya mtsho bsam yas dag /sbyongs zhing 'byam klas phyogs bcu kun na yang / /la la zhing gcig rnam par sbyong ba mdzad/ /smon lam
108b4(phal chen): ma lus kun kyang tshul gcig go/ /la la bsam gyis myi khyab theg pa'i rgyan/ /sems can yid bzhin sangs rgyas ston pa mdzad/ /la la theg pa gcig kyang rab ston te/ /rgyal ba'i thabs ni gcig kyang
108b5(phal chen): mtha' yas so/ /rang byung la la byang chub sangs rgyas nas/ /sems can mi mnga' lam la gzhog pa mdzad/ /la la skad gcig gcig gis sems can rnams/ /rgya mtsho bsam yas byang chub
108b6(phal chen): don du 'dul/ /la la spu yi sgo nas bsam yas pa'i/ /sangs rgyas sprul pa'i sprin rnams rab tu 'gyed/ /'gro ba kun tu de dag mngon bkang zhing / /thabs kyi sgo nas sems can 'dul ba mdzad/ /
108b7(phal chen): la la sangs rgyas gsung gis kun bkang zhing / /zhing du sems can yid bzhin rab tu sgrog /bsam yas bskal par de dag gsung sgrog cing / /sems can rgya mtsho mtha' yas rnam par 'dul/ /
108b8(phal chen): la la zhing brgyan bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ /'khor rnams yang dag kun nas 'khod bcas pas/ /zhing mang rgya mtsho phyogs su gang byas shing / /sangs rgyas mkha' la sprin ltar khyab par bzhugs/ /
109a1(phal chen): de ltar sangs rgyas thabs ni bsam mi khyab/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun tu rgyas bkang zhing / /'gro ba kun la sangs rgyas mngon sum ste/ /sna tshogs rgyan mang du ma'i tshul dang ldan/ /
109a2(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyi tshul shin tu bstan pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i tshul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya ste/ 'di ltar
109a3(phal chen): zhing rgya mtsho la la ni skal pa grangs med par byin gyis rlabs so/ /zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa tshad med par byin gyis rlabs pa'o/ /zhing rgya mtsho la la ni skal pa dpag tu med par byin gyis rlabs
109a4(phal chen): pa'o/ /zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab par byin gyis rlabs pa'o/ /zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa mtshungs pa med par byin gyi rlabs pa'o/ /zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa kun
109a5(phal chen): nas mtha' yas par byin gyis rlabs pa'o/ /zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa kun nas mu med par byin gyis rlabs pa'o/ /zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa gzhal du med par byin gyis rlabs pa'o/ /zhing
109a6(phal chen): rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa brjod du med par byin gyis rlabs pa ste/ de dag la stsogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa byin gyis rlabs kyi tshul shin tu bstan pa rgya mtsho ni 'jig rten gyi khams
109a7(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa'i byin gyis rlabs kyi tshul shin tu bskal pa 'di nyid yongs su bstan pa'i
109a8(phal chen): phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /'jig rten rgya mtsho'i bskal pa tha dad de/ /sna tshogs tshul 'jug rgyan
109b1(phal chen): rnams gzhan dang gzhan/ /phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun na snang / /skal pa'i tshul ni rgya mtsho grangs kyang med/ /bskal pa mi mthun 'gro ba kun dang mnyam/ /phyogs dbyings 'jig rten rgya
109b2(phal chen): mtsho'i khams na snang / /bskal pa mtha' yas la la ring dang thung / /bskal pa sna tshogs rgyal ba'i sgras kyang bsgrags/ /rgya mtsho'i zhing rnams 'di dag phyogs dbyings snang / /byin rlabs bskal pa
109b3(phal chen): zhing rdul snyed dang ldan/ /la la gzhan rnams bskal pa gcig gis 'jug /la la skal grangs smon lam du mas byung / /bskal pa la la dri med nyon mongs can/ /la la rnam dag nyon mongs rnam
109b4(phal chen): par dag / skal pa ming ni smon lam rgya mtsho'i tshul gyis byung / /sems can 'du shes rnam pas tha dad tshul la 'jug /bskal pa zhing gi rdul snyed sngon cad spyod spyad pas/ /'jig rten khams rnams
109b5(phal chen): rgya mtsho shin tu yangs shing dag / de dag kun nas sangs rgyas yul rgyan tshad kyang med/ /'di dag rgya chen bskal pa'i 'jig rten rgya mtsho'i khams/ /bskal pa'i 'od dang 'od zer rin chen ming sna tshogs/ /
109b6(phal chen): bcom ldan dbyangs dang 'od mnyam 'od 'phro'i mig snang ba/ /snang dang dri med bzang po bskal pa'i ming la 'jug /bskal pa 'di dag rnam dag bskal pa kun las byung / /dri med bskal pa la lar sangs
109b7(phal chen): rgyas gcig skye'o/ /bskal pa la lar mi'i gtso bo mtha' yas 'byung / /bskal pa'i tshul rnams thams cad sa tshul zad mi shes/ /smon lam stobs mthus bskal pa sna tshogs 'jug par 'gyur/ /bskal
109b8(phal chen): pa la la mtha' yas rnams kyang gcig tu 'dus/ /bskal pa la la gcig kyang bskal pa'i bye ba'i mthu/ /bskal pa rgya mtsho kun kyang sna tshogs sgo nas 'jug /phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten khams
110a1(phal chen): kyi nang nas sgra yang 'byin/ /bskal pa la lar sprul pa kun gyi rgyud kyang 'byung / /ming gi rgyan rnams rnam par dag pa'ang de la yod/ /bskal pa la la sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul mthu yis 'byung / /
110a2(phal chen): skal pa'i tshul rnams kun gyi 'di ni rgyan yangs yin/ /zhing dang bskal pa rgya mtsho tshul ni gcig gis dag /zhing gi rdul rnams kun kyang tshad med gzhal du med/ /skad cig yud tsam nyi ma'i grangs kyis bskal
110a3(phal chen): par 'gyur/ /'di dag thams cad sems can 'du shes rnam par byung / /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa mtha' yas pa'i rgyud kyi tshul rgya mtsho ni 'jig rten gyi
110a4(phal chen): khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya ste/ 'di ltar chos nyid rab tu thob pas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag bskal pas 'jig cing 'du ba la rab tu 'jug par gnas pa dang / 'jig
110a5(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtshor tog pa'i sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pas bskal pa mtha' yas pa kun nas gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtshor gtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyi bsod
110a6(phal chen): nams rgya mtsho rgya chen po stsogs pa rnam par dag pas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho kun nas nyon mongs la rnam par dag par gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste byang chub sems dpa' mos pa sna tshogs kyi spyod
110a7(phal chen): pa rnams skye bas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rnam par dag la kun nas nyon mongs par gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste sems can rgya mtsho rgya chen po byang chub kyi sems la gnas pas 'jig rten gyi khams
110a8(phal chen): rgya mtsho shin tu dag par gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste byang chub sems dpa' rnams 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan dang gzhan du 'dod pas bskal pa rgyan tha dad pa'i tshul du gnas pa 'di lta ste/ phyogs bcu'i
110b1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtshor 'dus pas bskal pa mtha' yas pa rgyan shin tu mang por kun tus gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste de bzhin gshegs pa yongs su mya ngan las 'das
110b2(phal chen): pas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag gi rgyan nub par 'gyur ba dang / 'di lta ste sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i tshe 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rnams kyi rgyan gyis brgyan par kun nas gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs
110b3(phal chen): pa rnam par 'phrul pas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa mtha' yas pas yongasu dag par gnas pa dang / de dag la stsogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho skal pa rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa'i rgyud kyi tshul rgya mtsho
110b4(phal chen): dang kun nas gnas pa'i tshul ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i skal pa mtha' yas pa'i tshul rgya
110b5(phal chen): mtsho 'di nyid yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho'i chos nyid 'di dag ltos/ /chos kyi byung
110b6(phal chen): ste ji ltar gnas pa ltar/ /de dag 'byung zhing 'jig par 'gyur ba yang / /zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad rab tu snang / /sems can nyon mongs mi zad ldan pa dang / /las dang nyon mongs ngan pas sgrib pa'i rnams/ /
110b7(phal chen): de dag bsam la zhing gi rgya mtsho rnams/ /kun nas nyon mongs ldan par gyur pa yin/ /sems can rnam dag bsam pa ldan rnams dang / /bsod nams brtan dang rnam dag spyod yul can/ /rnam dag yul la nyon mongs
110b8(phal chen): ldan gyur rnams/ /de dag mos pa sna tshogs spyod yul gyi/ /byang chub sems dpa' skye ba'i dus dag na/ /bskal pa de ni rnam par dag par snang / /sems can nyon mongs ldan par gyur pa yang / /de'i chos nyid bsam yas yangs pa yi/ /
111a1(phal chen): byang chub bsam pa ji ltar bskyed pa dang / /de dag bsam pa ji ltar rnam 'phel bas/ /de bzhin bskal pa rgya mtsho mang po dag /bsam gyis mi khyab zhing rgyan yongasu sbyong / /bya ba mang po mtha' yas mi
111a2(phal chen): bzad pa'i/ /byang chub sems dpa' phyogs bcu kun rgyu yang / /rgyan la rnam pa tha dad yod pa min/ /bskal pa tha dad tshul gyi bye brag snang / /rdul rnams re re sbubs su dus kun tu/ /sangs rgyas zhing gi rdul dang mnyam
