111a3(phal chen): pa yi/ /rgyal sras ji tshul 'dod pa de bzhin du/ /zhing rnam rgya mtsho de tshul dag par 'gyur/ /gal te rgyal ba rnams ni skyes 'gyur na/ /zhing rnams rgyan gyi shin tu brgyan par 'gyur/ /bsam pa yongs su dag bzhin rgyas 'gyur
111a4(phal chen): te/ /'di na zhing rgyan phun sum tshogs pa'o/ /gal te rgyal ba mya ngan 'das gyur pa/ /de tshe de zhing rgyan rnams 'grib par 'gyur/ /sems can rnams kyang snod du rung ba min/ /zhing gi rgya mtsho de yang nyon mongs ldan/ /sangs rgyas rdzu
111a5(phal chen): 'phrul rnam 'phrul yangs pa dag / bsam gyis mi khyab gang tshe ston pa na/ /de tshe zhing rnams rgya mtsho mang po dag /kun kyang rgyan gyis rnam par rgyan par 'gyur/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya
111a6(phal chen): mtsho tha myi dad pa'i tshul ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya ste/ de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
111a7(phal chen): gsungs so/ /gsung ngo gsung bar 'gyur ro/ /de ni 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho cig tu 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten
111a8(phal chen): gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu sangs rgyas skye zhing 'byung ba tha mi dad pa dang 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag gi snying po byang chub thams cad nas chos kyi dbyings kyi phyogs rgyas par 'gengs pa tha mi dad pa dang 'di lta
111b1(phal chen): ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag gi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag gi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor chos kyi
111b2(phal chen): dbyings rgyas par 'gengs pa tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa'i sprin dang / mtshan gyi 'khor lo tha mi dad pa dang 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu sangs
111b3(phal chen): rgyas thams cad kyi dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor skal pa mtha' yas par brjod cing rgyas par bya ba'i byin gyi rlabs tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu chos kyi 'khor lo'i tshul tha mi dad pa dang 'di lta ste
111b4(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su 'du ba tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu rdul 'byam klas pa thams cad
111b5(phal chen): la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi yul rgya chen po ston cing brjod pa tha mi dad pa dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de dag la stsogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho tha mi dad pa'i tshul 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i
111b6(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho tha mi dad pa'i tshul rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa 'di nyid gsal bar bstan pa'i phyir/
111b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /rdul gcig steng na zhing mang rgya mtsho ste/ /kun na rgyan mang rnam dag kun yod kyang / /
111b8(phal chen): gnod pa med cing 'dra ba gang yang med/ /'jug pa bsam gyis mi khyab 'di la ltos/ /rdul rnams kun la bsam yas sangs rgyas bzhugs/ /sems can kun
112a1(phal chen): kyi bsam pa yid bzhin du/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad khyab byas kyang / /de dag thabs la tha dad gang yang med/ /rdul rnams kun la shing dbang mtha' yas pa/ /sna tshogs rgyan phyung kun nas bres sbyang
112a2(phal chen): te/ /phyogs rnams kun gyi zhing du mngon bkang yang / /de dag tha dad 'gyur ba nam yang med/ /rdul phran rgya mtsho rdul phran re re la/ /mi'i gtso bo 'khor 'di kun bskor cing / /'jig rten kun tu bkang ste 'phags
112a3(phal chen): bzhugs kyang / /gnod pa dag dang 'dra ba'i nyes pa med/ /rdul cig la ni mtha' yas 'od kyi sprin/ /phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun bkang zhing / /bde gshegs rnams kyi byang chub spyod bstan kyang / /
112a4(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i zhing rnams tha dad gang yang med/ /rdul rnams kun la kha dog bsam mi khyab/ /sprul pa'i sprin gyis kun tu gang byas te/ /sangs rgyas sprul pas sems can rnam 'dul yang / /'byam klas phyogs na tha dad gang yang
112a5(phal chen): med/ /rdul rnams kun la rgya mtsho'i chos brjod de/ /de dag 'khor lo tshul bzhin 'khor mdzad cing / /thabs dang mthu'i sgo mo sna tshogs kyis/ /thams cad brjod kyang de la tha dad med/ /rdul gcig la ni rgyal ba kun gyi gsung / /
112a6(phal chen): 'gro ba snod du gyur la de dag brjod byas te/ /rgya mtsho'i zhing du bskal par byin rlabs kyang / /de dag gsung gi yan lag tha mi dad/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho mtha' yas rgyan gyi rnams/ /thams cad rdul sbubs gcig tu rab tu 'dzud/ /
112a7(phal chen): rgyal ba rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul mthu la ltos/ /las kyi dngos las de dag skyes pa min/ /rdul gcig la ni dus gsum rgyal ba dag /ji ltar byung ba de dag thams cad snang / /de dag gshegs dang byon pa gang yang
112a8(phal chen): med/ /'gro ba kun nas sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa'i phyogs gsal bar bya ba yang dag par bsgrub pa zhes bya ste le'u bzhi pa'o// //
112b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po brgyad pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gzhi dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa 'di/
112b2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe/ bskal pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis yongs su dag par
112b3(phal chen): byas te/ bskal pa re re zhing yang de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi zhabs kyi drung du/ smon lam rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
112b4(phal chen): kyi yongs su dag par byas so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dang gzhi dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa de ni rlung gi dkyil 'khor ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis shin tu
112b5(phal chen): bzung ba ste/ de la rlung gi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi 'og ma ni gzhi kun nas/ ston pa zhes bya ste/ rin po che thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba 'bar bas brgyan pa'i gzhis ston to/ /de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil
112b6(phal chen): 'khor rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyan 'byung ba zhes bya ba yod de/ nor bu'i rgyal po 'od rnam par dag pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi gzhis ston to/ /de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor rin po che'i mthu zhes bya ba yod de/ rin po che
112b7(phal chen): thams cad kyi dril bu'i gzhis ston to/ /de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor 'od 'phro ba mnyam par ston pa zhes bya ba yod de/ nor bu'i rgyal po nyi ma snang ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi 'khor lo'i gzhis ston to/ /de'i steng na rlung gi
112b8(phal chen): dkyil 'khor rgyan kun nas rnam par bres pa zhes bya ba yod do/ 'od zer gyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi me tog gi gzhis ston to/ /de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor gzhi kun nas dri ma med cing yongasu dag pa zhes bya ba yod de me tog
113a1(phal chen): thams cad 'phro ba'i seng ge'i khri'i gzhis ston to/ /de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor phyogs su sgra sgrog cing kun tu rgyu ba zhes bya ba yod de/ mu tig dang man shel gyi rgyal mtshan sna tshogs kyi gzhis ston to/ /
113a2(phal chen): de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor rin po che thams cad 'dzin pa zhes bya ba yod de/ nor bu'i rgyal po'i shing dang me tog sna tshogs kyi glong gi gzhis ston to/ /de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor kun nas 'dzin pa'i shugs shes bya ba
113a3(phal chen): yod de/ sprin gyi nor bu thams cad kyi ri rab kyi sprin gyi gzhis ston to/ /de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor gyi khyim kun tu rgyu ba zhes bya ba yod de/ rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog dang spos kyi khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin gyi gzhis ston
113a4(phal chen): to/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag rlung gi dkyil 'khor ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed de dag thams cad kyi steng ma ni rlung gi dkyil 'khor gzi brjid bzang po dpal gyi snying po zhes bya ste/ nor bu kun nas snang ba'i rgyan dang ldan pa'i
113a5(phal chen): spos kyi chu rgya mtsho'i gzhis ston to/ /spos kyi chu rgya mtsho nor bu kun nas snang ba'i gzhis brgyan pa'i snying po zhes bya ba de las pad+mo chen po spos kyi rgyal mtshan khyer ba'i 'od zer dang ze ba sna tshogs shes bya ba mngon par byung ste/
113a6(phal chen): pad+mo chen po de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gzhi dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa kun nas gru bzhir 'dug pa rnam par dag pa shin tu brtan pa rdo rje dang nor bu thams cad kyi 'khor yug gi bskor ba/ rim gyis
113a7(phal chen): gzhol bar gnas shing rgyud kyi rgya mtsho sa la rab tu gnas pa 'di 'dug go/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gzhi dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa 'di
113a8(phal chen): nyid kyi yon tan rgya mtsho yongasu dag pa'i phyogs 'di nyid brjod pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /gzhi rgyan me tog 'jig
113b1(phal chen): rten khams gang rgya mtsho de ni rin chen kun gyi snying po kha dog sna tshogs ste/ /rdul rnams kun dang mnyam pa'i sngon ched sangs rgyas kyis/ /drung du sngon tshe rgya mtshor sbyad pas dri med pa/ /rgya chen snying rje'i sprin gyis khams rnams
113b2(phal chen): kun bkang zhing / /zhing gi rdul dang mnyam pa'i lus kyang kun btang nas/ /sngon gyi skal pa rgya mtshor spyod pa spyad pas na/ /'jig rten rgya mtsho'i khams de yangs shing rnam par dag /sangs rgyas rnam par snang bas smon
113b3(phal chen): lam che mdzad de/ /'od snang btang ba mkha'i dkyil na gnas pa ni/ /rlung gi phung pos btab kyang mi bskyod mi g.yo ste/ /nor bu kun rgyan sangs rgyas gzugs brnyan snying po'o/ /me tog mdzod bkye gtor ba rin chen
113b4(phal chen): yid 'ong bzhin/ /sngon gyi smon lam dbang gis mkha'i dbyings la gnas/ /rgya mtsho'i rgyan rnams thams cad sna tshogs bstan par gnas/ /phyogs dang phyogs mtshams kun tu 'od kyi sprin kyang gtong / /nor bu
113b5(phal chen): thams cad sgo nas byang chub sems dpa'i rnams/ /byung zhing 'od zer sprin 'bar phyogs rnams kun tu 'dor/ /'od zer me tog tshon dang 'od zer 'khor lo'i tshogs/ /phyogs rnams ma lus kun gyi chos dbyings
113b6(phal chen): khyab par byed/ /rin chen kun gyi 'od zer sprin rnams bkye ba ni/ /phyogs dang phyogs mtshams kun gyi zhing rnams khyab par byed/ /sdug bsngal thams cad bcil zhing byang chub mchog la bgrod/ /'jig rten
113b7(phal chen): rgya mtsho thams cad 'od 'phro rab tu 'bar/ /'gro ba kun dang mnyam pa'i sprul pa sna tshogs rnams/ /rin chen kun dang spu rnams kun nas rgyal ba 'gyed/ /brgya byin dag dang mtshungs pa 'khor lo sgyur 'dra dang / /
113b8(phal chen): 'gro ba kun gyi lus su lus rnams kun kyang gnas/ /sprul pas 'od bkye chos kyi dbyings kyi tshad mnyam pa/ /'od zer sgo nas sangs rgyas thams cad mtshan kyang sgrog /'gro ba ma lus kun gyi bsam pa tshim
114a1(phal chen): byas nas/ /tshul rnams sna tshogs sgo nas sems can rnam par 'dul/ /'jig rten rgya mtsho me tog snying po de nang na/ /rdul phran kun gyi khongs na chos dbyings thams cad kyi/ /rin chen 'od kyi sangs rgyas sprin rnams
114a2(phal chen): 'bar bar snang / /rnam par snang mdzad chos dbyings rnam 'phrul zhing la ltos/ /bskal ba rgya mtshor 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal bstsal byas te/ /smon lam yangs pa'i sprin ni chos kyi dbyings mnyam dang / /bzang po
114a3(phal chen): spyod pa rnyes shing ye shes sa ldan pa'i/ /dgongs pa las ni rgyan mdzes de dag byung ba yin/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gzhi dang snying po me tog gi brgyan gyi rgyan pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho yongs su dag pas
114a4(phal chen): snang ba zhes bya ste/ le'u lnga pa'o// // kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gzhi dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i 'khor yug chen po ni nor bu'i rgyal po pad+mo nyi ma'i
114a5(phal chen): gzhi la brtan pa ste/ nor bu'i rigs rgya mtsho spos kyi tsan dan thams cad las grub pa/ nor bu'i rgyal po rgyan gyi yul thams cad kyis lhun shin tu 'phags shing zil gyis gnon pa nor bu spos zhim po gzi
114a6(phal chen): brjid kyi 'khor lo rnam par snang ba'i snying po can/ nor bu'i rgyal po rdo rje sra zhing mi shig pa ltar shin tu 'khrugs shing sra ba rin po che'i chu thams cad kun nas 'byung ba rin po che'i shing gi nags tshal gyi rgyan
114a7(phal chen): thams cad me tog shin tu rgyas pa/ spos kyi rtsi mchog bzang po thams cad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ spos kyi me tog dpal can shin tu bzang bas rnam par brgyan pa/ nor bu'i rgyal po 'jig rten gyi khams thams
114a8(phal chen): cad kyi dbyibs lta bu'i dra bas kun nas bres pa ste/ de dag la stsogs pa rgyan bzang po'i rnam pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rab tu brgyan pa'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa'
114b1(phal chen): kun tu bzang pos 'khor yug gi rgyan dang yon tan yongs su dag pa 'di nyid bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /
114b2(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gang yod pa/ /mtha' dang dbus med sna tshogs rnam pa can/ /nor bu mang pos rnam dag mtha' yas mdog /de dag sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pas byung / /dri med khor yug rgyan gyi
114b3(phal chen): brgyan pa ni/ /nor bu mang po de bzhin spos mang dang / /mu tig bstsal ba'i tshogs la rab tu gnas/ /kha dog mtha' yas rin chen rnams kyis brtan/ /snying po nor bu'i sprin can sna tshogs sra/ /'dzam bu chu klung
114b4(phal chen): 'od 'phro snying po'i tshogs/ /'od 'phro dam pa phyogs su snang zhing mdzer/ /khor yug dri ma med pa rnam par mdzes/ /nor bu'i rdo rjes byas shing sra zhing brtan/ /mtshams rnams mi phyed nor bu sna tshogs 'brul/ /
114b5(phal chen): mtshan ldan nor bu'i rin chen rnam bkod pa/ /rgyan rnams kun gyis yongasu dag par snang / /spos chu'i sprin gyis kha dog mtha' yas te/ /rin chen tsan dan me tog kun tu kram/ /pad+mo sna tshogs gos kyis kun nas yog /
114b6(phal chen): rin chen rtsi mchog dri zhim rnams dang ldan/ /sna tshogs shing gi sprin gyis kun nas brgyan/ /nor bzang kun gyis kun nas gzi brjid 'bar/ /'od zer sprin gyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor can/ /gos kyi mdzod kyis shin tu 'bar bar
114b7(phal chen): gnas/ /spos kyi 'od 'phro bdug pa gdugs 'chang ba'i/ /byang chub sems dpa' mang pos chos dbyings gang / /sgra dbyangs mang po rgya mtsho thams cad 'byin/ /'di ni rnam par snang mdzad chos 'khor lo/ /rin chen
114b8(phal chen): mdzes pa de dag thams cad dang / /nor bu dag dang kun nas 'od 'phro'i shing / /kun la rnam par snang mdzad sku gsal ba/ /gzugs brnyan tshul du nang na yod pa snang / /thams cad gzugs su sku rnams mtha'
115a1(phal chen): yas te/ /sangs rgyas sprul mang kha dog mu med pas/ /thams cad phyogs dang chos dbyings kun bkang zhing / /sems can mang po tshad med rnam par 'dul/ /thams cad rgyan las sgra dbyangs kun 'byung ste/ /
115a2(phal chen): rnam par snang mdzad smon lam 'khor lo yis/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho yongs su dag byas pa/ /de kun de las rnam par 'phrul zhing grags/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i 'khor yug gi/ rgyan rgya mtsho shin tu bstan
115a3(phal chen): pa zhes bya ba ste/ le'u ste drug pa'o// // kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la khor yug chen po de'i nang gi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i sa chen po'i gzhi ni nor bu mang po'i rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa/ rdo rje ltar shin
115a4(phal chen): tu 'khregs shing sra la brtan pa/ rin po che'i rigs thams cad las grub pa/ rgya mtshos rnam par phye ba mi shigs pa'i snying po can mi mtho ba mi dma' ba'i thang mnyam zhing rnam par dag pa/ nor bu rin po che
115a5(phal chen): thams cad kyi kha dog dang / 'od thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa/ sems can thams cad kyi lus kyi dbyibs lta bu'i nor bu'i gzugs sna tshogs gyi rab tu bsgrub pa/ rin po che'i tshon thams cad kyi rgyan gyis
115a6(phal chen): brgyan pa/ rin po che yid du 'ong ba'i pad+mo thams cad kyis gzhi byas pa dmigs pa thams cad du sna tshogs su gyur pa'i sprin gyis kun nas yog pa/ nor bu'i rgyal po spos kyi mdzod thams cad kyis gzhi mnyam
115a7(phal chen): par bdal ba/ nor bu'i rgyal po dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhing gi rgyan gyis sprin gyi dra ba rnam par bris pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyod yul gyi 'od dang nor bu'i dra ba mig 'phrul
115a8(phal chen): lta bus rnam par phye ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de dag la stsogs pa sa'i dkyil 'khor de'i rgyan shin tu bstan pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa'
115b1(phal chen): kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i gzhi'i rgyan rgya mtsho 'di nyid yongs su brjod pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smraso/ /
115b2(phal chen): sa'i dkyil 'khor gzhi ni rnam dag mnyam/ /'khor lo'i dra bas bsgrub pa mi shigs sra/ /rin chen sna tshogs mnyam pa'i gzhir gnas shing / /rin chen sna tshogs kun gyis kun tu gang / /de yid 'ongs ni rdo rje gser
115b3(phal chen): gyi bzhi/ /rin chen chu bo ri bo'i 'khor los bsgrubs/ /pad+mo'i dkyil 'khor gzhi yin me tog sa/ /tsan dan phye ma rin chen kun tu bkram/ /'od zer sna tshogs rin chen me tog rnams/ /'od 'phro 'gyed pas phyogs
115b4(phal chen): su sprin kyang 'bar/ /sangs rgyas 'od snang nor bu rnam par bkram/ /sa kun me tog yid du 'ong bas yog /thams cad sprin ni phyogs na sdug ldang bas/ /mi zad yangs pa kun nas khebs par 'dug /zhing rnams
115b5(phal chen): thams cad phyogs rnams kun bkang zhing / /sangs rgyas chos ni snyan par rab tu sgrog /rin chen nang snang sangs rgyas smon lam kun/ /shin tu dus ring rtag tu kun tu ston/ /sngan chad spyod pa ci 'dra spyod pa dag /kun kyang
115b6(phal chen): nor bu'i 'bru las gsal bar snang / /de yi rgya mtsho nor bu sna tshogs bting / /de'i nang na sangs rgyas spyod yul snang / /sangs rgyas spyod yul de dag zhing gi rnams/ /rgya mtsho kun gyi rdul phran re rer snang / /me tog
115b7(phal chen): snying po tshon gyis 'khor los bsgrubs/ /der ni byang chub sems dpa' rtag 'dong cing / /byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam kun kyang sgrogs/ snying po byang chub 'khor du rnam 'phrul lo/ /rin chen 'od zer
115b8(phal chen): 'od dang ldan pa dag / sa'i nor bu rgyan las rab tu 'byung / /sangs rgyas chos nyid 'di 'ang rtag tu ston/ /chos dbyings nam mkha' lta bu kun tu 'gengs/ /sangs rgyas kun yul ye shes rgya chen dang / /
116a1(phal chen): kun tu bzang po'i smon lam sus shes pa/ /de dag phyogs rnams rgya mtsho kun tu yang / /zhing rnams rgya mtsho dbyibs kyi 'phrul la 'jug /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i sa yi gzhi rgyan shin tu bstan pa zhes bya ba ste
116a2(phal chen): le'u bdun pa'o/ / // kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i gzhi sa'i dkyil 'khor de la spos chu'i rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod de/ de dag kun kyang gzhi rin
116a3(phal chen): rin po che thams cad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'o/ /nor bu'i rgyal po dang spos thams cad kyis rlung rab tu bsgrubs pa'o/ /nor bu'i rgyal po bzang zhing yid du 'ong pa'o/ /rnam par snang ba'i dra bar bris pa'o/ /rin po che thams
116a4(phal chen): cad kyi kha dog dang mdog tu snang ba'i spos kyi chus yongs su rgyan pa'o/ /rin po che thams cad kyi me tog sna tshogs glong du 'khyil pa'o/ /tsan dan gyi phye ma dang 'dres pa'o/ /sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung gi dkyil
116a5(phal chen): 'khor dang smon lam rgya mtsho'i sgra 'byin pa'o/ /rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi dkyil 'khor sprin rnam par snang ba'o/ /byang chub sems dpa'i lus kyi sprin me tog sna tshogs kyi kha dog lta bu rab tu 'gyed pa'o/ /
116a6(phal chen): kha dog dang dbyibs mtha' yas pa'i gdugs kyis khebs par rnam par 'phrul pas brgyan pa'o/ /dmigs pa thams cad la 'jig rten gyi khams mang po rgya chen po thams cad snang ba'o/ /phyogs kun nas
116a7(phal chen): rin po che'i them skas kyi phreng ba bcu rab tu bkye ba'o/ /mu tig rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog lta bu'i mu khyud kyi kun nas bskor ba'o/ /rin po che shel kyi rgyal mtshan bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa
116a8(phal chen): bcus kun nas brgyan pa'o/ /'di lta ste nor bu dang me tog gi khang pa brtsegs pa chu klung gang ga'i bye ma snyed kha dog mtha' yas pa bcus kun nas bskor ba'o/ /'di lta ste nor bu thams cad kyi pad+mo yid du 'ong ba'i
116b1(phal chen): grong khyer bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong bcus kun nas bskor ba'o/ /'di lta ste nor bu rdo rje shin tu phra ba'i gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis rab tu bsgrubs pa'o/ /rin po che thams cad kyi me tog
116b2(phal chen): pun da ri ka dang / spos kyi chu yongs su rgyas pas kun nas bskor ba'o/ /'di lta ste rin po che'i shing gi phreng ba rin po che 'bar zhing kun nas 'phyang ba'i nor bu'i dra ba can gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu
116b3(phal chen): phra ba snyed kyis kun nas bskor ba'o/ /tsan dan dang spos dang nor bu mang po sgra thams cad dang sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi phyag gis rnam par snang bar byas pa chu klung gang ga'i bye ma snyed kyis brgyan shin tu
116b4(phal chen): brgyan pa'o/ /'di lta ste rin po che dang gos dang rgyal mtshan dang / dril bu mang po thams cad kyi sgra 'byung bas rgyan shin tu rgyas pa'o/ /rin po che yid du 'ong ba'i nor bu thams cad kyi ra ba bye ba khrag khrig brgya
116b5(phal chen): stong brjod du med pas kun nas bskor ba'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang spos chu'i rgya mtsho'i rgyan 'di nyid yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs
116b6(phal chen): bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sa stengs de na spos kyi chu bo yi/ /rgya mtsho nor bus brgyan pa rnams brjod de/ /gzhi rnams rin chen gos kyi kun bting ba/ /
116b7(phal chen): mi shigs rdo rje lta bu'i sa zhing mdzes/ /spos dang nor bu'i rgyal po mang po dang / /nyi ma'i nor bu'i 'od 'phro sdug sprin dang / /pad+mo'i rin chen 'phreng ba'ang kun nas bres/ /gzhi rnams dri med yid du 'ong ba'o/ /
116b8(phal chen): spos kyi chu yis yongs su rgyas pa ste/ /rin chen 'od zer sna tshogs me tog glong / /sgra dbyangs rab tu gtong ba'i dbyangs kyis kyang / /sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa rab tu sgrog /them skas phreng ba yid du
117a1(phal chen): 'ong dang ldan/ /gzhi ni rin chen nor bu mang pos rgyan/ /stegs bu kun bkod rin chen pad+mo yis/ /sprin sdug dra ba rnam par bres pa ste/ /rin chen nor bu'i shing gi 'phreng ba dag /rin chen gser gyi kha dog
117a2(phal chen): yid 'ong 'bar/ /'od kyi tshogs dang rol mo sgra dag kyang / /rnam par 'phrul mang dbyangs su rab tu sgrog /spos chus yong gang rin chen bsgrubs pa ste/ /me tog pun da ri kas kun nas skor/ /spos dang 'od dang bdug
117a3(phal chen): spos 'od zer 'gyed/ /de dag 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par yangs/ /rin chen rgyal mtshan mu tig 'bar ba can/ /gos dang nor bu sna tshogs kun 'phyang zhing / /rin chen nor bu'i dril bu dra ba dag /thams cad
117a4(phal chen): mkhyen par 'jug pa'i sgra yang sgrog / pad+mo'i grong khyer rnams kyis kun nas bskor/ /kha dog mtha' yas nor bus rnam par brgyan/ /phyogs rnams kun nas mu tig sprin bkye zhing / /grong khyer rgya mtshos de dag
117a5(phal chen): rab tu brgyan/ /dra ba bzang pos kun nas bskor ba ste/ /rin chen byas pa'i gzugs bzang khyab kyi bar/ /rnam pa du mar 'bar zhing yid 'ong ba'i/ /rgya mtshos bzang zhing mdzes par rab tu rgyan/ /sngon cad sangs rgyas
117a6(phal chen): rnam par snang mdzad kyis/ /sna tshogs rgya mtsho zhing rnams yongs sbyangs pa/ /shin tu rgya che mtha' dang dbus med pa'ang / /de dag kun na rnam par 'phrul pa med/ /spos chu'i rgya mtsho de dag re re zhing yang spos chu'i chu klung
117a7(phal chen): g.yas phyogasu 'khor zhing 'bab pa gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor byas pa ste/ spos chu'i chu klung de dag thams cad kyang 'khor kun nas rdo rje'i pad+mo kha dog dang dri mtha' yas pas bsgrub
117a8(phal chen): pa'o/ /nor bu'i 'khor lo dang nor bu'i 'od rnam par dag pa sna tshogs kyi mtha' kun nas dkris pa'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog lta bus rnam par snang bar byas pa'i 'od zer
117b1(phal chen): gyi sprin dang ldan pa'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi sgra dbyangs sgrog pa'i dril bu'i dra ba rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog 'dug pas kun nas khebs pa'o/ /spyod pa'i 'od kyi klong sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mtshan gyi dbyibs
117b2(phal chen): lta bu rab tu 'byung ba'o/ /nor bu'i rgyal po rgyan thams cad nang na snang zhing 'od shin tu 'bar ba 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho lta bur snang ba thams cad kyi shin tu yog par byas pa'o/ /nor bu'i rgyal po phyogs bcu'i
117b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa rnam par snang ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i snying po'i me tog shin tu rgyas pas kun nas kheb pa'o/ /dus gsum du gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems
117b4(phal chen): dpa'i mtshan gyi 'khor lo dbyangs su sgrog pa'o/ /spos kyi chu dang rin po che 'od 'phro ba thams cad kyi 'od dang / de 'od zer gyi sprin rab tu 'byung ba ste/ chu klung de dag re re zhing yang rgyan shin tu stan pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
117b5(phal chen): 'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang spos chu'i klung gi brgyan dang / yon tan rgya mtsho 'di nyid yongasu bstan pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par
117b6(phal chen): bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /chu klung dri ma med pa'i chus rgyas shing / /gzhi ni nor bu rdo rje'i pad mos byas/ /rin chen mang po gsil bus gzhi bkram zhing / /kun nas brgyan pa sna
117b7(phal chen): tshogs yid du 'ong / /them skas phreng bas de dag kun nas bskor/ /pad+mo 'phyang ba'i mu khyud 'khor can te/ /me tog brgyan pa'i mu tig phreng ba dang / /me tog lda ldis sna tshogs kun nas bris/ /nor bu chu bo spos chu
117b8(phal chen): 'byung ba ni/ /rin chen kun gyi kha dog 'dog ltar 'bab/ /rin chen nor bu'i me tog mdzes par bkod/ /sil snyan sgra ni sangs rgyas gsung skad brjod/ /de dag rnyog pa nor bu zla ba ste/ /me tog 'od mang rin chen
118a1(phal chen): snying po can/ /phyogs rnams kun sgor 'gro ba khyab par byed/ /gzhi rnams nor bu mngon par bkram pa ste/ /me tog rnam bres rin chen 'bru dang ldan/ /kun nas rin chen sprin gyis khyab pa ste/ /rgyan dang
118a2(phal chen): sems can thams cad gzugs brnyan snang / /sangs rgyas 'od kyi nor bu'i rgyal po yis/ /sa rnams thams cad kun nas rnam par gang / /phyogs rnams thams cad 'bar zhing snang ba'i sprin/ /rdul phran
118a3(phal chen): kun la gzugs brnyan gyur pa snang / /nor bu'i rgyan gyis shin tu rnam par rgyas/ /mu tig gsal ba'i dra bas rnam par phye/ /nor bu'i 'khor lo kun nas rab tu bkang / /kun nas rgyal ba rnam par
118a4(phal chen): 'phrul pa snang / /'byam klas 'od gzer ldan pa'i rin chen gyis/ /sangs rgyas sprul pa bkye ba kun na snang / /sangs rgyas mang pos phyogs rnams kun khyab cing / /stobs bcu mnga' ba'i
118a5(phal chen): chos nyid rab tu sgrog / rin chen sna tshogs pun da ri ka yis/ /chu rnams kun rgyas snying po nor bu spos/ /de las mi zad 'od gzer rgya mtsho rnams/ /rab tu 'byung ba'i pad mo sna tshogs 'byung / /
118a6(phal chen): dus rnams gsum po'i rgyan rnams thams cad kyang / /nor bu de dag 'bru yi nang na ste/ /'byung ba med cing gzung du'ang yod pa min/ /de ni sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa'i mthu/ /rgyal ba
118a7(phal chen): rnam par snang mdzad thams cad du/ /rgyan dang sprul pa thams cad rab tu 'gyed/ /sngan cad sangs rgyas smon lam mthu dag gis/ /de dag 'gro zhing 'ong bar snang ba cha med de/ /rdul rnams rgya mtsho
118a8(phal chen): thams cad dag la yang / /rgyal sras thams cad spyad par rab spyod de/ /rang gi zhing dang lus kyi bstan pa'i rnams/ /bsam pa rnam dag tshul bzhin de dag mthong / /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag
118b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rgyan shin tu bstan pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gzhi dang snying
118b2(phal chen): po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i dmigs pa dag la'ang / dmigs pa re re zhing yongs su dag pa'i yon tan dang / rgyan shin tu bstan pa rgya mtsho ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du
118b3(phal chen): shes par bya'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho yongs su dag cing yon tan mtha' dang dbus med pas yon tan rnam par dag pa'i rgyan shin tu bstan pa rgya mtsho
118b4(phal chen): 'di nyid yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /zhing gi rgya mtsho 'di rnams thams cad
118b5(phal chen): kyang / /rin chen rgyan can 'od zer gnas pa ste/ /sdug cing bstsal ba'i sprin gyis kun nas yog /rin chen thams cad 'od kyang rnam par 'bar/ /mu tig nor bu'i sprin mang zad mi shes/ /sangs rgyas
118b6(phal chen): gzugs brnyan phyogs su rnam par snang / /zhing na yod pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa rnams/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams la rtag tu ston pa byed/ /sangs rgyas gsung gi sprin ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ /
118b7(phal chen): nor bu'i rgyal po thams cad snyan par sgrog /rnam par snang mdzad sngon gyi spyod pa rnams/ /rin chen rnams las rtag par snang zhing grag /sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad dri med 'od/ /rgyan rnams thams
118b8(phal chen): cad nang na rnam par snang / /'khor rnams gzugs brnyan mtshan nyid 'chang ba dang / /sprul pa rnams kyis zhing gi rgya mtsho gang / /sangs rgyas sprul pa rnams ni sgyu ma 'dra/ /de dag la ni byon pa
119a1(phal chen): gang yang med/ /sangs rgyas yul rnams byin gyis rlabs pa yis/ /zhing rnams kun na sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul/ /zhing rnams 'byam klas par ni rnam 'phrul zhing / /sangs rgyas yul
119a2(phal chen): rnams byon pa gang yang med/ rin chen sna tshogs thams cad dba' glong ngo / /phyogs rnams bcu po kun tu rtag par yang / /spos dang bdug pa 'od 'phro'i rgyan 'byung ngo / /chu bo rnams las rin chen thams cad kyi/ /
119a3(phal chen): 'od gzer 'phro ba kun tu rab tu 'byung / /me tog nor bu'i phung po gdugs rnams kyang / /rin chen kun gyis gzer du rab tu 'bar/ /phyogs bcu'i zhing gis gzugs brnyan mang po dang / /sangs rgyas gzugs
119a4(phal chen): brnyan rin chen rnams las snang / /rin chen 'khor lo'i gzhi brten yid 'ong las/ /spos chus rgyas pa'i chu klung rnams kyang 'bab/ /rin chen gser gyis dril bu'i dra ba yis/ /yog cing sangs rgyas
119a5(phal chen): gsung du sgra sgrogs 'babs/ /rgyal ba kun gyis byang chub spyod pa dang / /kun tu bzang po'i spyod mchog rab tu 'dzud/ /sangs rgyas smon lam sgra dbyangs rnam pa dang / /sangs rgyas thams cad sngon
119a6(phal chen): gyis sbyor ba dag / rnams dag nor bu'i ngos dang ngogs kun nas/ /sgra rnams sgrogs pa kun na rab tu snang / /chu bo thams cad dba' glong dag las kyang / /byang chub sems dpa'i sprin chen
119a7(phal chen): 'bar ba dag / chos kyi dbyings rnams rab tu rgyas byed pa/ /'byam klas phyogs rnams kun na rab tu snang / /chu klung de dag thams cad dri med cing / /nor bu'i rgyal po sprin gyis kun khyab pa/ /
119a8(phal chen): mdzod pu'i dpal dang sangs rgyas gzi brjid 'bar/ /nor bu'i rgyal po sangs rgyas gzugs brnyen snang / /spos chu'i chu klung de dag gis bar dag kyang sna tshogs la rin po che thams cad kyis
119b1(phal chen): rab tu brgyan pa ste/ chu klung gi bar de dag re re zhing yang rin po che'i me tog pun da ri ka'i phreng ba/ gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis kun nas bskor ba'o/ /chu klung gis
119b2(phal chen): bar de dag re re zhing yang rin po che'i shing gi phreng ba gling bzhi'i/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis rnam par phye ba'o/ /shing gi gseb thams cad nas kyang rgyan thams cad kyis
119b3(phal chen): sprin rtag par rab tu 'byung ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po byang chub sems dpa'i dpal 'byung ba'i sprin dang / 'od rnams kyang rab tu 'byung ngo / /shing gi bar de dag thams cad kyang 'od shin tu 'bar
119b4(phal chen): ba ste/ spos dang me tog sna tshogs kyis rab tu gang ba'o/ /nor bu'i rgyal po'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi smon lam bskal pa thams cad du byin gyis rlobs pa'i sgra sgrogs pa'i sprin
119b5(phal chen): gyis yongs su gang ba'o/ /spos 'od 'phro ba'i sprin gyis 'od gzer gyis rnam par snang bar byed pa'i sprin gyis mngon par khyab pa'o/ /spos kyi rgyal po yid du 'ong ba sna tshogs kyis rnam
119b6(phal chen): par rgyas pa'o/ /nor bu'i rgyal po rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i kha dog yang dag par ston pas mnyam pa nyid mngon par gang ba'o/ /gos sna tshogs sprin lta bus mngon par yog pa'o/ /
119b7(phal chen): nor bu'i rgyal po phyogs bcur 'od gzer gyis dra ba'i sprin gyis yog par byed pas rnam par rgyas pa'o/ /nor bu'i rgyal po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i 'od kyi mngon par gang ba'o/ /
119b8(phal chen): nor bu'i rgyal po sems can thams cad kyi las rnam par smin pa rgya mtsho'i gzugs rnyan shin tu ston pas rgyas pa ste/ de dag las stsogs pa chu klung gi bar de dag re re zhing yang rgyan shin tu bstan pa ni/
120a1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang spos chu'i chu klung gi bar gyi rgyan yongs su dag pa rgya mtsho 'di nyid yongasu bstan pa'i
120a2(phal chen): phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /chu klung bar rnams shin tu rnam par dag /rin can rgyan can gser gyis rnam
120a3(phal chen): par bres/ /yal ga me tog sprin rnams 'phyang lding ba/ /shing gi phreng bas kun nas mngon par khyab/ /shing gi yal ga'i dkyil 'khor sgo dag nas/ /rin chen mang po'i sprin rnams byin rlabs pa'i/ /
120a4(phal chen): zhing rnams kun na sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul/ /zhing rnams 'byam klas par ni rnam 'phrul zhing / /ji snyed zhing du de dag kun rgyu ba/ /de dag nor bu kun la rab tu snang / /de ltar zhing gi rgya mtsho rnam
120a5(phal chen): par sbyangs/ /sprul pa rnams ni mig yor 'dra ba ste/ /thams cad dag na chos nyid 'di yang snang / /'di ni rnam par snang mdzad spyod yul te/ /smon lam rnam par 'phrul las byung ba'o/ /
120a6(phal chen): bzang po spyod pas gang rnams byung gyur pa'i/ /byang chub sems dpa' shes mchog rgya mtsho can/ /de dag rdul phran phan la rang rang gis/ /rang gi zhing rnams rgya mtsho dag par byed/ /de bzhin gshegs
120a7(phal chen): pa kun gyi zhabs ring du/ /bskal pa bye ba rgya chen bsam yas su/ /de dag spyod yul thams cad mthong bas na/ /skad cig sems la de dag thams cad ston/ /zhing rnams mnyam med 'byung ba
120a8(phal chen): med pa ste/ /de dag mkha' 'dra mnyam zhing mtshan nyid med/ /smon lam stobs kyis kun tu gnas pa ste/ /sems can rnams la phan phyir rab tu sbyangs/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi
120b1(phal chen): khams kyi rnam par dgod pa shin tu bstan pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'jig rten gyi khams kyi spos chu'i rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed po de dag la
120b2(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu gnas so/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud de dag re re zhing 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa sangs rgyas
120b3(phal chen): kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor gyis bskor ba'o/ /'jig gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa de dag thams cad kyang gzhan dang gzhan la gnas pa/ dbyibs gzhan dang
120b4(phal chen): gzhan du 'dug pa/ phyogs gzhan dang gzhan la lta ba/ rnam pa gzhan dang gzhan gyis 'jug pa/ rgyan gzhan dang gzhan yod pa/ gzhan dang gzhan gyis rgyas par 'gengs pa/ gzhan dang gzhan
120b5(phal chen): du 'du ba/ rnam pa gzhan dang gzhan du ma 'dres pa/ rnam par 'phrul ba dang / byin gyis rlabs gzhan dang gzhan yod pa dag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam
120b6(phal chen): klas pa la la ni pad+mo'i rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni rin po che'i kha dog mtha' yas pa'i me tog rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi
120b7(phal chen): khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni rin po che'i 'phreng ba mu tig gi 'bru'i snying po can gyis rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni spos chu'i rgya mtsho la
120b8(phal chen): rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni me tog thams cad kyi rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni nor bu rin po che'i
121a1(phal chen): dra ba'i rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni 'od gzer gyi rgya mtsho klong du gyur pa'i chu bo la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam
121a2(phal chen): klas pa la la ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i nor bu'i cod pan sna tshogs kyi rgyan la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni sems can gyi lus sna tshogs rgya mtsho
121a3(phal chen): la rab tu gnas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis gsungs nor bu'i rgyal po la rab tu gnas so/ /de dag la stsogs pa 'jig rten
121a4(phal chen): gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa'i gnas shin tu bstan pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad kyang dbyibs gzhan dang gzhan du 'dug
121a5(phal chen): pa sha stag ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni ri rab kyi dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni chu klung gi dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten
121a6(phal chen): gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni kun tu 'khor ba'i dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni kun nas 'khyil ba'i dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams
121a7(phal chen): 'byam klas pa la la ni 'khor lo'i dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni myig mangs ris kyi dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas
121a8(phal chen): pa la la ni shing gi dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni khang pa brtsegs pa'i dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni rdo rje'i
121b1(phal chen): rgyal mtshan gyi dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni phyogs 'byam klas pa'i dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni khang ba'i dbyibs lta
121b2(phal chen): bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni pad+mo'i dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni sta dgab kyi dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa
121b3(phal chen): la la ni sems can gyi lus kyi dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni sprin gyis dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni sangs rgyas kyi
121b4(phal chen): mtshan gyi dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni 'od kyi dkyil 'khor kyi dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni dra ba sna tshogs bkye ba'i
121b5(phal chen): dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni sgo kun nas yod pa'i dbyibs lta bu'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa la la ni dmigs pa thams cad kyi dbyibs
121b6(phal chen): lta bu ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la stsogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa'i dbyibs rnam par phye ba shin tu bstan pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do/ /kye rgyal ba'i
121b7(phal chen): sras dag 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i tshul de dag ni lhun gzhan dang gzhan du bstan pa ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni phyogs thams cad kyi nor bu'i sprin gyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten
121b8(phal chen): gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni 'od kyi tshul can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni rin po che dang spos 'od 'phro ba thams cad kyi tshul can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni rin po che
122a1(phal chen): thams cad kyi me tog kha dog sprod las bsgrubs pa'i lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni byang chub sems dpa'i lus kyi gzugs brnyan gyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyis
122a2(phal chen): khams kyi tshul la la ni sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni rin po che'i 'od kyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni sangs rgyas kyi kha dog gi
122a3(phal chen): lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi khams kyi kha dog gi 'od kyi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni sems can thams cad kyi bsod nams
122a4(phal chen): rgya mtsho yang dag par 'byung ba'i sgra yi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtsho yang dag par 'byung ba sgra yi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyis
122a5(phal chen): khams kyi tshul la la ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su dag pa'i sgra yi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi
122a6(phal chen): smon lam gyi rgya mtsho'i sgra yi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni sangs rgyas kyi tshul thams cad mngon par bsgrub pa'i sgra yi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni
122a7(phal chen): zhing gi rgyan thams cad 'byung ba dang 'jig pa'i sgra yi lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang dbyangs mtha' dang dbus med pa'i lhun can no/ /'jig rten gyi khams
122a8(phal chen): kyi tshul la la ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sprul pa'i 'khor lo'i sgra yi lhun can no/ / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i 'byung ba'i sgra yi lhun can no/ /
122b1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshul la la ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan rgya mtsho yongs su dag pa'i sgra yi lhun can no/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de dag las stsogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud 'byam klas pa'i tshul gyi
122b2(phal chen): lus ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya'o/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud 'byam klas pa'i tshul gyi lus
122b3(phal chen): rnam par dgod pa shin tu bstan pa 'di nyid gsal bar brjod pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /
122b4(phal chen): zhing gi rgyud rgyan shin tu bstan par grub/ /dri med dri bral 'od 'gyed snying po can/ /nor bu pad+mo rgya mtsho kun la gnas/ /la la gang ga'i rgya mtsho dag la gnas/ /rnam pa sna tshogs tshul gyis
122b5(phal chen): gzhi gnas shing / /dbyibs kyang sna tshogs kha dog gzugs kyang mang / /ri rab grong khyer shing gi dkyil 'khor dang / /zhing rgyud thams cad la la phyogs kun lta/ /la la 'od lus me tog snying po
122b6(phal chen): can/ /nor bus byas pa kun nas sprin dang chu/ /la la'i rgyud gsal mu tig 'od zer lus/ /nor bu'i gzhi gnas kun kyang mi shigs sra/ /'byam klas la la kha dog sna tshogs bstsal/ /
122b7(phal chen): 'od 'dra 'od 'phro me mar sprin gyi mdog /la la'i rgyud ni sgra dang skad kyi lus/ /de la sangs rgyas gsung dbyangs mtha' yas 'byung / /la la'i rgyud ni smon lam sgra yi lus/ /spyod pa rnam 'phrul
122b8(phal chen): sprin gyi sgra yi lus/ /la la bsod nams yangs dang las kyi sgra/ /la la'i lus ni rgyal ba'i yon tan sgra/ /gang gi rgyud rnams rgya mtsho bsam yas pa/ /kun nas mi zad du ma'i sgo nas 'jug /
123a1(phal chen): rnam 'phrul yangs pa mi zad rgyan gyi rnams/ /tshad med kun gyis phyogs kun rgyas par 'gengs/ /phyogs rnams kun tu zhing rnams 'du 'gyur te/ /yangs pa'i tshul gyis zhing gi rgyud zhugs par/
123a2(phal chen): phyogs bcu kun tu 'du bar snang ba yang / /'gro ba med cing 'jug pa yod pa min/ /tshul gcig gi ni rgyud rnams kun kyang 'grengs/ /thams cad ma lus re rer rab tu 'du/ /de la tha dad gang yang mi
123a3(phal chen): dmigs te/ /gzhi med kun 'gengs mtha' dang dbus yang med/ /zhing rnams tshul gyi rgyud la rnam 'phrul ba/ /sangs rgyas rnam snang mdzad pa kun nas snang / /smon lam sgra ni rgya mtsho rab brjod cing / /
123a4(phal chen): zhing gi dbyings na sems can kun kyang 'dul/ /zhing rnams sangs rgyas sku yis kun khyab snang / /bsam gyis mi khyab byang chub sems dpa' gang / /sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul mi mnyam stobs ston cing / /
123a5(phal chen): sems can mang po tshad med rnam par 'dul/ /zhing gi rgyud kyi gnas shin tu bstan pa zhes bya ste/ le'u brgyad pa'o// //
123a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po dgu pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gangs can mtsho'i dbyings de ni
123a7(phal chen): spos chu'i rgya mtsho mig 'phrul gyi rnam par phye ba gzhi kun la rab tu gnas pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed de/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la gangs chen
123a8(phal chen): mtsho'i dbyings kyi spos chu'i rgya mtsho/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi nang na/ spos chu'i rgya mtsho dbus ma ni ze ba/ yid du 'ong zhing 'od mtha' yas pa zhes bya ste
123b1(phal chen): d e'i nang nas nor bu'i rgyal po byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi lus rnam par dmigs pa'i gzugs brnyan gyi rgyal mtshan gyi pad mo chen po bzhi spos dang nor bu'i rgyal po thams cad kyi brgyan
123b2(phal chen): pa'i rgyan can ces bya ba mngon par byung ste/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud phyogs kun nas rin po che'i 'od rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med
123b3(phal chen): pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor gyis bskor ba/ dmigs pa thams cad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i lhun can rab tu gnas te/ de dag las thams cad kyi 'og ma ni dpal 'byung ba'i 'od zer rnam
123b4(phal chen): par snang ba zhes bya ba 'jig rten gyi khams te/ de ni rdo rje thams cad kyi rgyun dang / 'od kyi 'khor lo'i sa mtshams nor bu'i rin po che'i ze ba mang po la rab tu gnas pa/ nor bu'i 'khor thams cad
123b5(phal chen): dang rin po che'i me tog gi rgyan thams cad kyis rab tu yog par gyur pa ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis bskor ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag kyang gzhan
123b6(phal chen): dang gzhan la gnas pa/ rgyan gzhan dang gzhan dag ste/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa tshul rnam par dag cing dri ma med pa'i mar me zhes bya ba bzhugs so/ /de'i steng 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing
123b7(phal chen): gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams spos sna tshogs kyi pad+mo dpal gyi rgyan ces bya ba rgyan thams cad kyi sa mtshams can rin po che'i pad+mo shin tu mang ba la rab tu gnas pa
123b8(phal chen): seng ge'i khri'i dbyibs ltar 'dug pa/ mu tig gi 'bru rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog lta bu'i bla re'i sprin gyis kun nas yog pa/ kun nas nyon mongs shing rnam par dag pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams
124a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing gnyis kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor gyis bskor ba yod de de na de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge'i 'od zer mchog gi 'od ces bya ba bzhugs so/ /de'i steng sangs rgyas kyi
124a2(phal chen): zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'das pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che thams cad kyi rgyan kun tu snang ba zhes bya ba spos kyi rlung gi dkyil 'khor gyi sa mtshams can rin po che'i

124a5(phal chen): bzhugs so/ /de'i steng 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'od zer sna tshogs kyi yid du 'ong ba zhes bya ba rin po che'i rgyal po thams
124a6(phal chen): cad kyi mtshams can kha dog sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i rdo rje brag gi rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas pa rin po che pad mo'i dbyibs ltar 'dug pa/ rdo rje'i 'od zer dang rin po che 'bar ba mtha' yas par snang ba'i
124a7(phal chen): 'od kyi nor bu'i rgya mtsho'i sprin gyis kun nas yog pa gcig tu dag pa 'jig rten gyi khams/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bzhi'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor gyis bskor ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs
124a8(phal chen): pa rdo rje'i 'od zer stobs dang brtson 'grus mtha' yas pa yang dag par 'byung ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so/ /de'i steng 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa na
124b1(phal chen): ' jig rten gyi khams 'od shin tu bkye ba'i me tog sil ba'i 'khor lo zhes bya ba rin po che thams cad kyi dril bu'i dra ba'i rgyan gyi sa mtshams can shing dang nags tshal gyi rgyan thams cad 'byung ba'i rin

127b1(phal chen): mongs shing rnam par dag pa/ nor bu'i rgyal po rin po che sprin mi zad pa rab tu 'gyed pa'i sa mtshams can/ spos dang 'od 'phro ba kha dog mtha' yas pa'i ri rab kyi rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas pa dbyibs

127b3(phal chen): dang namakha' kun tu snang ba'i 'od ces bya ba bzhugs so/ /de'i steng 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che'i 'od 'phro 'khyil ba'i
127b4(phal chen): dpal yang dag par 'byung ba zhes bya ba 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing nyi shu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor gyis bskor ba/ gcig tu rnam par dag pa rin po che nyi zla rnam par snang ba'i sa
127b5(phal chen): mtshams can dbyibs lha'i dbang po thams cad ltar 'dug pa/ nor bu'i rgyal po'i rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas pa'i rgyan gyi rnam pa du ma dang rin po che sna tshogs thams cad dang rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyis
127b6(phal chen): sprin gyis kun nas yog pa/ nor bu'i sgron ma'i 'bru yi dra bas kun nas yog pa yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan bsod nams kyi sprin gyis shin tu 'phags pa'i gzi brjid ces bya ba bzhugs
127b7(phal chen): so/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud phyogs kun nas rin po che 'bar ba'i 'od rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba de ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas gzhan dang gzhan la rab tu gnas pa dbyibs gzhan dang
127b8(phal chen): gzhan du 'dug pa/ lhun gzhan dang gzhan can/ phyogs 'byam klas pa gzhan dang gzhan la lta ba/ rnam pa gzhan dang gzhan gyis 'jug pa/ rgyan gzhan dang gzhan can/ gzhan gyi rgyas par 'gengs pa/
128a1(phal chen): gzhan dang gzhan du yongs su 'du ba/ gzhan dang gzhan gyi rnam par ma 'dres pa/ rnam par 'phrul pa dang byin gyis brlabs gzhan can/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul
128a2(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed kyi kun nas yongs su bskor ba ste/ 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams kun nas bskor ba/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi kun nas yongs su bskor ba'o/ /
128a3(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams chu klung sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis kun nas yongs su bskor ba'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams kun nas bskor ba/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i
128a4(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kun nas 'khyil pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi 'khor lo sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i
128a5(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi dkyil 'khor sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi shing sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin
128a6(phal chen): tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi phung po/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdo'i rgyal mtshan sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i
128a7(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams phyogs 'byams klas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams khang pa sangs rgyas kyi
128b1(phal chen): zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams pad mo sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams khyad khyud sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i
128b2(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa sems can sna tshogs kyi gzugs dang / lus kyi dbyibs ltar 'dug pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba

128b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa sa la mngon par blta ba'i dbyibs ltar 'dug pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu

169a8(phal chen): pa nas snang ba zab mo yang dag par 'byung ba rgya mtsho la ye shes kyi snang ba rab tu thob bo/ /'di lta ste phyir mi ldog pa'i stobs chen po'i shugs kyi snying po dang mthu chen po'i rgya mtsho la ye shes kyi snang ba
169b1(phal chen): rab tu thob bo/ /'di lta ste chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med par sprul pas brgyan cing 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor la ye shes kyi snang ba rab tu thob bo/ /'di lta ste yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho tshad
169b2(phal chen): med par 'jug pa la mngon par bsgrub pa ye shes kyi rgya mtsho rab tu thob bo/ /'di lta ste sangs rgyas thams cad rnam par dmyigs shing mos pa rgya mtsho sprin gyi rgyan yang dag par bsgrub pa rgya
169b3(phal chen): mtsho la ye shes kyi snang ba rab tu thob bo/ /'di lta ste chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa dang / mnyam par de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par dmyigs par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad
169b4(phal chen): mngon du bstan pa dang sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rgya mtsho la ye shes kyi snang ba rab tu thob bo/ /'di lta ste sangs rgyas kyi chos stobs dang / mi 'jig pa thams cad la ye shes kyi snang ba
169b5(phal chen): rab tu thob bo/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' gzi brjid chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa yon tan thams cad kyi/ ri rab kyi dpal gyi sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho la ye shes kyi snang ba rab tu thob nas/
169b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyi de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smraso rgyal ba'i chos nyid 'di thos nas/ /bdag gis ye shes snang ba skyes/ /des ni sangs rgyas sngon spyod pa/ /rgya mtsho
169b7(phal chen): rnams kyang rab tu mthong / /sku tshe kun tu ji lta bur/ /phun sum tshogs gyur kun kyang mthong / /mtshan gyi rnam pa rnams dmigs dang / /gang gi sangs rgyas mchod pa'ang shes/ /sngon chad sangs
169b8(phal chen): rgyas drung dag du/ /bskal pa rgya mtshor spyod spyad de/ /sangs rgyas rgya mtsho mang mchod nas/ /zhing gi rgya mtsho yongs su sbyangs/ /sku'i rgya mtsho mang po dag /rgya mtsho yongasu kun btang zhing / /
170a1(phal chen): spyod pa'i dam pa rab spyad de/ /rgya mtsho'-i zhing yang shin tu sbyangs/ /snyan dang shang mang rgya mtsho dang / /phyag zhabs dbu yang de bzhin te/ /rgyal srid btsun mo'i 'khor btang zhing / /zhing gi rgya
170a2(phal chen): mtsho yongs su sbyangs/ /zhing rnams so so re re la/ /bskal pa bye ba bsam yas su/ /byang chub spyod pa rab spyod de/ /zhing gi rgya mtsho rab tu sbyangs/ /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam gyi/ /spyod pa
170a3(phal chen): rgya mtsho kun spyad nas/ /sangs rgyas rgya mtsho kun drung du/ /zhing gi rgya mtsho rab tu sbyangs/ /ji ltar nyi ma'i 'od snang bas/ /nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor mthong ba bzhin/ /sangs rgyas ye shes 'od
170a4(phal chen): snang bas/ /sngon gyi spyod pa rnams kyang mthong / /byang chub 'tshang rgya zhi ba yi/ /chos kyi dbyings ni kun gang ba'i/ /zhing gi rgya mtsho dag pa'i rnams/ /dri med 'od can kun kyang mthong / /sangs rgyas kun gyi
170a5(phal chen): byin rlabs kyis/ /byang chub spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe/ /zhing gi rgya mtsho yangs pa'i rnams/ /de ltar bdag gis sbyang bar bya/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' gzi brjid chen
170a6(phal chen): pos/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa yon tan thams cad kyi ri rab dpal gyi sprin de mthong ba dang / bsnyen bkur ba dang / mchod pas de bzhin gshegs pa las mngon par
170a7(phal chen): khong du chud de/ 'jig rten thams cad ni snang bar byed/ sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho ni rab tu brjod/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rgya mtsho'i tshul ni rab tu sgrog /sangs rgyas thams cad
170a8(phal chen): kyi yon tan rgya mtsho'i tshul ni shin tu brjod/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba'i ye shes kyi sgo yongs su sbyang ba ni shin tu ston/ snying po byang chub thams cad la mngon
170b1(phal chen): par 'tshang rgya ba'i rgya mtsho'i rnam par 'phrul pa ni rab tu brjod/ sangs rgyas kyi stobs dang mi bsnyengs pa dang / ye shes tha mi dad pa ni shin tu brjod/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku sgo kun nas
170b2(phal chen): rnam par dmigs shing mthong ba ni rab tu brjod/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa shin tu ston/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa mtha' dang dbus med pa'i rgyan ni rab
170b3(phal chen): tu ston/ byang chub sems dpa'i kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa dang / smon lam ni mngon par bsgrub pa byed cing / sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byang chub tu sems bskyed de/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin
170b4(phal chen): tu phra ba snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa'ang yongasu 'dzin du btsud do/ /de nas de bzhin gshegs pa yon tan thams cad kyi ri bo ri rab dpal gyi sprin gyi/ byang chub sems dpa' gzi brjid chen po la tshigs
170b5(phal chen): su bcad de gsungs pa/ sems can kun la phan pa'i phyir/ /byang chub don du khyod zhugs pa/ /gzi brjid chen po legaso legs/ /bsod nams snying po grags pa che/ /snang ba khyod kyis rab tu non/ /chos
170b6(phal chen): kyi dbyings ni khyab byas shing / /bsod nams chen po'i sprin ldan pa'i/ /sangs rgyas ye shes rgya mtsho gyur/ /bskal pa zhing gi rdul snyed du/ /zhing gcig na yang spyod spyad cing / /nga yi ye shes ji lta bur/ /
170b7(phal chen): khyod kyi mthong ba de ltar 'gyur/ /tshul 'di kun nas shes par ni/ /brtson 'grus chung ngus mi nus te/ /brtson 'grus stobs chen ldan pa'i rnams/ /rgya mtsho'i zhing rnams dag par byed/ /thams cad
170b8(phal chen): rdul la 'jug tshul du/ /bskal pa rgya mtshor su spyod pa/ /rgya mtsho'i zhing gi rgyan gyi rnams/ /de la 'di 'drar rab tu 'gyur/ /sems can rnams ni re re'i phyir/ /bskal pa rgya mtshor spyod spyad cing / /
171a1(phal chen): 'khor kyang skyo ba med pa'i rnams/ /de dag 'jig rten mgon por 'gyur/ /bskal pa phyi ma'i mthar thugs pa/ /rgyal ba re re mchod byed kyang / /gang gi sems la skyo med na/ /de dag de bzhin gshegs
171a2(phal chen): par 'gyur/ /dus gsum gshegs pa'i mgon po kun/ /khyod kyi smon lam dbang gis bstsal/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi 'khor rnams ni/ /khyod kyi lus kyang rab tu gnas/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi smon lam
171a3(phal chen): dag / mtha' dang dbus med rgya mtsho la/ /blo chen gang rnams 'jugs pa na/ /de dag tshul 'di gnas par 'gyur/ /de la mchod pa byas pas kyang / /gzi brjid chen po stobs chen gyis/ /sems can ri
171a4(phal chen): rab rdul mnyam par/ /byang chub yongasu smin par byas/ /byang chub sems dpa' grags chen dag /kun tu bzang po dpa' ba'i rnams/ /chos kyi dbyings ni kun bkang zhing / /zhing gi rgya mtsho dag par byed/ /
171a5(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la bskal pa rgya chen po rig pa zhes bya ba de la bskal pa bar ma chu klung gang ga'i bye ma snyed gcig byung ste/ de'i dus na mi rnams kyi tshe yang bskal pa bar ma gnyis thub par gyur te/
171a6(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin gshegs pa yon tan thams cad kyi ri/ ri rab dpal gyi spyan de'i sku tshe'i tshad ni lo bye ba phrag lnga bcur gyur to/ /de yongasu mya ngan las 'das nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa pha rol
171a7(phal chen): tu phyin pa'i spyan bzang po'i rgyan gyi rgyal po zhes bya ba 'jig rten du nags tshal chen po yal ga'i dkyil 'khor rin po che'i me tog rgyas pa de nyid la byung te/ de bzhin gshegs pa pha rol tu phyin pa'i spyan
171a8(phal chen): bzang po rgyan gyi rgyal po de mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa rgyal bu gzhon nu gzi brjid chen pos mthong ngo / /mthong nas kyang sgo rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa'i snying po zhes bya ba rab tu thob bo/ /
171b1(phal chen): ye shes rgya chen po byin gyis rlabs dang chos kyi glong gi gzungs kyang rab tu thob bo/ /kun gyi rjes su song bar 'gro ba 'dul ba'i rnam par thar pa zhes bya ba'i byams pa chen po yang rab tu thob bo/ /dmigs pa'i
171b2(phal chen): sgo'i sprin thams cad kyis rgyas par byed pa zhes bya ba'i snying rje chen po yang rab tu thob bo/ /sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yon tan rgya mtsho dang byin gyis rlabs kyi mdzod ces bya ba'i dga' ba chen po yang rab tu thob bo/ /
171b3(phal chen): chos kyi rang bzhin namakha'i dbyings rnam par dag pa zhes bya ba'i btang snyoms chen po yang rab tu thob bo/ /rang bzhin dri ma med pa'i chos kyi dbyings yongasu dag pa'i lus shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yang rab tu thob bo/ /
171b4(phal chen): tshogs pa med pa'i dbyings rnam par snang ba'i rjes su song ba zhes bya ba'i mngon par shes pa yang rab tu thob bo/ /rab tu khong du chud pas dri ma med pa'i glong la yang dag par 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i tha dad pa'i
171b5(phal chen): yang dag par shes pa yang rab tu thob bo/ /sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos dkyil 'khor yongs su dag par byed pa zhes bya ba'i ye shes snang ba yang rab tu thob bo/ /de dag la stsogs pa chos kyi sgo stong
171b6(phal chen): phrag bcu kun nas non par gyur te/ de nas rgyal bu gzhon nu gzi brjid chen pos sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyi 'khor gyi tshogs thams cad la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ bskal pa bye ba
171b7(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab du/ /'jig rten gtso bo'i dam pa shin tu dkon/ /sangs rgyas zhing 'di sems can thob par thob/ /de dag sangs rgyas gnyis pa 'di yang mthong / /sangs rgyas sku las 'od rnams
171b8(phal chen): rab bkye ba/ /kha dog mtha' yas rgya mtsho rnam par dag /'od zer spyan gyis 'jig rten kun tu khyab/ /kun tu rgyal ba'i yon tan grags par byed/ /'od kyi rig pa rmad kyi dga' ba skye/ /'gro ba de dag
172a1(phal chen): kun gyi sdug bsngal zhi/ /phun tshun srid zhu byams pa'i sems gyur cing / /sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul 'di dag kun kyang mthong / /sprul pa'i sprin rnams bsam mi khyab/ /rnam pa du ma'i 'od kyi dra
172a2(phal chen): ba 'gyed/ /phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams kun kyang gang byas shing / /sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa rab tu ston/ /rgyal ba rnams kyi spu rtse re re nas/ /dbyangs sprin bkye bas namakha' kun bkang zhing / /mun
172a3(phal chen): nag chen po kun nas snang bar byed/ /dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal kun kyang rnam par sel/ /sangs rgyas dbyangs ni phyogs rnams bcu po ni/ /sems can rnams kyi sngon dge rgya mtsho rnams/ /thams
172a4(phal chen): cad dbyangs kyi kun tu sgra yang sgrog / sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa de dag ltos/ /sangs rgyas 'khor rnams rgya mtsho rgya che ba/ /mtha' dang dbus med yang dag rab tu byung / /de na rgyal ba chos kyi 'khor
172a5(phal chen): lo bskor/ /sems can rgya mtsho mi zad rnams kyang 'dul/ /tshad med rnam par 'phrul pa dag la ltos/ /zhing rnams kun na rgyal ba mngon par bzhugs/ /de ltar bde gshegs ye shes chags pa med/ /
172a6(phal chen): sems can don du rnam par mngon sangs rgyas/ /dga' zhing mos par kun kyang 'ong bar gyis/ /bde ba'i yid dang srid zhu spro ba yis/ /bde gshegs de ni blta ba'i phyir 'dong ngo / /de mthong sdug bsngal tha~Ms
172a7(phal chen): cad zhi bar 'gyur/ /byang chub sems ni yang dag bskyed byas shing / /'gro ba kun la byams pa'i sems gyur te/ /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam kun btab cing / /chos rgyal ji bzhin bdag cag 'gyur bar bya/ /
172a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis de'i sgra la thog pa med pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du khyab par gyur te/ de thos pa'i sems can tshad med pa rnams kyang byang chub tu smon lam btab par gyur
172b1(phal chen): to/ /de nas pha dang ma dang lhan cig tu 'khor thams cad dang / sems can bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong de dag gis bskor cing mdun du byas te/ rin po che'i gdugs kyi sprin lngas namakha' thams cad kun nas
172b2(phal chen): yog par byas te/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der dong ngo / /'ongs pa de dag la bcom ldan 'das pha rol tu phyin pa'i spyan bzang po brgyan gyi rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pas chos kyi dbyings rang bzhin
172b3(phal chen): dri ma med pa'i rgyan ces bya ba'i mdo 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi mdo'i 'khor can yang dag par bstan to/ /des de thos nas tshul thams cad rnam par dag pa la 'jug pas 'byung
172b4(phal chen): ba rab tu skyes so/ /ye shes kyi rim pa rnam par dag cing dri ma med pa'i snang ba zhes bya ba yang non par gyur to/ /pha rol tu phyin pa'i dkyil 'khor 'gro ba thams cad dga' bar lta ba'i rgyan ces bya bar
172b5(phal chen): yang zhugs par gyur to/ /zhing thams cad du yang dag par 'jug pa dang snang ba mtha' yas pa mthong bas rnam par dag pa'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor la yang rab tu zhugs so/ /spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor
172b6(phal chen): bsod nams kyi sprin dri ma med pa'i 'od kyi rgyal mtshan ces bya ba la yang rab tu zhugs par gyur to/ /rjes su rtog pa'i dkyil 'khor chos rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa thams cad snang ba zhes bya ba yang rjes su
172b7(phal chen): rtog par gyur to/ /'jug pa'i dkyil 'khor ye shes chen po'i shugs kyi rgyan ces bya ba la yang rab tu zhugs so/ /rang 'byung du 'gyur ba shin tu mthong ba'i shugs kyis dbang skur ba'i ye shes rgya mtsho
172b8(phal chen): la yang zhugs par gyur to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho'i mtshan nyid kyi 'od rnam par snang ba chen pos kyang shin tu snang bar gyur to/ /smon lam gyi stobs tshad med pa la mos pa rgya mtsho'i snying po'i
173a1(phal chen): smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes kyi stobs la yang rnam par dag par gyur to/ /de nas de bzhin gshegs pa pha rol tu phyin pa'i spyan bzang po rgyan gyi rgyal pos/ byang chub sems
173a2(phal chen): dpa' gzi brjid chen po la tshigs su bcad de gsungs pa/ legaso yon tan ye shes rgya mtsho can/ /sangs rgyas byang chub smon lam yang dag gnas/ /sems can kun gyi mgon dang gnas gyur pa/ /
173a3(phal chen): rgyal ba dam pa bsam gyis mi khyab 'gyur/ /ye shes rgya mtsho chen por mngon par byung / /chos kyi dbyings su thams cad rgyas byas te/ /sangs rgyas spyod yul rgya chen mi zad pa'i/ /bsam gyis myi
173a4(phal chen): khyab tshul la 'jug par 'gyur/ /sangs rgyas thams cad yon tan sprin mthong ba'i/ /ye shes su yang mi zad non par gyur/ /pha rol phyin pa rgya mtsho kun gyi tshul/ /grags pa chen po yongs su rgyas
173a5(phal chen): par byed/ /gzungs kyi tshul rnams rgya mtsho mang po dang / /tha dad yang dag shes tshul mi zad dang / /spyod pa smon lam khyod kyis mngon bsgrubs pas/ /gzhal med ye shes ldan par khyod 'gyur ro/ /ting nge
173a6(phal chen): 'dzin gyi rgya mtshor 'jug par 'gyur/ /smon lam rgya mtsho'i nang du khyod skyes te/ /rnam 'phrul 'di langs shin tu 'byung bar 'gyur/ /'di ni sangs rgyas chos nyid bsam mi khyab/ /chos dbyings dam pa
173a7(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i/ /bsam pa rgya chen rnam par sbyangs byas te/ /sangs rgyas sprin la rnam par blta bar gyis/ /rgya mtsho'i zhing rnams dri med rnam par sbyongs/ /nga'i byang chub spyod la 'jug par
173a8(phal chen): gyis/ /sngon gyi sbyor tshul rgya mtsho mang po yi/ /spyod pa ngas ni ji ltar rnam sbyangs pa/ /de 'dra'i tshul yang khyod kyi shes par gyis/ /zhing rnams re rer sangs rgyas mang po ngas/ /rgya mtsho brgya mang shin tu
173b1(phal chen): mchod pa byas/ /sngon spyod de yi 'bras bu 'di yin to/ /'di 'dra dri ma med pa'i rgyan la ltos/ /las kyi rgya mtsho mi zad rgya chen dang / /zhing rnams rgya mtsho dag bya'i spyod pa dang / /smon lam bsam
173b2(phal chen): yas go ca bgos pas na/ /'di rnams 'di 'dra'i rnam par 'phrul par 'gyur/ /sangs rgyas rgya mtsho ma lus mchod byas shing / /zhing rnams rgya chen rgya mtsho sbyangs byas nas/ /bskal pa 'byam klas kun
173b3(phal chen): tu sbyangs byas shing / /rgyal ba yon tan rin chen mnga' bar 'gyur/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin gshegs pa pha rol tu phyin pa'i spyan bzang po rgyan gyi rgyal po de yongasu mya ngan las 'das nas blta na dga' ba
173b4(phal chen): shin tu gtsang ba'i bdag po de yang dus byas par gyur te/ rgyal bu gzhon nu gzi brjid chen pos 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal srid thob par gyur to/ /nags tshal chen po yal ga'i dkyil 'khor rin po che'i
173b5(phal chen): me tog rgyas pa zhes bya ba der yang de bzhin gshegs pa bsod nams rgya mtsho shin tu 'phags shing zil gyi mi non pa zhes bya ba gsum pa byung bar gyur te/ des de bzhin gshegs pa de mngon par 'tshang rgya
173b6(phal chen): ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa ma thob nas/ 'khor thams cad dang dpung gi yan lag bzhi'i tshogs dang / rin po che bdun dang / grong gi myi dang yul mir bcas te/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
173b7(phal chen): pa bsod nams rgya mtsho shin tu 'phags shing zil gyi mi non pa gang na bzhugs pa der dong nas/ des bcom ldan 'das de la rin po che'i khang pa brtsegs pa/ spos dang nor bu thams cad kyi rgyan gyi
173b8(phal chen): snying po zhes bya ba phul lo/ /der de bzhin gshegs pa des kun tu blta ba'i spyod pa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa snang ba zhes bya ba'i mdo/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
174a1(phal chen): kyi mdo'i 'khor dang bcas pa'ang yang dag par bshad par gyur to/ /des thos nas byang chub sems dpa' gzi brjid chen pos/ bsod nams chen po rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
174a2(phal chen): rab tu thob po/ /ting nge 'dzin de thob nas kyang dus gsum gyi byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi bsod nams rgya mtsho mngon du gyur to/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa bsod nams
174a3(phal chen): rgya mtsho shin tu 'phags shing zil gyi mi non pas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la rnam par gzigs te/ byang chub sems dpa' gzi brjid chen po la tshigs su bcad de gsungs pa/
174a4(phal chen): yon tan bsod nams kun gyi gzi brjid can/ /byang chub mchog gi smon lam yid ldan pa/ /'gro ba kun la snying rje rgya mtsho yis/ /nga yi drung du khyod 'ongs legaso legs/ /snying rje'-i snying po khyod
174a5(phal chen): ni sems can rnams/ /sdug bsngal gyur pa kun tu grol zhugs pas/ /'gro ba kun gyi mgon dang skyabs su 'gyur/ /byang chub spyod pa'i tshul yang de yin no/ /byang chub sems dpa' shin tu
174a6(phal chen): brtan pa rnams/ /skyo med yid kyis spyad pa spyod pa dag /mchog tu gyur cing dam pa chags med pa/ /ye shes 'di 'dra shin tu thob par 'gyur/ /de ltar khyod ni kun tu bzang po yi/ /mthu chen
174a7(phal chen): smon lam spyod par zhugs pa ni/ /bsod nams 'od dang bsod nams dpal yin te/ /bsod nams 'byung gnas mchog kyang yin/ /bsam gyis myi khyab rgyal ba rgya mtsho dag /mtha' dang
174a8(phal chen): dbus med pa ni khyod kyi shes/ /mtha' dang dbus med de dag mthong gyur nas/ /de dag bsod nams rgya mtsho rtog par 'gyur/ /khyod kyi phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams thams cad kyi/ /rgyal ba'i
174b1(phal chen): sprin rnams kun kyang shin tu thos/ /de dag spyod pa rgya mtsho thams cad kyang / /sngon chad ji ltar spyad pa bzhin du mthong / /'di tshul rgya mtsho 'di la su zhugs shing / /ye shes sa la su dag gnas gyur
174b2(phal chen): pa/ /de dag sangs rgyas kun gyi rjes slob cing / /thams cad gzigs par gdon myi za bar 'gyur/ /khyod ni zhing kun rgya mtsho'i rdul snyed kyi/ /bskal pa rgya mtshor spyod pa rab spyod nas/ /rgyal ba kun
174b3(phal chen): gyi sngon spyad rgya mtsho rnams/ /bslabs nas rang byung nyid du 'gyur bar 'ongs/ /zhing rnams rgya mtsho yongs su dag pa rnams/ /phyogs bcu dag tu ji ltar mthong ba bzhin/ /khyod kyi zhing yang rnam par

185a3(phal chen): thob par 'gyur ba sha stag ste/ dus gsum thams cad du thogs pa med pa'i ye shes la rnam par spyod pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang ldan pa
185a4(phal chen): sha stag go/ /ci'i phyir na bza' shing gi ra ba mya ngan dang bral ba de la/ mya ngan dang bral ba zhes bya zhe na/ shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams mya ngan dang bral ba zhes bya ba na/ de bzhin gshegs
185a5(phal chen): pa mya ngan dang bral ba zhes bya ba bzhugs ste/ de dang mthun pa'i rgyus grub pas de'i phyir na bza' shing gi ra ba mya ngan dang bral ba zhes bya'o/ /de dag la sogs pa bza' shing gi ra ba mya ngan dang bral
185a6(phal chen): ba de ni/ yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan pa ste/ mdor na grong rdal mdzod mtha' yas pa na/ yon tan gang ji snyed yod pa de snyed kyi yon tan ni bza' shing gi ra ba mya ngan dang bral ba de na yod do/ /
185a7(phal chen): bza' shing gi ra ba mya ngan dang bral ba de'i nang na khang pa brtsegs pa kun nas smad du med pa zhes bya ba 'jig rten gyi khams rang bzhin chos nyid kyis gnas pa'i dbyibs su 'dug pa khang pa brtsegs pa
185a8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor dang ldan pa yod de/ khang pa brtsegs pa kun nas smad du med pa de ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yon tan rin po che sna tshogs
185b1(phal chen): kyi rang bzhin rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed las byung ba'o/ /sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi bsam pa sna tshogs rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu
185b2(phal chen): yi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi snying po dang ldan pa'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing sna tshogs dam pa'i rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rjes 'dong ba'o/ /khang pa brtsegs pa kun
185b3(phal chen): nas smad du med pa der sems can gang ji snyed skyes pa de dag thams cad kyang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes gang chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad kyi ye shes sgyu ma rgya mtsho bcu'i
185b4(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sprul pa/ ye shes sgyu ma rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rnam par bsgrub pa/ ye shes sgyu ma rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i
185b5(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa thob pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs yongasu bsgrubs pa
185b6(phal chen): gang ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad kyi/ sems can de dag gi ba spu'i bu ga re re nas mngon par grub pa sha stag go/ /ci'i phyir na khang pa brtsegs pa kun nas smad du med pa de la kun nas smad du med pa
185b7(phal chen): zhes bya zhe na/ chos kyi dbyings 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir te/ de'i phyir khang pa brtsegs pa kun nas smad du med pa zhes bya'o/ /de ltar
185b8(phal chen): de dag las sogs pa khang pa brtsegs pa kun nas smad du med pa de ni yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan pa ste/ mdor na bza' shing gi ra ba mya ngan dang bral ba na yon tan gang ji snyed yod pa de snyed kyi
186a1(phal chen): yon tan ni bza' shing gi rab kun nas smad du med pa de na yod do/ /de lta bu'i pho brang brtsegs pa kun nas smad du med pa de na/ byang chub sems dpa' ye shes kyi rdo rje'i lhun dang ldan pa'i seng ge'i
186a2(phal chen): khri'i rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar
186a3(phal chen): byung ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi rnam pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis kun nas bskor cing 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba rang sangs rgyas
186a4(phal chen): kyi 'khor gyi rnam pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi kun nas bskor te/ 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos kyis 'khor gyi rnam pa rgya
186a5(phal chen): mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi bskor cing / de bzhin du lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang nam mkha' lding dang / mi'am ci dang lto 'phye chen
186a6(phal chen): po dang / myi dang myi ma yin pa 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i 'khor rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis kun nas bskor cing bzhugs
186a7(phal chen): so/ /rnam par spyod do byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho nas/ myi dang myi ma yin gyi 'khor rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho'i bar 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba de dag las
186a8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' de dag re re zhing yang byang chub sems dpa' 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i 'khor rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor
186b1(phal chen): dang ldan pa rang sangs rgyas 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor dang ldan pa/ nyan thos 'das pa dang

186b3(phal chen): ma yin dang nam mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang lto 'phye chen po dang / myi dang myi ma yin pa 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i 'khor rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
186b4(phal chen): bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor dang / de ltar 'khor gyi gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' rgya

186b6(phal chen): pa tha dad pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang ldan pa sha stag te/ lus rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu
186b7(phal chen): phra ba snyed de dag las lus re re la yang / mgo rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod do/ /mgo rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi
186b8(phal chen): khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed po de dag las mgo re re la yang mig gi dbang po rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod do/ /de bzhin du rna ba
187a1(phal chen): dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi dbang po rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho'i bar du yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod de/ mig gi dbang po rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho
187a2(phal chen): ' jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed nas yid kyi dbang po rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho'i bar 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed po de dag la dbang po ji snyed cig yod
187a3(phal chen): pa de dag las dbang po re re la yang mig gi rnam par shes pa'i rnam par rtog pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod do/ /de bzhin du rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid
187a4(phal chen): kyi rnam par shes pa'i rnam par rtog pa rgya mtsho'i bar du 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod do/ /mig gi rnam par shes pa'i rnam par rtog pa rgya mtsho nas yid kyi rnam

187a7(phal chen): cig yod pa de dag las ye shes re res kyang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho mang po'i sangs rgyas tha dad pa rgya mtsho'i ye shes rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho'i tshul du chos kyi 'khor lo rnam pa tha dad pa rgya mtsho 'jig
187a8(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu bskor bar byed do/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams la ji lta ba de bzhin du rang sangs rgyas dang / de bzhin du nyan thos dang de bzhin lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang
187b1(phal chen): dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang mi dang mi ma yin pa rnams la 'ang shes par bya ste/ ye shes la ji lta ba de bzhin du chos thams cad la yang shes
187b2(phal chen): par bya'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang myi dang mi ma yin pa'i bar de dag gi gnas kyi yon tan rnam par phye ba rgya mtsho ji snyed cig yod pa dang / stan gyi yon tan rnam par phye ba ji snyed cig
187b3(phal chen): yod pa dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po'i yon tan rnam par phye ba ji snyed cig yod pa dang / rgyan gyi yon tan rnam par phye ba rgya mtsho ji snyed cig yod pa dang / gos kyi yon tan rnam par phye ba rgya mtsho ji snyed
187b4(phal chen): cig yod pa de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa' nas mi dang mi ma yin pa'i bar de dag gi mig gi rdul shin tu phra ba re re nas lus kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed re re zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyas
187b5(phal chen): par 'gengs pa de dag ni/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi bskal pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du bstan
187b6(phal chen): cing brjod kyang zad par mi rung ngo / / //sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po/ bam po bcu bzhi pa/ bcom ldan
187b7(phal chen): 'das ye shes gangs can mtsho rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i ba spu'i bu ga re re nas kyang 'od zer rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bkye'o/ /'od zer rgya mtsho de dag
187b8(phal chen): re re las kyang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho pad mo rgya mtsho la bzhugs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mngon par byung ste/ sangs rgyas re re'i sku'i ba spu'i sgo re re nas
188a1(phal chen): kyang yang dag par bskul ba'i tshigs su bcad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mngon par mthon to/ /de dag las yang dag par bskul ba'i tshigs
