188a3(phal chen): dpa' rgya mtsho ji snyed cig yod pa dang / rang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho dang / nyan thos rgya mtsho ji snyed cig yod pa dang / lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang nam mkha' lding dang /

188a6(phal chen): bskul nas/ rang rang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rgya mtsho dag nas/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho gang bzhugs pa de dag la zhus te/ gnang nas byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho re re dang myi dang myi ma yin pa rgya
188a7(phal chen): mtsho'i bar de dag re re zhing byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor rgya mtsho nas/ mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'khor rgya mtsho'i bar dang ldan par 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag gi mthil gyi snying
188a8(phal chen): po la rab tu gnas pa gang na ba der 'dong bar gyur to/ /byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho de dag dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa rgya mtsho'i bar de dag la byang chub sems dpa' ji snyed cig yod pa de dag las byang chub sems
188b1(phal chen): dpa' re re dang / myi dang myi ma yin pa'i bar de dag re re zhing yang / lus rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang ldan pa sha stag ste/ lus re re la yang lag pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten

188b7(phal chen): yang bstod pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi mngon par bstod nas/ rang rang gi stobs dang rdzu 'phrul gyis sprul pa'i stan rgya mtsho dag la 'khod par gyur to/ /

189a1(phal chen): snang mdzad des zhus pa de dag re re la shin tu bstan pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi shin tu bstan pa mdzad de/ byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho dang / myi dang

189a3(phal chen): bstan to/ /de nas shar phyogs su 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad kyi gnas kyi

189a5(phal chen): dge ba'i chos don bzang po/ yi ge bzang po dag pa yongs su gsal ba/ yongs su byang ba/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa yang dag par ston cing / byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho

189a7(phal chen): ji snyed cig mtha' yas pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi yon tan rnam par phye ba rgya mtsho ji snyed cig mnga' ba dang / sku tshe yon tan rnam par phye ba rgya mtsho ji snyed cig mnga' ba dang / sems can
189a8(phal chen): yongs su smin par mdzad pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho ji snyed cig mnga' ba dang / sku yongs su bstan pa'i yon tan rnam par phye ba rgya mtsho ji snyed cig mnga' ba dang / chos bstan pa'i yon tan rnam par phye
189b1(phal chen): ba rgya mtsho ji snyed cig mnga' ba de dag ni/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis/ dus gsum rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams
189b2(phal chen): rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du gsungs te/ bstan kyang zad par mi rung ngo / /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad kyi gnas kyi snying po zhes bya ba de na 'khor los
189b3(phal chen): bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rin chen mang po zhes bya ba 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bdag po lha dang myi'i dbang po yod de/ 'jig rten gyi

189b5(phal chen): chen mang po de'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho re re na yang rin po che rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod de/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas kyi spyan rin po che rgya mtsho dang /
189b6(phal chen): de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi snyan dang / shangs dang ljags dang sku dang thugs rin po che rgya mtsho dang / sangs rgyas kyi gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos rin po che rgya mtsho
189b7(phal chen): dang / thams cad kyis blta na yid du 'ong ba'i bud med rin po che rgya mtsho dang / don thams cad grub pa'i khyim bdag rin po che rgya mtsho dang / kun tu rnam par phye ba'i blon po rin po che rgya mtsho dang / nam
189b8(phal chen): mkha'i mthas klo ba'i rta rin po che rgya mtsho dang / yid bzhin du 'gro ba'i glang po rin po che rgya mtsho dang / chos kyi dbyings rdo rje'i lte ba can gyi 'khor lo rin po che rgya mtsho dang / kun tu snang
190a1(phal chen): bar byed pa'i yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che rgya mtsho dang / nam mkha' rgyan gyis 'gengs pa'i gdugs rin po che rgya mtsho dang / rang bzhin gyis dri ma med pa'i gos rin po che rgya mtsho dang zla ba'i
190a2(phal chen): cha zer lta bu'i rdul yab rin po che rgya mtsho dang / shes rab kyi ral gri rin po che rgya mtsho dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyi ltar myi mthong ba'i spyi tsug bsgribs pa med pa rin po che rgya mtsho dang / thams cad du 'gro
190a3(phal chen): ba'i lham rin po che rgya mtsho dang / ting nge 'dzin dang mnyam par bzhags pa thams cad kyi mdzod du gyur pa'i ting nge 'dzin rin po che rgya mtsho dang / chos gangs chen mtsho thams cad kyi klong dang ldan pa'i
190a4(phal chen): gzungs rin po che rgya mtsho dang / de ltar de dag las sogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho re re na yang rin po che rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod de rin po che rgya
190a5(phal chen): mtsho de dag la rin po che ji snyed cig yod pa de dag las rin po che re re zhing yang las 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byed pa sha stag go/ /'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rin po
190a6(phal chen): che mang po de la bu rgya mtsho kun kyang myi chen po'i mtshan rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang ldan pa/ 'od chen po'i rgyan rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i
190a7(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang ldan pa/ lus dpe byad bzang po rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis rab tu brtsal bar brgyan pa/ phas kyi rgol ba'i sde 'jig rten
190a8(phal chen): gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu 'joms pa/ sa bcu rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la rab tu gnas pa/ dpa' bar
190b1(phal chen): 'gro ba'i ting nge 'dzin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu thob pa/ snying po byang chub kyi rgyan rnam par phye ba'i ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin
190b2(phal chen): tu phra ba snyed yongs su gnon pa la mkhas pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod do/ /'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rin po che mang po de la bu mo rgya mtsho kun kyang byang
190b3(phal chen): c hub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis sprul pa'i bud myed rin po che dang 'dra bar yid kyi lus 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin
190b4(phal chen): tu phra ba snyed dang ldan pa srid pa'i lam gyi rgyud kyi 'khor lo sna tshogs rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang ldan pa/ byang chub kyi sems bla na myed pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten

190b6(phal chen): bsam pa dang lhag pa'i bsam pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi smin tshugs can/ shes rab dang ye shes yangs pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul
190b7(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed kyi myig dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad las thos pa 'dzin pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rna ba yid du 'ong ba dang ldan pa/ sdom pa
190b8(phal chen): chen po yang dag par blangs pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sna legs pa dang ldan pa/ chos rgya mtsho rab tu sgrog pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul

191a2(phal chen): byams pa chen po dang snying rje chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi lag pa dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad kyi don yongs su bsgrubs pas myi ngoms pa rgya mtsho 'jig

191a4(phal chen): dang ldan pa chos zab mo sna tshogs rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi lte ba dang ldan pa/ dmyigs pa thams cad yongs su bstsal ba'i mthar thug pa/ rgya mtsho 'jig
191a5(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rjes su rtog pa dang ldan pa/ rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin yangs shing mi shigs la brtan pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi
191a6(phal chen): sta zur dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa thams cad rim gyis legs par 'brel ba rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rkang pa dang ldan pa/ byang chub kyi yan lag gi me tog
191a7(phal chen): sna tshogs kyi dra ba dang phreng ba rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mdzes par thogs pa/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi rnam par
191a8(phal chen): thar pa'i gos rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed shin tu bzang bar gyon pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi rgyan rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams
191b1(phal chen): rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis legs par brgyan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul khrims dri zhim po rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi spos kyis lus shin tu
191b2(phal chen): byugs pa/ dga' ba'i rgyan dang thabs mkhas pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog thob pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin
191b3(phal chen): phra ba snyed yod do/ de dag gi kha nas ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i chos rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'byung ngo / /de dag gi lus kyi ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas kyang
191b4(phal chen): snying rje'i rjes su 'brang ba'i tsan dan gyi spos rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'byung ngo / /spos rgya mtsho de dag gi dri zhim pos kyang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i
191b5(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho mang po yongs su rgyas par 'gengs te/ de dag gi dga' ba'i rgyan dang / thabs mkhas pa rgya mtshos 'dul ba'i sems can rgya mtsho gang ji snyed
191b6(phal chen): yod pas dri zhim po rgya mtsho de dag tshor bar gyur pa de dag thams cad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul khrims dri zhim po rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu thob bo/ /
191b7(phal chen): sems can gang dga' ba'i rgyan dang thabs mkhas pa rgya mtshos 'dul ba de dag gis gzugs kyi yon tan rnam par phye ba rgya mtsho de dag mthong ba de thams cad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i shes rab
191b8(phal chen): dang ye shes kyi sku rnam par dag yongs su ston pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu thob bo/ /gang gis dbyangs rgya mtsho thos par gyur pa de dag thams cad kyang /
192a1(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad las thos pa yongs su 'dzin pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu 'thob bo/ /gang gi lag na bzung ba de dag thams
192a2(phal chen): cad kyang byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen po rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu thob bo/ /gang gis mtha' la rig pa de dag thams cad kyang bsod nams dang ye
192a3(phal chen): shes sna tshogs kyi rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu 'thob bo/ /gang dang stan cig la lhan cig tu 'khod pa de dag thams cad kyang snying po byang chub kyi seng
192a4(phal chen): ge'i khri rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la rab tu gnas par 'gyur ro/ /gang gis kha dang khar phrad par byas pa de dag thams cad kyang rnam par thar pa'i sgo rgya
192a5(phal chen): mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu phra ba snyed rab tu thob bo/ /gang gis pang du khyud pa de dag thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi sku mnyam pa nyid rgya mtsho 'jig
192a6(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu thob bo/ /gang dang chos kyi dbyings su sten par gyur pa de dag thams cad kyang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho mang po 'jig rten gyi khams
192a7(phal chen): rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed na sems can gyi khams rgya mtsho gang ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad kyi bsam pa yongs su dag pa rgya mtsho la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs
192a8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu thob pa dang yongs su dag pa dang yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur bar sa bon rgya mtsho rab tu 'debs so/ /de nas 'khor los
192b1(phal chen): s gyur ba'i rgyal po rin po che mang po des yang dag par bskul ba'i tshigs su bcad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed thams cad du khyab pa'i rna ba rgya mtshos thos nas rdzu 'phrul
192b2(phal chen): gyi stobs rgya mtsho chags pa med cing sgribs pa med pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad kyi don gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad gang na ba der song ste phyin nas/ bcom ldan 'das
192b3(phal chen): de'i zhabs gnyis la mgo rgya mtsho'i spyi bos btud de phyag 'tshal nas/ chos kyi dbyings rab tu sgrog pa'i lce'i dbang po rgya mtshos zhu ba yongs su zhus pa bcom ldan 'das de ltar yang dag par bskul ba'i
192b4(phal chen): tshigs su bcad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ba de su'i mthu las byung ba lags/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams
192b5(phal chen): cad kyi don gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad kyi/ rgyal po rin po che mang po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ /rgyal po chen po 'di nas nub phyogs logasu 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul
192b6(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag gi mthil gyi snying po la rab tu gnas pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes gangs chen
192b7(phal chen): mtsho rnam par snang mdzad ces bya ba da ltar bzhugs shing mtsho skyong de chos ston to/ /yang dag par bskul ba'i tshigs su bcad pa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
192b8(phal chen): byung ba 'di yang de'i mthus byung ngo / /de nas rgyal po rin chen mang pos de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad kyi don gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad la 'di skad ces gsol to bcom ldan 'das
193a1(phal chen): bdag kyang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag gi mthil gyi snying po la rab tu gnas pa der/ de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad kyi zhal blta
193a2(phal chen): ba dang de la phyag bgyi ba dang / mchod pa dang bsnyen bkur ba dang / chos mnyan pa'i slad du mchi'o/ /de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad kyi don gangs chen

193a4(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag gi mthil gyi snying po la rab tu gnas pa der ni 'gro bar dka' ste/ der 'gro ba dang de bzhin gshegs pa de'i zhal blta ba dang / de la phyag bya ba dang / bsnyen bkur ba dang / chos mnyan
193a5(phal chen): par ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis rlabs ma gtog par/ byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin snying po byang chub kyi rgyan rnam par phye ba'i snying po rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra
193a6(phal chen): ba snyed la rab tu gnas pas kyang bde blag du bya bar sla ba ma yin gyi/ rgyal po chen po de lta ma yin pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho mtshams bzang po dbyangs zhes bya ba zhig yod do/ /de khyod kyis
193a7(phal chen): sngan bcad mthong ngam/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de phyogs ni gang na 'dug /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de 'di nas ni nye 'am ring / de na da ltar de bzhin gshegs pa gang zhig bzhugs shing mtsho
193a8(phal chen): skyong ba dang / chos ston pa mdzad pa shes sam/ rgyal po rin chen mang pos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das bdag gi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de mthong ba'am 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de phyogs gang na
193b1(phal chen): mchis pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de 'di nas ni nye 'am ring zhig na mchis pa dang / da ltar de na de bzhin gshegs pa gang bzhugs pa dang / 'tsho skyong zhing chos ston pa ni smos su 'ang ma mchis te/
193b2(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de ni sngon tshe bdag gi ma thos so/ /de nas de bzhin gshegs pa sems can gyi don gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad kyis/ rgyal po rin chen mang po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal
193b3(phal chen): to/ /rgyal po chen po 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de gang na yod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de 'di nas ji srid pa dang / de na da ltar de bzhin gshegs pa gang bzhugs shing 'tsho skyong ba dang chos
193b4(phal chen): ston pa legs par soms shig / de nas rgyal po rin chen mang pos 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du yongasu gzhon pa'i ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho las stsogs pa ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams
193b5(phal chen): rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la mnyam par bzhag kyang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de phyogs gang na yod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de 'di nas nye 'am ring ba dang / de na da ltar de
193b6(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa gang bzhugs shing 'tsho skyong ba dang / chos ston pa yang ma shes te/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de'i mtshan ma rtsam yang ma mthong ngo / /de nas rgyal po rin chen mang po ting nge 'dzin rgya
193b7(phal chen): mtsho de dag las langs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad kyi don gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad de la 'di skad ces gsol to/ /bcom ldan 'das bdag gis 'jig rten gyi khams
193b8(phal chen): rgya mtsho de mthong ba 'am/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de phyogs gang na mchis pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de 'di nas ring ngam nye ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gang zhig da ltar de na bzhugs
194a1(phal chen): shing 'tsho skyong ba dang / chos ston pa lta smos kyang ci 'tshal te/ bdag gis 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de'i mtshan ma tsam yang ma mthong ngo / /de nas de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad kyi
194a2(phal chen): don gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad kyis/ rgyal po rin chen mang po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ /de lta bas na rgyal po rnam grangs des kyang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de bzhin gshegs pa'i
194a3(phal chen): phyag gi mthil gyi snying po la rab tu gnas pa de de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis rlabs ma gtogs par/ ting nge 'dzin gyi snying po byang chub kyi rgyan rnam par phye ba snying po rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams
194a4(phal chen): rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtshos kyang 'gro bar bya ba 'am/ de bzhin gshegs pa blta ba 'am/ de la phyag bya ba 'am bsnyen bkur ba 'am de las chos
194a5(phal chen): mnyan pa bde blag ma yin par shes par gyis shig de nas rgyal po rin chen mang pos de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad kyi don gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad la 'di skad ces gsol to/ /
194a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das bstan tu gsol/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de ni phyogs gang na mchis/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de 'di nas ni thag ji srid cig na mchis/ de bzhin gshegs pa ni gang

194a8(phal chen): skad ces bka' stsal to/ /rgyal po chen po khyod kyis khams 'di nub phyogs logs kyi sa 'tshams kyi mtha' 'di nas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams klong gi rdul shin tu phra ba
194b1(phal chen): snyed 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho sa 'tshams bzang po'i dbyangs zhes bya ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa spyod pa thams cad dang myi mthun pa'i phyogs yang dag par bsgrub pa'i gangs
194b2(phal chen): chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad ces bya ba da ltar bzhugs shing 'tsho skyong ngo chos ston to/ /de nas de skad ces bka' stsal kyang / rgyal po rin chen mang pos 'jig rten gyi khams rgya rgya mtsho de ma shes ma
194b3(phal chen): mthong nas/ 'di snyam du bsamaso/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de de ltar nye na 'ang bdag la mthu'i khyed par myed na/ de bas ring ba lta ci smos snyam nas/ de ltar rjes su bsams
194b4(phal chen): te/ de'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis rlabs legs par len pa'i ting nge 'dzin kun tu sgrib pa myed pa las sogs pa ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin

194b8(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa spyod pa thams cad dang mi mthun pa'i phyogs yang dag par bsgrub pa'i gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag
195a1(phal chen): gi mthil gyi snying po la rab tu gnas pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes gangs chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad dang / de ma yin pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho

215b8(phal chen): phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang nub byang gi phyogs mtshams dang 'og gis phyogs dang steng gi phyogs dag tu yang 'jig rten gyi khams bcu bcu snang bar

220b7(phal chen): sems dpa' bcu bcu 'ongs par gyur to/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang ming 'di zhes bya ba dag ste/ 'di ltar 'jam dpal zhes bya ba nas bzang po'i dpal gyi bar dag go/ /byang chub sems
220b8(phal chen): dpa' de dag thams cad kyang 'jig rten gyi khams ming 'di zhes bya ba dag nas 'ongs pa dag ste/ 'di ltar gser gyi mdog ces bya ba nas 'dra ba'i mdog ces bya ba'i bar dag go/ /byang chub sems
221a1(phal chen): dpa' de dag thams cad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan 'di zhes bya ba dag gis zhabs ring na tshangs pa'i spyad pa spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ltar rig byed mi g.yo ba zhes bya ba nas
221a2(phal chen): rig byed sna tshogs shes bya ba'i bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
221a3(phal chen): dang lhan cig tu phyin pa dag ste/ gcig ji lta ba de bzhin thams cad do/ /thams cad na yang byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal zhes bya ba sha stag don 'di nyid brjod de/ gcig na ji lta
221a4(phal chen): ba de bzhin thams cad na yang brjod do/ /de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag kyang so so nas smra bar gyur to/ /mi 'dul kha lo bsgyur ba mthu chen la/ /gang dag kha dog rigs kyis lta 'dod pa/ /mig nyams
221a5(phal chen): log par blta bar gyur pa ste/ /de dag rgyal ba'i chos nyid mi shes so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i kha dog dbyibs dag ni/ /'jig rten dag na'ang shes par nus pa med/ /gang gis bskal pa bye bar bsam yas
221a6(phal chen): kyang / /mthu chen rnams kyi kha dog mtha' med do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan nyid mi mnga' ste/ /chos rnams thams cad mtshan nyid med cing dben/ /yan lag kun ldan blta na nyams
221a7(phal chen): med pa/ /bsam pa ji bzhin kun na rab tu snang / /sangs rgyas chos rnams gzhal du yod pa min/ /gang rnams ci yang 'di yi tshul bshad de/ /ldan pa ma yin mi ldan ma yin pas/ /
221a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas chos rnams rang bzhin rab tu dben/ /de bzhin gshegs pa phung po 'jigs pa med/ /'byung dang 'jig par spro bar mi mdzad de/ /mnga' brnyes mnga' bsgyur rnam par gdon mi za/ /brjod du
221b1(phal chen): med par bstan pa rnam par spyod/ /lus dang sems kyang mnyam par rab gyur cing / /nang dang phyi yis rnam par dben pas na/ /gnyis po bgrang du mi rung shes pa rnams/ /chags med bcings med bde bar
221b2(phal chen): gshegs par 'gyur/ /gya nom snang zhing thugs gsal 'od mdzad pa/ /spyod yul yongs dag kun tu snang gyur te/ /thams cad mkhyen pa kun gzigs kun na bzhugs/ /skye dgu'i don kyang rgya chen yangs
221b3(phal chen): pa mdzad/ /gcig tu gyur cing mang por rab tu gyur/ /mang por gyur cing gcig tu de bzhin 'gyur/ /'gro ba'i khams ni du mar thugs chud cing / /thams cad tshul dang 'dra bar rab tu 'gyur/ /sku med
221b4(phal chen): de la chags pa gang yang med/ /byon pa med cing bstsags pa yod ma min/ /kha dog mtha' yas rnam par dgod byas shing / /'gro ba sna tshogs lus su de dag snang / /'jig rten thams cad
221b5(phal chen): sems kyis brtags pa yin/ /sems ni rtog pa nam yang ma yin te/ /bde bar gshegs pa de 'dra'i rang bzhin no/ /de phyir rgyal ba'i sku ni 'di 'drar snang / /de nas 'od zer de dag 'jig rten gyi khams
221b6(phal chen): de dag nas 'das te/ shar phyogs logs su 'jig rten gyi khams brgya stong phrag bcur snang bar byas nas/ gzhung de bzhin du steng gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams brgya stong phrag bcu'i bar du snang
221b7(phal chen): bar byas te/ 'jig rten gyi khams re rer yang 'dzam bu'i gling bye ba phrag brgya bstan pa nas/ 'og min bye ba phrag brgya'i bar du bstan to/ /'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi khongs su gang ci yang rung ste gtogs
221b8(phal chen): par gyur pa de dag thams cad ril gyis bstan to/ /ji ltar bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi gdan la bzhugs shing / byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang thabs
222a1(phal chen): gcig par snang ba de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams re re'i gling bzhi pa bye ba phrag brgya dag na yang / de bzhin gshegs pa bye ba phrag brgya dag sangs rgyas kyi gdan la bzhugs par snang ste/ thams
222a2(phal chen): cad du yang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyi phyogs bcu nas byang chub sems dpa' bcu bcu 'ongs par gyur to/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang ming 'di zhes bya ba dag ste/ 'di ltar
222a3(phal chen): 'jam dpal zhes bya ba nas bzang po'i dpal gyi bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang 'jig rten gyi khams ming 'di zhes bya ba dag nas 'ongs pa dag ste/ 'di ltar gser gyi mdog ces
222a4(phal chen): bya ba nas 'dra ba'i mdog ces bya ba'i bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan 'di zhes bya ba dag gi zham ring na tshangs pa'i spyad pa spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ltar rig byed
222a5(phal chen): mi g.yo ba zhes bya ba nas rig byed sna tshogs shes bya ba'i bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin
222a6(phal chen): tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu phyin pa dag ste gcig ci lta ba de bzhin thams cad do/ /thams cad na yang byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal zhes bya ba sha stag don 'di nyid brjod do/ /gcig na ji lta ba de bzhin
222a7(phal chen): thams cad na yang brjod do/ /de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag kyang so so nas smra bar gyur to/ /'jig rten rang byung de las mchog med pa/ /mi gnas dam pa phul dang mchog gi rnams/ /drang srong chen po
222a8(phal chen): srid pa'i rgyud 'grel ba/ /yon tan kun ldan rnam dag 'di yin no/ /'du 'dzi med cing chags pa mi mnga' la/ /'du shes dngos med gnas pa med pa rnams/ /phun sum dge ldan smad pa mi mnga' ba/ /
222b1(phal chen): mgon po rnams kyi chos nyid thub par dka'/ /shin tu 'od snang dag par gyur pa rnams/ /brgal du glags med rnyog pa med pa'i rnams/ /g.yo med mtha' ma rnam par spangs pa yi/ /
222b2(phal chen): bde gshegs rnams kyi ye shes tshul 'di yin/ /lus dang sems la rnam par rtog med cing / /bde gshegs chos la gang zhig 'jug 'gyur ba/ /de dag chos rnams kun gyi rang bzhin la/ /nam yang
222b3(phal chen): nem nur dbang du mi 'gro ba/ /'jig rten dag na dmyigs pa gang yod pa/ /de dag kun la bstan pa'i chos 'jug ste/ /gang dag phyir rgol med pas bstan mdzad kyang / /rang bzhin ldog par
222b4(phal chen): 'gyur ba gang yang med/ /dngos po rab shes las rnams yod min par/ /the tsom thams cad rnam par spangs byas te/ /sangs rgyas byang chub rab tu rtogs pa'i tshe/ /sems la rnam
222b5(phal chen): par 'gyed pa gang yang med/ /mi shes chos rnams rnam par phye ba dag /byung med tshig gi lam gyis rab brjod pa/ /sangs rgyas gsung gi rjes su 'brangs byas na/ /gcig kyang ma yin
222b6(phal chen): mang po 'ang ma yin no/ /mang dang gcig pa nam yang yod min te/ /mang po rnams la gcig pa yod med do/ /mang dang gcig pa rnam par bsgom byas na/ /sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas
222b7(phal chen): shes par 'gyur/ /'jig rten kun tu sems can zhing rnams dang / /shin tu zhi ba'i chos rnams rnam bltas te/ /mi gnas sems la rtogs pa med pa yi/ /dran ldan
222b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas byang chub thob par 'gyur/ /sems can chos dang de bzhin zhing gi rnams/ /de dag rang bzhin ji bzhin brtag byas na/ /
223a1(phal chen): gcig dang tha dad gyur pa ma yin te/ /de ltar sangs rgyas tshul 'di shes pa yin/ /de nas 'od zer de dag 'jig rten gyi khams de dag nas 'das te/ shar phyogs logs su 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba
223a2(phal chen): phrag brgya snang bar byas pa nas/ steng gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba phrag brgya'i bar du snang bar byas te/ 'jig rten gyi khams re rer yang 'dzam bu'i gling bye ba phrag brgya bstan pa nas/ 'og min
223a3(phal chen): bye ba phrag brgya'i bar du bstan to/ /'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi khongs su gang ci yang rung ste/ gtogs par gyur pa de dag thams cad ril gyis bstan to/ /ji ltar bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi gdan
223a4(phal chen): la bzhugs shing byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang thabs gcig par snang ba de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams re re'i gling bzhi pa bye ba phrag brgya kun na yang / de bzhin
223a5(phal chen): gshegs pa bye ba phrag brgya dag sangs rgyas kyi gdan la bzhugs par snang ngo / /thams cad du yang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcu nas byang chub sems dpa' bcu bcu 'ongs par gyur to/ /
223a6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' de dag kyang ming 'di zhes bya ba dag ste/ 'di ltar 'jam dpal zhes bya ba nas bzang po'i dpal gyi bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad gang 'jig rten gyi khams
223a7(phal chen): ming 'di zhes bya ba dag nas 'ongs pa dag ste/ 'di ltar gser gyi mdog ces bya ba nas 'dra ba'i mdog ces bya ba'i bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan
223a8(phal chen): 'di zhes bya ba dag gi zham ring na tshangs pa'i spyad pa spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ltar rig byed mi g.yo ba zhes bya ba nas rig byed sna tshogs shes bya ba'i bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang
223b1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu phyin pa ste/ gcig ji lta ba de bzhin thams cad do/ /thams cad na yang byang chub sems dpa'
223b2(phal chen): 'jam dpal zhes bya ba sha stag don 'di nyid brjod de/ gcig na ji lta ba de bzhin thams cad na'ang brjod do/ /de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag so so nas smra bar gyur to/ /shes rab dpag med chos rnams
223b3(phal chen): mtha' yas pa/ /srid pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol phyin pa dag /tshe ring nad med mnyam med mtshungs med 'od/ /yon tan che mnga' de dag sbyor 'di'o/ /gang gis sangs rgyas chos rnams dngos rtogs shing / /
223b4(phal chen): dus gsum kun tu brtags kyang mi ngoms te/ /dmigs pa shes byed rnam par mi rtog pa/ /bsam yas mos pa de dag sbyor 'di yin/ /sems can yul mos sems can 'du shes med/ /
223b5(phal chen): 'jig tshogs chos shes lam gyi rgyud dang bral/ /bsam gtan nang dang sems la bcings pa med/ /chags med yid ldan de dag sbyor 'di yin/ /rtog mkhas rab tu rtogs pa'i chos can rnams/ /
223b6(phal chen): mya ngan 'das spyod rigs la brtson pa dag /thar pa'i lam brtson mnyam pa nyid ldan pa/ /zhi ba thob pa de dag sbyor 'di'o/ /ded dpon rjes song sangs rgyas byang chub mchog /thams cad mkhyen pa chos
223b7(phal chen): dbyings bzhin rtogs shing / /bden 'jug mkhas pas sems can rnams 'don pa/ /bde gshegs bsam can de dag sbyor 'di'o/ /sangs rgyas don tshig rjes su shes bya zhing / /chags med
223b8(phal chen): blo yangs rtogs shing bsam gtan byed/ /kun tu 'gro bar song las rtsol spyod pa/ /rang byung spyod pa de dag sbyor 'di'o/ /nam mkha'i dbyings dang sprul pa yid ldan rnams/ /
224a1(phal chen): gnas dang rang bzhin mtshan nyid shes pa dag /mya ngan 'das rigs spyod pa mkha' 'dra rnams/ /thob dka' thob pa rnams kyi sbyor 'di'o/ /zla ba zla phyed nyin dang nub bgrang zhing / /lo dang bskal pa'i rang bzhin
224a2(phal chen): su sems pa/ /'jig rten 'du zhing 'jig par 'gyur ba dang / /grangs tshul sus rtogs de dag sbyor 'di'o/ /zhing gi sems can ji snyed skye 'chi ba/ /gzugs dang gzugs med 'du shes 'du shes med/ /
224a3(phal chen): de dag ming dang gnas pa rtogs shes pa/ /bsam gyis mi khyab rtogs pa'i sbyor 'di'o/ /'das pa'i dus dang ma 'ongs da ltar la/ /ngag gis lam gyis gang na rtog byed cing / /dus gsum rang bzhin ji bzhin
224a4(phal chen): rtogs gyur pa/ /mnyam med de dag sbyor ba 'di yin no/ /de nas 'od zer de dag 'jig rten gyi khams de dag nas 'das te/ shar phyogs logasu 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba phrag bcu snang bar byas nas/
224a5(phal chen): steng gi phyogs su 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba phrag bcu'i bar du snang bar byas nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams re rer yang 'dzam bu'i gling bye ba phrag brgya bstan pa nas/ 'og min bye ba phrag brgya'i bar

224a8(phal chen): gshegs pa bye ba phrag brgya dag sangs rgyas kyi gdan la bzhugs par snang ngo / /thams cad du yang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcu nas byang chub sems dpa' bcu bcu 'ong par
224b1(phal chen): gyur to/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang ming 'di zhes bya ba dag ste/ 'di ltar 'jam dpal zhes bya ba nas bzang po'i dpal gyi bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang 'jig
224b2(phal chen): rten gyi khams ming 'di zhes bya ba dag nas 'ongs pa dag ste/ 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams gser gyi mdog ces bya ba nas 'dra ba'i mdog ces bya ba'i bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams
224b3(phal chen): cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan 'di zhes bya ba dag gi zham ring na tshangs pa'i spyad pa spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ltar rig byed mi g.yo ba zhes bya ba nas rig byed sna tshogs shes bya ba'i bar dag go/ /
224b4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang / byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / lhan cig tu phyin pa dag ste/ gcig ji lta ba
224b5(phal chen): de bzhin thams cad do/ /thams cad na yang byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal zhes bya ba sha stag don 'di nyid brjod de/ gcig ji lta ba de bzhin thams cad na yang brjod do/ /de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa
224b6(phal chen): 'di dag kyang so so nas smra bar gyur to/ /'das dus gang gis bsgrub dka'i brtul zhugs che brtsams shing / /nam yang zhum pa'i sems su gtong bar mi byed do/ /brgal dka' rgal te bdag gis sems can
224b7(phal chen): kun 'dul zhes/ /seng ge'i sgra sgrog de dag spyod yul 'di yin no/ /gang zhig 'dod dang sred pa 'byung zhing 'jug pa dang / /ma rig gzhol ba gti mug mun sgrib 'jig rten rnams/ /sems can rang bzhin
224b8(phal chen): bdag med brtan pa bzod par 'gyur/ /bdag kyang 'jig rten mgon 'gyur zhes pa de yul 'di/ /'jig rten sems can mang po 'dod dregs 'dam bying ba/ /med pa'i chos la rtog pas sdug bsngal
225a1(phal chen): mthong gyur nas/ /sangs rgyas spyod yul chos la bag yod gang spyod cing / /bdag gi sems can kun bsgrub de dag spyod yul 'di/ /sngon mtha' shes dka' tshad med brtan pas mthong gyur cing / /
225a2(phal chen): bdag brtan sems can pha rol mtha' yas 'khor sgyur ba/ /de dag rgyal bas theg pa zhi ba mchog la bkod/ /bdag gi de 'dra'i chos bstan de yi spyod yul lo/ /sems can khams rnams mgon
225a3(phal chen): med nad kyis gzir gyur cing / /ngan song gzhol ba 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug gdungs/ /me lce 'bar phung 'jigs gzugs mi bzad bsregs gyur pa/ /mthong nas dgrol phyir zhugs pa de dag spyod yul
225a4(phal chen): 'di'o/ /lam gol lam ma yin pa'i rkyen la spyod gyur cing / /mun pa chen po rtol bar dka' rnyed 'go mthong nas/ /snang ba chen po bskyed de sangs rgyas chos ston ces/ /'di skad tshig brjod de dag spyod yul
225a5(phal chen): 'di yin no/ /srid pa'i mtshos g.yengs sems can rab tu mang ba dag /mtha' mi mthong zhing skyabs med do zhes mi dga' ba/ /mthong nas brtson 'grus stobs skyed chos kyi gru sbyar cing / /pha rol su 'gro zhes rjod
225a6(phal chen): de dag spyod yul 'di'o/ /sems can rtsa ba med la gnas pa mi mkhas kun/ /g.yang sa chen por ltung zhing sems nyams rmongs mthong nas/ /snying rjes chos kyi zam la mkhas pa su 'god cing / /dran par gyis
225a7(phal chen): shes su smra de dag spyod yul 'di'o/ /shin tu dog pa'i brtson rar sdug bsngal sems can rnams/ /nad dang dga' bas gzir cing tsam gyis mnar ba dag /mthong nas bdag gis thabs kyi chos rnams kun brtsams
225a8(phal chen): te/ /sems can kun dgrol sems pa de dag spyod yul 'di'o/ /sangs rgyas chos rnams thams cad thos gyur the tsom med/ /chos dbyings spyod yul phyogs bcu kun tu rgyas bkang ste/ /'di dag thams cad rtags na
225b1(phal chen): gsog kyang mi 'jigs shing / /sems can kun la snyoms byed de yi spyod yul lo/ /de nas 'od zer de dag 'jig rten gyi khams de dag nas 'das te/ shar phyogs logasu 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba phrag brgya snang
225b2(phal chen): bar byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams bye ba stong snang bar byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams bye ba brgya phrag stong snang bar byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams bye ba khrag khrig snang bar byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams bye ba khrag
225b3(phal chen): khrig stong snang bar byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong snang bar byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams tshad med pa snang bar byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams gzhal du med pa snang bar byas so/ /'jig
225b4(phal chen): rten gyi khams grangs med pa snang bar byas so/ de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams bsam gyis mi khyab pa mtshungs pa med pa kun tu mtha' yas pa/ mu med pa sa mtshams med pa dpag tu med pa brjod du med pa dag kyang snang bar
225b5(phal chen): byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi dbyings kyi klas pa namakha'i mthas gtugs pa thams cad kyang snang bar byas so/ /gzhung de bzhin du lho phyogs dang / de bzhin du nub phyogs dang / de bzhin du byang phyogs dang /
225b6(phal chen): de bzhin du byang shar kyi phyogs mtshams dang / de bzhin du shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / de bzhin du lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang / de bzhin du nub byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / de bzhin du 'og gi phyogs
225b7(phal chen): nas steng gi phyogs kyi bar du 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba snang bar byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams bye ba brgya snang bar byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams bye ba stong snang bar byas so/ nam mkha'i mthas gtugs
225b8(phal chen): pa'i bar gyis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar byas so/ /de ltar phyogs bcu shin tu rgyas par byas nas/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyang snang bar byas so/ /'jig rten gyi khams re rer yang
226a1(phal chen): 'dzam bu'i gling bye ba phrag brgya bstan pa nas/ gzhung de bzhin du 'og min bye ba phrag brgya'i bar du bstan to/ /'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi khongasu gang ci yang rung ste gtogs par gyur pa de dag thams
226a2(phal chen): cad kyang ril gyis bstan to/ /ji ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis gdan la bzhugs shing / byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang thabs cig par snang ba de bzhin
226a3(phal chen): du 'jig rten gyi khams re re'i gling bzhi pa bye ba phrag brgya kun tu yang / de bzhin gshegs pa bye ba phrag brgya dag sangs rgyas kyi gdan la bzhugs par snang ngo / /thams cad du yang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi
226a4(phal chen): rlabs kyis phyogs bcu nas byang chub sems dpa' bcu bcu 'ongs par gyur to/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang ming 'di zhes bya ba dag ste/ 'di ltar 'jam dpal zhes bya ba nas bzang
226a5(phal chen): po'i dpal gyi bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang 'jig rten gyi khams ming 'di zhes bya ba dag nas 'ongs pa ste/ 'di ltar gser gyi mdog ces bya ba nas 'dra ba'i mdog ces bya ba'i
226a6(phal chen): bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan 'di zhes bya ba dag gi zham ring na tshangs pa'i spyod pa spyad pa dag ste/ 'di ltar rig byed mi g.yo ba zhes bya ba nas/
226a7(phal chen): rig byed sna tshogs shes bya ba'i bar dag go/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang
226a8(phal chen): lhan cig tu phyin pa dag ste/ gcig ji lta ba de bzhin thams cad do/ /thams cad na yang byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal zhes bya ba sha stag don 'di nyid brjod de/ gcig na ji lta ba de bzhin
226b1(phal chen): thams cad na yang brjod do/ /de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag kyang so so nas smra bar gyur to/ /bskal pa gzhal yas bsam gyis mi khyab sems kyi skad cig la/ /gang gi mthong yang bstsags med
226b2(phal chen): 'gro dang dngos po'i tshul med pa'i/ /lam du 'jug pa de ni thams cad kun gyi shes 'gyur te/ /stobs bcus tshul 'di ji ltar mkhyen bzhin 'jigs med sangs rgyas 'gyur/ /grags pa snyan par phyogs
226b3(phal chen): rnams kun tu mtshungs med grags gyur cing / /bgegs rnams kun las 'das te chos nyid 'di la dgar spyad de/ /tshad med thams cad so sor zhi zhing don rnams kun rtogs pas/ /de phyir phyogs rnams kun
226b4(phal chen): bkang bde gshegs chos nyid 'di ston to/ /dgongs pa ji bzhin de ni spyod pa'i 'bras bu 'thun pa ste/ /'jig rten don 'gyur de bzhin gshegs la mchod pa yongs byas shing / /de dag thams cad so sor
226b5(phal chen): 'thun par ye shes rnam sgoms pas/ /sems can dam pa sangs rgyas rnams 'phrul 'di 'dra phyogs bcur bstan/ /thog mar nyan 'dod bla na med kun bzod pa des byas shing / /rang bzhin med pa'i chos la
226b6(phal chen): rab rtog bsam gtan bsnyen byed pa/ /bde gshegs nyid ni rtogs 'gyur 'gro ba rnam skom sems tshim byed/ /chos nyid de 'dra spyad pa myur du bde gshegs thob par 'gyur/ /snying nas 'dri zhing phyogs
226b7(phal chen): rnams rgyas byed rtse gcig thob byed cing / /rgyal ba'i yon tan mos las mi zlog spyod pas tshim byed pa/ /dngos dang dngos med thams cad shes byas spangs shing dngos zad pa/ /sangs rgyas bdag
226b8(phal chen): med dpe med mthong ba de dag lus 'di yin/ /bzang po'i spyod yul can gyi sems kyi phyogs rnams kun bkang zhing / /zhing rnams thams cad chos kyi gter gyis khyab byas tshim byed pa/ /
227a1(phal chen): ji bzhin ches gnas chos nyid mtha' la the tsom med pa'i rnams/ /stobs bcu ci 'dra de bzhin gyur pa'i lus ni 'di dag go/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis gsung gang sgra brjod de la 'jug byed
227a2(phal chen): cing / /chos kyi 'khor lo ji bzhin blta dka' gzhal yas rtag bskor ba/ /de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs pa'i gsung kun byang chub yan lag rtogs/ /de ltar 'jug pas rtag tu sangs rgyas sku rab
227a3(phal chen): 'di dag mthong / /mthong yang mig gi rnam shes tshul du rdul med mthong ba med/ /rnam shes sgyu ma gzhan pas mig stong stobs bcu mi mthong ngo / /'du shes thams cad rnam rtog yin gyi sangs rgyas
227a4(phal chen): mthong ba min/ /shin tu chags med yul med de ni rgyal ba mthong ba yin/ /sems can las mang bstsags pa de dag shin tu blta dka' ste/ /nang dang phyi dang dbyibs dang mdog tu phyogs bcu kun na med/ /
227a5(phal chen): de bzhin rang byung sku ni gzhal yas phyogs rnams kun 'gengs pa/ /shes par dka' ba 'dren pa sgrib pa med pas brnyes/ /namakha' dag la zhing rnams bye ba dngos por gnas par snang / /de nas
227a6(phal chen): 'ong ba med cing phyogs bcu kun tu 'gro ba med/ /tshig cing gnas par 'gyur yang de dag ci la'ang gnas pa med/ /de bzhin rang byung rnams kyi sku ni mkha' dbyings rtag tu 'gengs/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i

227a8(phal chen): dpal gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas dpal la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag rang bzhin gcig pa'i sems la bye brag tha dad pa'i rnam pa 'di lta bu dag 'di lta ste/
227b1(phal chen): bde 'gror 'gro ba dang / ngan song du 'gro ba dang / dbang po tshang ba dang / dbang po ma tshang ba dang / skye ba 'thun pa dang skye ba mi 'thun pa dang / sdug pa dang mi sdug pa dang bde ba myong ba dang sdug bsngal myong ba
227b2(phal chen): snang ba dag la ltos/ lus kyis ni sems mi shes so/ /sems kyis ni lus mi sheso/ /tshor bas ni rnam par smyin pa mi sheso/ /rnam par smin pas ni tshor ba mi sheso/ /sems kyis ni tshor ba mi sheso/ /
227b3(phal chen): tshor bas ni sems mi sheso/ /rgyus ni rkyen mi shes so rkyen kyis ni rgyu mi sheso/ /dngos pos ni dmigs pa mi sheso dmigs pas ni dngos po mi shes so/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas dpal gyis

227b8(phal chen): gnas gyur kyang / /gcig gis gcig ni mi shes te/ /chos kyi chos nyid de bzhin no/ /mig dang rna ba sna dag dang / /lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnams/ /de dag lam ni rgyu 'khor kyang / /byed pa po ni gang yang med/ /
228a1(phal chen): 'byung ba'i rang bzhin med pa yis/ /'byung ba nye bar bstan byas kyang / /bstan par byas pa gang yang med/ /bstan pa la ni dngos po med/ /mig ni rang bzhin nyid kyi stong / /rna ba sna yang rang

228a3(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab po/ /yang dag pa dang yang dag min/ /bden nam 'on te rdzun yang rung / /'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten kun/ /tshig gi las kyis brjod pa yi/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa'
228a4(phal chen): 'jam dpal gyis byang chub sems dpa' nor dpal la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sems can thams cad med mod kyi/ 'on kyang de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can 'dul
228a5(phal chen): ba'i dus la ji ltar 'bab pa dang / sems can gyi tshe ji lta ba dang lus ci lta ba dang spyod pa ji lta ba dang / mos pa ji lta ba dang mtshan ma ji lta ba dang bsam pa ji lta ba dang sbyor ba ji lta ba dang sems
228a6(phal chen): ji lta ba dang spyod pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can 'dul ba'i phyir mthong ngo / /de nas byang chub sems dpa' nor dpal gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal la tshigasu bcad de smras pa/
228a7(phal chen): gang rnams rab tu zhi spyod pa/ thos dang ldan pa'i sa 'di yin/ /'di don ji 'dra de bzhin du/ /'jam dpal bdag las mnyan par gyis/ /bdag gi lus la su gnas zhes/ /gang gi nang ni rab
228a8(phal chen): shes pa/ /yang dag yod dam med pa'i don/ /des ni rab tu shes pa yin/ /lus kyi rnam par dgod pa ni/ /phyogs ni mi gnas brjod pa yin/ /de bas shes pa de gnas la/ /nam yang chags par
228b1(phal chen): mi byed do/ /lus ni rnam par spyad pa yis/ /dngos po kun kyang rnam par bsgoms/ /sems ni phyir ldog mi 'gyur te/ /dngos po kun gyis brtags pa'o/ /gang gi tshe ni rjesu 'brang / /gang gi tshe ni phyir ldog

228b7(phal chen): ba'i tshor ba dag kyang snang / sdug bsngal kyi tshor ba dag kyang snang / yid du 'ong bar byed pa dang / yid du mi 'ong bar byed pa dang / nang du byed pa dang phyi rol du byed pa dang / tshor ba chung ba dang /

271b8(phal chen): rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /kye ma sangs rgyas dpal chen rnams/ /de bzhin gshegs pa tshad med do/ /rnam grol thugs ni sdigs mi mnga'/ /
